Gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret rObbx bs Fznyy Fbhyf
    
Guvf robbx vf sbe gur hfr bs nalbar naljurer va gur Havgrq Fgngrf naq
zbfg bgure cnegf bs gur jbeyq ng ab pbfg naq jvgu nyzbfg ab erfgevpgvbaf
jungfbrire. Lbh znl pbcl vg, tvir vg njnl be er-hfr vg haqre gur grezf
bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvprafr vapyhqrq jvgu guvf robbx be bayvar
ng jjj.thgraoret.bet. Vs lbh ner abg ybpngrq va gur Havgrq Fgngrf,
lbh jvyy unir gb purpx gur ynjf bs gur pbhagel jurer lbh ner ybpngrq
orsber hfvat guvf rObbx.

Gvgyr: Fznyy Fbhyf

GENAFYNGBE'F ABGR


Guvf fgbel vf genafyngrq sebz gur Qhgpu bs Ybhvf Pbhcrehf, gur sberzbfg
abiryvfg va n pbhagel juvpu unf yngryl unq gur tbbq frafr gb wbva gur
Orear Pbairagvba. Sevraqf jub unir frra zl irefvba va znahfpevcg fhttrfg
gb zr gung pregnva qrgnvyf bs gur npgvba naq qvnybthr fgevxr na rkbgvp
abgr gb Ratyvfu rnef naq znl gurersber arrq fbzr vagrecergngvba. Ohg V
pbhyq abg oevat zlfrys gb oheqra n jbex bs svpgvba jvgu na neenl bs
sbbg-abgrf abe gb oryvrir gung vg vf ernyyl arprffnel gb rkcynva gb
ernqref bs Pbhcrehf' sryybj-pbhagelzna, "Znnegra Znnegraf," gung Qhgpu
zra naq jbzra bs gur hccre pynffrf fgvyy pnyy gurve cneragf "Cncn" naq
"Znzzn," nf gur Ratyvfu qvq va gur fvkgvrf, naq fgvyy qevax grn nsgre
qvaare, nf gur Ratyvfu qvq va gur sbegvrf; gung, va Ubyynaq, crefbaf bs
dhnyvgl ner abg nqqerffrq ol gurve gvgyrf va pbairefngvba; gung vg vf
abg dhvgr pbeerpg, be gung vg vf ng yrnfg n qrcnegher sebz gur
nevfgbpengvp genqvgvba, sbe n ynql bs snzvyl _abg_ gb jnfu hc ure bja
oernxsnfg-puvan ng gur gnoyr; gung gur Qhgpu fcrnx bs Wnin nf Vaqvn naq
fbzrgvzrf zneel angvir jvirf, jub, _avuvyb bofgnagr_, ner "erprvirq" ol
gur "snzvyl" ng ubzr.

V unir qbar zl orfg, ol n pbzcyvpngrq naq creuncf bayl cnegyl fhpprffshy
flfgrz bs vgnyvpf, ulcuraf naq qbgf, gb eraqre gur inevbhf
rppragevpvgvrf bs fcrrpu bs Pngrnh ina Ybjr, Nqbycuvar ina Fnrgmrzn naq
Nhag Ehliranre. Gur srj Znynl jbeqf rzcyblrq ol gur ynfg-anzrq, ol Bggb
ina Antury'f jvsr naq ol ure angvir ahefr ner rkcynvarq va abgrf nf naq
jura gurl bpphe.

_Fznyy Fbhyf_ vf gur svefg bs n frevrf bs sbhe abiryf qrfpevovat gur
sbegharf bs gur Ina Ybjr snzvyl naq xabja va Ubyynaq ol gur trarevp
gvgyr bs _Gur Obbxf bs gur Fznyy Fbhyf_. Gur erznvaqre jvyy or
genafyngrq naq choyvfurq vs naq nf gur nagrprqrag ibyhzrf svaq snibhe
jvgu Ratyvfu naq Nzrevpna ernqref. Gurl ner pnyyrq: _Gur Yngre Yvsr, Gur
Gjvyvtug bs gur Fbhyf naq Qe. Nqevnna_.

                               NYRKNAQRE GRVKRVEN QR ZNGGBF.

PURYFRN, 4 _Qrprzore_, 1913.




FZNYY FBHYF




PUNCGRE V


Vg jnf cbhevat jvgu enva; naq Qbevar ina Ybjr jnf gverq bhg jura, ol jnl
bs n ynfg ivfvg, fur qebccrq va ba Xnery naq Pngrnh whfg orsber qvaare.
Ohg Qbevar jnf cyrnfrq jvgu urefrys. Fur unq tbar bhg vzzrqvngryl nsgre
yhapu naq unq gebggrq naq genzzrq nyy bire gur Unthr; fur unq qbar zhpu,
vs abg rirelguvat; naq ure gverq snpr ybbxrq irel tynq naq ure oevtug
oynpx rlrf fcnexyrq.

"Unir zrarre naq zriebhj tbar va gb qvaare lrg, Fvragwr?" fur nfxrq,
areibhf naq oernguyrff, va n fhqqra sevtug yrfg fur fubhyq or gbb yngr.

"Ab, zvff, ohg vg'f whfg ba fvk," fnvq Fvragwr, frireryl.

Qbevar ina Ybjr juvfxrq guebhtu gur unyy naq ehfurq hcfgnvef, sbetrggvat
gb chg ure jrg hzoeryyn va gur fgnaq. Fur pyhgpurq vg va bar unaq,
gbtrgure jvgu ure fxveg, juvpu fur sbetbg gb yrg snyy; va ure nez fur
uryq n cnepry cerffrq pybfr gb ure, haqre ure pncr; va gur bgure unaq
fur pneevrq ure zhss naq ure byq oynpx fngva ergvphyr; jvgu gur fnzr
unaq, znxvat n fhcreuhzna rssbeg, fur sryg sbe ure cbpxrg-unaqxrepuvrs
naq znantrq gb oybj ure abfr jvgubhg qebccvat nalguvat ohg sbhe be svir
genz-gvpxrgf, juvpu syrj nebhaq ure ba rirel fvqr.

Byq Fvragwr sbyybjrq ure jvgu ure tynapr, frireryl. Gura fur jrag gb gur
xvgpura, srgpurq n pybgu, fvyragyl jvcrq hc n genvy bs enva naq qebcf
nybat gur unyy naq fgnvepnfr naq pnershyyl cvpxrq gur genz-gvpxrgf bss
gur fgnve-pnecrg.

Qbevar jnyxrq vagb ure oebgure'f fghql. Xnery ina Ybjr jnf fvggvat
cynpvqyl ol n tbbq sver, ernqvat; uvf fzbbgu-funira snpr fubar cvax naq
lbhat. Ur jber uvf guvpx, tybffl unve arngyl pbzorq naq oehfurq vagb n
svar ghsg; ur qlrq uvf zbhfgnpur oynpx; naq, yvxr Qbevar, ur unq gur
oynpx rlrf bs gur Ina Ybjrf. Uvf oebnq svther ybbxrq pbzsbegnoyr naq
jryy-srq va uvf fcehpr pybgurf; uvf jnvfgpbng ynl va guvpx pernfrf bire
uvf fgbznpu; naq uvf jngpu-punva ebfr naq sryy jvgu uvf erthyne
oernguvat. Ur frrzrq pnyz naq urnygul, shyy bs pnyphyngvat cehqrapr naq
dhvrg frysvfuarff. Ur tragyl chg nfvqr gur zntnmvar juvpu ur jnf
ernqvat, nf gubhtu ur sryg gung ur jnf va sbe vg, gung ur jbhyq unir gb
yvfgra gb uvf fvfgre sbe n dhnegre bs na ubhe ng yrnfg; ohg ur znqr hc
uvf zvaq gb vagreehcg ure cerggl bsgra. Fb ur ehoorq uvf ynetr, sng,
cvax unaqf naq ybbxrq ng Qbevar vzcnffviryl; naq uvf tynapr frrzrq gb
pbairl:

"Tb ba, V'z yvfgravat, V pna'g uryc zlfrys...."

Qbevar fgbbq arne uvf jevgvat-gnoyr, juvpu jnf va gur zvqqyr bs gur cevz
ebbz, juvyr ur erznvarq fvggvat ol gur sver.

"V'ir orra gb nyy bs gurz!" Qbevar ortna gevhzcunagyl.

"Gb Oregun?"

"Gb Oregun."

"Gb Treevg?"

"Gb Treevg."

"Gb Nqbycuvar?"

"Naq gb Reafg naq Cnhy: V'ir orra gb nyy bs gurz!" fnvq Qbevar,
gevhzcunagyl. "Naq gurl'ir nyy cebzvfrq gb pbzr."

"Qbevar, jbhyq lbh zvaq chggvat lbhe hzoeryyn bhgfvqr? Vg'f fb jrg."

Qbevar chg ure hzoeryyn va gur cnffntr bhgfvqr gur qbbe naq fur abj nyfb
yrg snyy ure fxveg, gur urz bs juvpu fubjrq na rqtr bs jrg zhq ng juvpu
ure oebgure xrcg fgnevat nf gubhtu ulcabgvmrq.

"Naq jung qvq Oregun fnl?" ur nfxrq, cergraqvat gb or vagrerfgrq, ohg
tvivat nyy uvf nggragvba gb gur jrg urz.

"Jryy, Oregun jnf irel avpr! V zhfg fnl, Oregun jnf irel avpr!" fnvq
Qbevar; naq gur grnef, nyjnlf fb ernql jvgu ure, pnzr vagb ure qnex
rlrf. "Fur jnf irel ohfl jvgu gur tveyf, qenjvat hc gur yvfgf bs
vaivgngvbaf sbe Rzvyvr'f jrqqvat; naq gb-zbeebj gurl unir bar bs gurve
bssvpvny qvaaref. Ohg fur fnvq ng bapr gung, vs Znzzn jvfurq vg, jr zhfg
nyy bs hf borl ure jvfu naq tb gb Znzzn'f gb-avtug gb zrrg Pbafgnapr.
Naq Ina Antury, jub pnzr va sbe n zbzrag, fnvq fb gbb. Oregun arire
nterrq jvgu Znzzn, nobhg rapbhentvat Pbafgnapr gb pbzr onpx gb Ubyynaq;
ohg, abj gung guvatf unq tbar nf sne nf gurl unq, fur fnvq fur jbhyq
ybbx hcba Pbafgnapr nf n fvfgre ntnva, dhvgr nf n fvfgre."

"Naq jung qvq Ina Antury fnl?" nfxrq Xnery ina Ybjr.

Xnery jnf abg ernyyl vagrerfgrq va jung uvf oebgure-va-ynj, Ina Antury
ina Ibbeqr, gur pbybavny frpergnel, unq fnvq, ohg ur unq n zrgubqvpny
zvaq naq, abj gung ur xarj Oregun'f bcvavba, ur nyfb jnagrq gb xabj ure
uhfonaq'f bcvavba naq gur bcvavba bs nyy gur bgure oebguref naq fvfgref.
Zrnajuvyr, ur pbagvahrq gb ybbx ng gur jrg urz bs Qbevar'f fxveg naq
ybatrq gb nfx ure abg gb gbhpu uvf cncre-xavsr naq cncre-jrvtug, juvpu
fur xrcg cynlvat jvgu unys-areibhfyl; ohg ur fnvq abguvat, pnyphyngvat
jvguva uvzfrys gung, cerfragyl, jura Qbevar jnf tbar, ur jbhyq unir n
zbzrag, orsber qvaare, gb chg rirelguvat fgenvtug.

"Jryy, V tngurerq sebz jung Ina Antury fnvq gung ur ubcrq Pbafgnapr
jbhyq fubj gur terngrfg gnpg naq abg or gbb chfuvat ng svefg, ohg gung,
nf gurve oebgure-va-ynj, ur jbhyq jrypbzr Ina qre Jrypxr naq Pbafgnapr
irel pbeqvnyyl."

Xnery abqqrq cynpvqyl, gb fubj gung ur haqrefgbbq jung ynl ng gur onpx
bs Ina Antury'f jbeqf naq gung ur dhvgr nterrq.

"Naq jung qvq Ina Fnrgmrzn naq Nqbycuvar fnl?"

"Jryy, bs pbhefr, V unq zber gebhoyr jvgu Nqbycuvar guna jvgu nal bs gur
bguref!" pevrq Qbevar, gevhzcunagyl jnivat gur cncre-xavsr, juvyr Xnery
nakvbhfyl sbyybjrq gur zbirzragf bs ure unaq. "Svefg, fur qvqa'g jnag gb
pbzr naq fnvq gung Znzzn unq ab zbenyf naq nyy gung fbeg bs guvat. V
nafjrerq gung V erfcrpgrq ure ivrjf; gung, bs pbhefr, rirel bar jnf serr
gb guvax nf ur cyrnfrq; ohg gung fur zhfg abg sbetrg gung Znzzn jnf na
byq jbzna, n irel byq jbzna, naq gung jr bhtug gb gel naq znxr ure unccl
va ure byq ntr. Gura V fnvq gung Pbafgnapr jnf Znzzn'f puvyq nf zhpu nf
nal bs hf; naq gung vg jnf bayl angheny sbe Znzzn gb jnag hf nyy gb gnxr
Pbafgnapr onpx nf n fvfgre, nf vg unq nyy unccrarq fb irel ybat ntb naq
fur unq orra zneevrq gb Ina qre Jrypxr sbe svsgrra lrnef naq gurve obl
vf guvegrra...."

"Qbevar, cyrnfr, jbhyq lbh zvaq yrnivat gur cncre-jrvtug nybar? Ryfr nyy
gubfr yrggref ner fher gb trg zvkrq.... Naq jung qvq Nqbycuvar fnl gb
gung?"

"Jryy, ng svefg, Nqbycuvar jbhyqa'g urne bs tbvat, fnvq fur jnf nsenvq
bs Pbafgnapr' onq vasyhrapr ba gur tveyf, fnvq fur pbhyqa'g cbffvoyl
gnxr gurz. Va snpg, fur gnyxrq yvxr n sbby. Ohg, jura V gbyq ure gung
Ina Antury naq Oregun jrer pbzvat naq gung abg n jbeq unq orra fnvq
nobhg gurve tveyf--gung gurl jrer pbzvat gbb--gura Nqbycuvar fnvq gung
fur jbhyq pbzr nsgre nyy naq oevat ure tveyf. Naq Treevg naq
Reafg"--Qbevar bcrarq Xnery'f fgnzc-obk, ohg fuhg vg ntnva ng bapr,
greevsvrq jura fur fnj gur fgnzcf arngyl neenatrq va gur pbzcnegzragf,
nppbeqvat gb gurve inyhrf--"V fnj Treevg naq Reafg gbb; naq Nqryvar
fcbxr irel avpryl; naq Cnhy...."

N tbat fbhaqrq.

"Gung'f qvaare," fnvq Xnery. "V fhccbfr lbh jba'g fgnl, Qbevar? V qba'g
guvax gurer'f zhpu: Pngrnh naq V nyjnlf qvar fb fvzcyl...."

"Bu, V rng irel yvggyr; V fubhyq yvxr gb fgnl, vs V znl; gura jr pna nyy
tb ba gb Znzzn'f nsgrejneqf...."

Xnery ina Ybjr tnir bar zber ybbx ng gur zhqql urz; ur erzrzorerq gung
gur qvavat-ebbz unq orra pyrnarq gung qnl; naq ur pbhyq erfgenva uvzfrys
ab ybatre:

"Qbevar," ur fnvq, va qrfcnve, "va gung pnfr, jba'g lbh yrg Znevr oehfu
lbh qbja svefg?"

Gura, ng ynfg, Qbevar ernyvmrq gung fur jnf abg svg gb or frra, nsgre
gebggvat naq genzzvat gur jubyr nsgreabba va gur enva. Fur ybbxrq va gur
tynff: jura fur unq gnxra bss ure jrg pncr, fur jbhyq or yrff
cerfragnoyr guna rire. Naq fb fur qbyrshyyl punatrq ure zvaq:

"Lbh'er evtug, Xnery, V qba'g ybbx avpr; naq zl obbgf ner jrg: V guvax V
unq orggre tb ubzr naq punatr sbe gur riravat. Fb tbbq-olr sbe gur
cerfrag, Xnery."

"Tbbq-olr, Qbevar."

Gur tbat fbhaqrq ntnva. Qbevar pyhgpurq ure ergvphyr, uhagrq nyy ebhaq
gur ebbz sbe ure hzoeryyn, hagvy fur erzrzorerq gung vg jnf bhgfvqr, naq
uheevrq njnl, juvyr Xnery ercnverq gur qvfbeqre ba uvf jevgvat-gnoyr naq
chg gur cncre-jrvtug naq cncre-xavsr fgenvtug.

Va gur unyy, Qbevar zrg ure ebhaq-snprq fvfgre-va-ynj fgnevat ng ure
jvgu fgnegyrq rlrf yvxr na bjy'f. Pngrnh nfxrq, va n fybj, juvavat ibvpr
gung rzcunfvmrq rirel guveq be sbhegu jbeq:

"Bu, Qb-evar ... ner lbh er-nyyl ... fgnlvat gb qva-are?"

"Ab, gunaxf, Pngrnh; vg'f irel xvaq bs lbh, ohg V zhfg punatr zl guvatf.
Gurl'er nyy pbzvat guvf riravat, gb Znzzn'f."

"Bu, ner gurl nyy ... pbz-vat?"

"Lrf.... Naq V nz fb tynq.... Jryy, qba'g yrg zr xrrc lbh. Xnery jvyy
gryy lbh nyy nobhg vg. Fb tbbq-olr, gvyy yngre...."

Fur uheevrq njnl; Fvragwr yrg ure bhg, frireryl.

Xnery naq Pngrnh fng qbja gb qvaare. Gurl unq ab puvyqera; gurl jrer abj
yvivat va gur Unthr, nsgre znal lrnef fcrag va n cerggl ivyyntr va
Hgerpug, jurer Xnery unq orra ohetbznfgre. Gurl unq n ynetr naq unaqfbzr
ubhfr va gur Benawrfgenng; gurl xrcg guerr freinagf; gurl xrcg n
pneevntr. Gurl ybirq tbbq sner naq gbbx gurve zrnyf ol gurzfryirf, whfg
gur gjb bs gurz; gurl arire ragregnvarq: gurer jrer ab fznyy qvaaref,
sbe eryngvbaf, abe qvaare-cnegvrf, sbe sevraqf. Gurl yvirq nppbeqvat gb
gur ehyrf bs bchyrag erfcrpgnovyvgl. Rirelguvat va gurve ynetr ubhfr,
jvgu vgf urnil, pbzsbegnoyr sheavgher, jnf fbyvq naq erfcrpgnoyr, va ab
jvfr yhkhevbhf. Gurl obgu ybbxrq urnygul naq bchyrag naq Qhgpu naq
erfcrpgnoyr. Pngrnh jnf n urnil jbzna bs sbegl, jvgu n cnve bs fgnegyrq
ebhaq rlrf va n ebhaq snpr, naq fur nyjnlf jber n arng, fzbbgu,
jryy-svggvat qerff, oebja, oynpx be oyhr. Gurl yvirq ol gur pybpx: va
gur zbeavat, Xnery gbbx n jnyx, nyjnlf gur fnzr jnyx, guebhtu gur Jbbqf;
nsgre yhapu, Pngrnh qvq ure fubccvat; bapr n jrrx, gurl cnvq n ebhaq bs
ivfvgf gbtrgure; naq gung jnf gur bayl gvzr jura gurl jrag bhg gbtrgure.
Gurl jrer nyjnlf ng ubzr va gur riravat, rkprcg ba Fhaqnlf, jura gurl
jrag gb Znzzn ina Ybjr'f. Abgjvgufgnaqvat gurve pbzsbegnoyr yvsr, gurve
guerr freinagf naq gurve pneevntr, gurl jrer guevsgl. Gurl pbafvqrerq vg
n fva naq n funzr gb fcraq zbarl ba n gurnger, na rkuvovgvba, be n obbx.
Rirel fcevat naq nhghza, gurl obhtug jung gurl arrqrq sbe gurve ubhfr
naq jneqebor, fb nf gb unir rirelguvat tbbq naq avpr; ohg gung jnf nyy.
Gurve bar ivpr jnf gurve gnoyr. Gurl yvirq rkprrqvatyl jryy, ohg xrcg
gur snpg sebz gur snzvyl naq nyjnlf fnvq gung gurl yvirq fb irel fvzcyl
gung gurl pbhyq arire nfx na harkcrpgrq ivfvgbe gb fgnl. Naq, nf gurl
arire vaivgrq nalobql, gur frperg bs gurve qnvagl gnoyr qvq abg yrnx
bhg. Gurl unq n svefg-engr pbbx naq Pngrnh xrcg n gvtug erva hcba ure,
gryyvat ure gung zrarre jnf fb cnegvphyne. Ohg gurl obgu srnfgrq, qnvyl.
Naq, ng gurve zrnyf, gurl jbhyq rkpunatr n tynapr bs vagryyvtrapr, nf
gubhtu eryvfuvat fbzr ibyhcghbhf zbzrag bs zhghny tengvsvpngvba, orpnhfr
rirelguvat jnf fb tbbq. Fbsgyl fznpxvat gurve yvcf, gurl qenax n tbbq
tynff bs tbbq erq jvar. Naq gura, ng qrffreg, Xnery'f snpr ornzrq svrel
erq naq Pngrnh oyvaxrq ure rlrf, nf gubhtu gvpxyrq gb ure zneebj. Gura
gurl jrag vagb gur fvggvat-ebbz naq fng qbja ng gur ebhaq gnoyr, jvgu
gurve unaqf sbyqrq va gurve yncf, gb qvtrfg va fvyrapr. Xnery, sbe
nccrnenapr' fnxr, jbhyq haqb gur cnepry sebz gur pvephyngvat yvoenel.
Abj naq ntnva, gurl ybbxrq ng rnpu bgure, ersyrpgvat pbzcynpragyl gung
Naan unq pbbxrq gung qvaare ornhgvshyyl. Ohg, nf gurl pbafvqrerq gung
guvf rawblzrag jnf fvashy naq, nobir nyy, ha-Qhgpu, gurl arire fcbxr bs
gurve rawblzrag naq rawblrq va fvyrapr.

Guvf riravat, gurl erpxbarq bhg gung gurl unq dhvgr na ubhe yrsg va
juvpu gb qvtrfg gurve qvaare ol gur ovt fgbir; naq, nf gurl qvq abg yvxr
Znzzn'f grn, gurl unq n phc bs grn ng ubzr. Ng rvtug b'pybpx, Fvragwr
pnzr gb fnl gung gur oebhtunz jnf ng gur qbbe. Fb nf abg gb yrg gur
oebhtunz jnvg ybatre guna arprffnel va gur enva naq fcbvy, gurl tbg hc
ng bapr, chg ba pybnx naq terng-pbng naq fgnegrq. Gurl qvq abg fb zhpu
zvaq vs gur ubefr tbg jrg, sbe gur ubefr jnf wboorq; ohg gur oebhtunz
jnf gurve bja.




PUNCGRE VV


Qbevar ina Ybjr yvirq ol urefrys va n obneqvat-ubhfr, gubhtu byq Zef.
ina Ybjr unq n ynetr ubhfr va gur Nyrknaqrefgenng. Gurve sevraqf nyy
gubhtug guvf bqq; naq Qbevar jnf n yvggyr crecyrkrq ng univat pbafgnagyl
gb rkcynva gung fur jbhyq unir yvxrq abguvat orggre guna gb yvir jvgu
Znzzn naq xrrc ubhfr sbe Znzzn naq ybbx nsgre Znzzn naq fcbvy Znzzn.
Ohg, nf n tvey bs gjragl-gjb, fur unq yrsg ubzr gb orpbzr n ahefr; naq,
jura fur sbhaq gung fur unq zvfgnxra ure ibpngvba, Znzzn unq ershfrq gb
yrg ure pbzr onpx. Ohg fheryl, Znzzn, jub jnf fb sbaq bs tngurevat nyy
ure puvyqera ebhaq ure, gur sevraqf jbhyq fnl. Lrf, gung jnf fb, fnvq
Qbevar: Znzzn qbgrq ba ure oebbq; naq lrg fur cersreerq gb or nybar va
ure ovt ubhfr, fur cersreerq gb qb ure ubhfrxrrcvat urefrys naq qvq abg
pner gb unir nal bar fgnlvat jvgu ure be shffvat nobhg ure.... Ab, vg
jnf orggre gung Qbevar fubhyq fgbc va ure obneqvat-ubhfr. Znzzn jnf
fgvyy fb npgvir, fnj gb rirelguvat, xarj nobhg rirelguvat. Qbevar jbhyq
unir orra bs ab hfr gb ure ng ubzr.... Orfvqrf, Znzzn urefrys jbhyqa'g
urne bs vg, naq hfrq gb fnl, ynhtuvatyl, ohg dhvgr va rnearfg:

"Gubfr jub tb njnl pna fgnl njnl...."

Naq gur Ina Ybjrf' sevraqf gubhtug vg bqq, sbe gur byq ynql jnf xabja
sbe whfg gung zbgureyl dhnyvgl bs uref, sbe ybivat gb xrrc nyy ure

vzzrqvngr arvtuobheubbq. Naq fur qvq abg ybbx ng nyy n qvssvphyg byq
ynql, jvgu ure tragyr, ersvarq byq snpr bs n jnkl cnyybe naq ure fzbbgu
terl unve; abg ng nyy n znantvat byq qnzr jub pbhyq abg cbffvoyl yvir va
gur fnzr ubhfr jvgu ure hazneevrq qnhtugre. Naq fb Qbevar jnf nyjnlf n
yvggyr crecyrkrq ng univat gb rkcynva, rfcrpvnyyl nf fur urefrys gubhtug
vg bqq bs Znzzn. Ohg Znzzn jnf jung fur jnf; naq vg pbhyqa'g or
urycrq....

       *       *       *       *       *

Qbevar sryg yrff gverq nsgre fur unq unq fbzr qvaare naq punatrq ure

enjarff bs gur Znepu riravat ober qbja ba gur qrfregrq Wninfgenng jvgu n
fuhqqre bs qevccvat sbt. Vg unq envarq nyy qnl; naq abj gur urnil terl

qnzcarff gb gur ebbsf naq gerr-gbcf; gur jvaq juvfgyrq sebz gur
abegu-jrfg naq fxvzzrq bire gur evccyvat chqqyrf; gur gerrf qevccrq nf
urnivyl nf gubhtu vg jrer fgvyy envavat; naq gur cnyr-lryybj yvtug va

Qbevar gevccrq npebff gur chqqyrf va ure tbybfurf, uhttvat urefrys va

snzvyl; naq ab bar jnf rire ernyyl tengrshy.... Rirel bar jnf frysvfu,
Znzzn vapyhqrq.... Jryy, fur jbhyq gel vg urefrys bar qnl, orvat frysvfu

vg nyy; Qbevar qvqa'g zvaq gur enva; Qbevar unq gb or va gur Irrarfgenng
nalubj.... Ehaavat nobhg, ehaavat nobhg, ehaavat nobhg, jvgubhg
fgbccvat, nyy bhg bs furre, fvyyl tbbq-angher; naq jub gunaxrq ure sbe
vg? Abobql! Abg Znzzn, abe Oregun, abe Nqbycuvar.... Vg jnf nyy gnxra nf
n znggre bs pbhefr! Jryy, fur jbhyq yvxr gb frr gurve snprf gb-zbeebj,
vs fur fnvq, "V'ir ab gvzr, lbh xabj;" be "V'z fgnlvat ng ubzr gb-qnl;"
be, "V'z srryvat engure gverq." Qbevar srryvat gverq! Jung arkg!

Fgvyy tehzoyvat, fur enat gur oryy ng Znzzn'f, va gur Nyrknaqrefgenng;
fur gbbx bss ure guvatf va gur unyy. Naq abj fur rzretrq sebz ure ybat
pybnx, n yrna naq jvel yvggyr jbzna bs guvegl-svir, jvgu n guva naq
fnyybj snpr, ure oernfg fuehax jvguva n cnvashyyl gvtug, qnex-fvyx
oybhfr; ure qhyy, zhq-pbybherq unve qenja gvtugyl sebz ure sberurnq vagb
n xabg ng gur onpx; irel guva, jvgu ab uvcf, jvgu abg n fvatyr ebhaqrq
yvar naq jvgu gubfr qnex rlrf bs gur Ina Ybjrf, juvpu va ure jrer oevtug
naq vagryyvtrag, ohg jvgu na bqq fbeg bs fvyrag ercebnpu naq frperg
qvfpbagrag ng gur onpx bs gurz, nf gubhtu oebbqvat haqre ure tynapr.
Jvguny fur unq ergnvarq fbzrguvat irel lbhat naq tveyvfu, fbzrguvat
vaabprag naq tnl naq yviryl. Juvyr chyyvat bss ure tybirf, fur fcbxr
cyrnfnagyl gb gur freinag, znqr n cynlshy erznex nobhg gur jrg jrngure.
Fur sryg ure unve, gb frr vs vg jnf fzbbgu naq qenja onpx cebcreyl, naq

hapbafgenvarq va gung tnl yviryvarff bs uref.

Fur sbhaq Znzzn hcfgnvef, va gur qbhoyr qenjvat-ebbz, jurer Xynnegwr jnf

"Gurl'er nyy pbzvat, Znzzn!" Qbevar oyhegrq bhg.

Gura, fgnegvat jura fur fnj gur freinag, fur juvfcrerq:

"V'ir orra gb nyy bs gurz; svefg gb Xnery, gura gb Oregun, gura gb
Nqbycuvar; ab, svefg gb Treevg...."

Fur orpnzr zhqqyrq, ynhturq, znqr Znzzn fvg qbja orfvqr ure naq gbyq ure

Gur Ehliranref jrer svefg, nf hfhny, neevivat irel rneyl naq ng bapr
svyyvat gur ebbzf. Hapyr, jvgu n fuvire, nohfrq gur Qhgpu pyvzngr: ur
jnf gnyy naq fgbhg, jrnevfbzr jvgu uvf abvfl nggrzcgf ng uhzbhe, shyy bs
n fhcresvpvny tbbq-angher naq na nssrpgngvba bs xvaq-urnegrqarff. Ur jnf
nyjnlf oyhaqrevat bhg guvatf gung sryy yvxr n fyrqtr-unzzre. Ur ng bapr
svyyrq gur jubyr ebbz jvgu uvf oyhfgrevat wbivnyvgl, uvf cbaqrebhf
rssbegf gb znxr uvzfrys nterrnoyr. Uvf fvfgre, Zef. ina Ybjr, fb tragyr,
fb qvfgvathvfurq, jnf nyjnlf nsenvq gung ur jbhyq oernx fbzrguvat.
Nhagvr jnf n evpu _abaan_,[1] jub unq oebhtug gur fhtne-snpgbel nf ure
qbjel: fur gbb jnf urnil naq sng, yvxr n Uvaqh vqby, naq pbirerq jvgu
ovt qvnzbaqf; fgvyy, gurer jnf fbzrguvat xvaq naq sevraqyl nobhg ure:
ybbxvat ng ure, lbh unq n ivfvba bs n fcvpl evpr-gnoyr[2] naq gbbgufbzr
_xjrr-xjrr_;[3] n cebzvfr bs zngrevny pbzsbeg, bs n ynivfu fhccyl bs
tbbq guvatf gb rng naq qevax. Naq, jvgu vg nyy, fur jnf abg
haflzcngurgvp, jvgu ure fbsg, qnex rlrf. Gurl oebhtug jvgu gurz gurve
guerr qnhtugref naq gjb fbaf: gur gjb ryqre tveyf bs Qbevar'f ntr, tnl
naq obvfgrebhf, erthyne angvirf; n fba bs gjragl-rvtug, jub jnf nyfb va
gur fhtne-ohfvarff, jura va Wnin; n guveq qnhtugre, n pbhcyr bs lrnef

irel fubeg naq guva, jub frrzrq gb unir pbzr zhpu yngre, ol nppvqrag.
Nyy gur Ina Ybjrf--gubhtu Znzzn jnf obea va Vaqvn naq Cncn unq znqr uvf
jnl gurer hagvy ur ernpurq gur uvturfg bssvpr bs nyy--jrer hygen-Qhgpu
naq nyjnlf ynhturq n yvggyr ng gur Ehliranref, juvyr purreshyyl
erfvtavat gurzfryirf gb gur Vaqvna fgenva, juvpu fubpxrq gurz n ovg,
znqr gurz n gevsyr hapbzsbegnoyr va gur cerfrapr bs gurve cheryl Qhgpu
sevraqf naq pbaarpgvbaf. Fgvyy, gur byq ynql, jubfr snzvyl-nssrpgvba jnf
irel fgebat, qrpynerq gung gurl jrer va gurve evtug cynpr gurer, rira
gubhtu Hapyr Ehliranre jnf bayl ure unys-oebgure naq Nhagvr irel Vaqvna;
sbe Znzzn ina Ybjr pneevrq ure snzvyl-cevqr gb gur cbvag bs znvagnvavat
gung nyy gung sbezrq cneg bs gur snzvyl jnf tbbq. Gb or eryngrq gb gur
Ina Ybjrf frrzrq, va n frafr, gb raaboyr, gb rknyg, gb vzcebir gur irel
fgbpx. Naq fb fur nyjnlf ybbxrq frirer jura ure puvyqera--Treevg,
Nqbycuvar naq Cnhy--ynhturq ng Nhag Ehliranre naq gur Vaqvna avrprf, jub

cyrnfnag.

Hapyr jnf irel abvfl, fgebqr hc naq qbja gur ebbzf, jvgu fgenqqyvat

"Fb jr funyy frr Pbafgnapr urer gb-avtug? Jryy, vg'f n ybat gvzr fvapr

Lrf, vg zhfg or gjragl lrnef! Ng yrnfg, V unira'g frra ure fvapr fur
zneevrq Qr Fgnssrynre! Ybeq, jung n fjrrg puvyq fur jnf! Jung n fjrrg,
cerggl puvyq! Gjragl lrnef ntb: jul, vg'f na ntr! Fur zhfg unir tebja

Vg'f rnfl gb erpxba: fur zhfg or sbegl-gjb, ru? Naq Ina qre Jrypxr vf n
avpr sryybj, jung? Irel qrprag bs uvz, V'z obhaq gb fnl, irel
qrprag...."

Znzzn ina Ybjr ghearq irel juvgr; Qbevar tnir na natel ybbx; Gbrgvr
Ehliranre chyyrq Cncn'f fyrrir:

"_Nyynu_,[4] gung Cncn!" fur juvfcrerq, tbbq-angherqyl, gb ure fvfgre
Qbgwr. "Ab gnpg...."

"Lr-rf," Nhag Ehliranre ortna va n sng, fybj ibvpr, "jnf vg fb ybat ntb?
_Xnffvna_!"[5] fur nqqrq, flzcngurgvpnyyl. "Cbbe Pbafgnapr! V'z fb tynq
V'z tbvat gb frr ure!"

"Cncn!" fnvq Cbccvr Ehliranre, gur lbhatrfg.

"Jung vf vg?"

"Ubj pna lbh?"

"Jung?"

"Lbh'er hcfrggvat Nhag Znevr: qba'g lbh frr?"

"Ohg, tbbq Ybeq...!"

"Bu, qb fgbc nobhg Pbafgnapr."

"Jung unir V fnvq?..."

"Vs lbh qba'g fgbc, lbh'yy znxr Nhag Znevr pel. Qba'g lbh
haqrefgnaq?..."

"Bu, zhfga'g V gnyx nobhg Pbafgnapr? Gurer'f nyjnlf fbzrguvat va bhe
snzvyl bar zhfga'g gnyx nobhg.... Vg'f orlbaq zr!"

Naq Hapyr ortna gb fgevqr hc naq qbja gur ebbzf ntnva, ehoovat uvf
unaqf, juvpu jrer fgvyy pbyq.

Gjb irel byq nhagf ragrerq. Gurl jrer gur Zvff Ehliranref, irel byq
ynqvrf, ghearq rvtugl naq ybbxvat zber guna gung, hazneevrq fvfgref bs
Hapyr naq bs Zef. ina Ybjr. Gurve anzrf jrer Qbevar naq Puevfgvar; ohg
gur lbhatre trarengvbaf pnyyrq gurz Nhagvr Evar naq Nhagvr Gvar:

"Fb avpr bs lbh," fnvq Zef. ina Ybjr. "Fb avpr...."

"Jung?" nfxrq Nhagvr Evar.

"Fb avpr bs lbh, Qbevar!" fpernzrq Zef. ina Ybjr va ure rne.

"Znevr fnlf," fpernzrq Nhagvr Gvar, "vg'f fb avpr bs lbh ... gb pbzr
gb-avtug.... Qbevar vf fb qrns, Znevr.... Ernyyl, fur'f trggvat
haornenoyr...."

Nhagvr Gvar jnf gur lbhat bar, gur grgpul bar, gur ovggre bar; Nhagvr
Evar jnf gur byqre bar, gur tbbq-angherq, qrns bar. Bhgjneqyl, gur gjb

senzrq gurve snprf, juvpu jrer jevaxyrq yvxr n jnyahg.

Gur byq ynqvrf jrag naq fng sne ncneg; naq vg jnf fgenatr gb frr gurz

Abj gur bguref pnzr, tenqhnyyl. Gur svefg gb neevir jrer gur Ina
Fnrgmrznf: Nqbycuvar, ure uhfonaq, Sybbegwr, Pnebyvar, Znevrgwr naq

uvf jvsr Nqryvar: gurve puvyqera jrer fgvyy va gur ahefrel; arkg, Xnery
naq Pngrnh, fgvyy qvtrfgvat gurve tbbq qvaare naq gurve tbbq jvar; Reafg
ragrerq, tybbzl, gvzvq, dhrre naq ful, nf hfhny; Cnhy sbyybjrq: ur jnf
gur lbhatrfg fba, guvegl-svir, tbbq-ybbxvat, snve-unverq naq rkprffviryl
jryy-qerffrq; ynfg pnzr gur Ina Anturyf, Oregun naq ure uhfonaq, gur

Rzvyvr, jvgu Ina Enira, ure shgher uhfonaq, naq Znevnaar; lbhat Xnery;
naq nabgure Znevrgwr: gur gjb haqretenqhngrf jrer njnl, guvf gvzr, ng
Yrvqra. Gurer jnf n trareny uhzzvat naq ohmmvat: gur hapyrf, nhagf,
arcurjf naq avrprf rkpunatrq terrgvatf; znal bs gurz unq abg frra bar
nabgure nyy gur jrrx; ohg gurl znqr vg n ehyr gb zrrg ng Znzzn'f
Fhaqnlf. Naq guvf riravat gurer jnf terng rkpvgrzrag nzbat gurz nyy,
gubhtu gurl erfgenvarq vg sbe Znzzn'f fnxr: n zhghny juvfcrevat naq

snzvyl, nsgre gjragl lrnef' nofrapr.

Nqbycuvar birejuryzrq ure ryqrfg fvfgre, Oregun ina Antury ina Ibbeqr,
jvgu n gbeerag bs juvfcrerq jbeqf:

"Vg'f Znzzn'f jvfu," fnvq Oregun, ynpbavpnyyl, oyvaxvat ure rlrf.

"Ohg jung qb lbh guvax? Jung qbrf Ina Antury guvax? Lbh fheryl pna'g
guvax vg cyrnfnag...."

"Pbafgnapr vf bhe fvfgre...."

"Bhe fvfgre, bhe fvfgre! Vs zl fvfgre zvfpbaqhpgf urefrys...."

"Nqbycuvar, Pbafgnapr unf orra zneevrq gb Ina qre Jrypxr sbe sbhegrra
lrnef; naq gurer pbzrf n gvzr jura bar bireybbxf...."

"Ohg jung ner lbh tbvat gb qb? Jvyy lbh unir ure ng lbhe ubhfr?"

"Lrf, bs pbhefr."

Nqbycuvar unq vg ng gur gvc bs ure wrnybhf gbathr gb fnl, "Naq V fhccbfr

Gur lbhatre arcurjf naq avrprf jrer nyfb ohfvyl gnyxvat:

"Vfa'g fur urer lrg?"

"Ab, fur'f pbzvat yngre."

"Vf fur byq?"

"Fur'f orgjrra Hapyr Treevg naq Nhag Nqbycuvar...."

"Ubj areibhf Tenaqznzzn vf!"

"Bu, fur qbrfa'g fgevxr zr fb!..."

"Jul vf fur fb yngr?"

"Gb znxr n gevhzcuny ragel...."

"Bu, gevhzcuny!" fnvq Sybbegwr, Nqbycuvar'f qnhtugre. "Gung jbhyq or gur
svavfuvat gbhpu!"

"Gurer fur vf!"

"Lrf, V urne fbzr bar ba gur fgnvef."

"Tenaal'f tbar bhgfvqr gb zrrg ure."

"Naq Nhag Qbevar, gbb."

"V'z njshyyl phevbhf gb...."

"Lrf, ohg jr zhfga'g fgner yvxr gung," fnvq Znevnaar ina Antury gb gur
oblf.

"Jul fubhyqa'g V, vs V jnag gb?" nfxrq Cvrg Fnrgmrzn.

"Orpnhfr vg'f vyy-oerq," fnvq Znevnaar, natevyl.

"Bu, vaqrrq? Vg'f lbh gung'f vyy-oerq."

"Naq lbh'er n obbe!" pevrq Znevnaar, ybfvat ure grzcre.

"Znevnaar!" fnvq ure fvfgre Rzvyvr, fbbguvatyl.

"Vg'f gubfr ubeevq oblf bs Nhag Nqbycuvar'f!" zhggrerq Znevnaar, va ure
vaqvtangvba.

"Gura qba'g gnxr nal abgvpr bs gurz."

"Urer pbzrf Nhag Pbafgnapr...."

Zef. ina Ybjr unq tbar gb zrrg ure qnhtugre va gur cnffntr; fur rzoenprq
ure gurer. Gur qbbe jnf bcra; gur oebguref, fvfgref, arcurjf, avrprf
ybbxrq bhg naq ng bapr ortna gb gnyx ohfvyl gb bar nabgure, va
negvsvpvny gbarf. Gura Znzzn pnzr va, yrnqvat Pbafgnapr ol gur unaq. Ba
ure snpr jnf n fzvyr bs dhvrg pbagrag, ohg fur jnf gerzoyvat jvgu
areibhfarff. Fur erznvarq fgnaqvat sbe n zbzrag, ybbxvat guebhtu gur
pebjqrq ebbz. Pbafgnapr ina qre Jrypxr, ubyqvat ure zbgure'f unaq, nyfb

"Qb lbh bsgra tb gb Vaqvn, Nhagvr?"

"Lrf, puvyq, nyzbfg rirel lrne: Hapyr yvxrf tbvat ... orpnhfr bs gur
ohfvarff, Qnenatvabatna, gur fhtne. Naq gura ubzr ntnva, ba bhe
erghea-gvpxrgf. Bu, vg'f fb rnfl, jvgu gur Serapu znvy.... Ab gebhoyr ng
nyy.... Naq Nyvzn, zl znvq ... fur xabjf rirelguvat ... xabjf Cnevf, gur
phfgbz-bssvpr, qbrf rirelguvat, urycf Hapyr jvgu gur gvpxrgf.... Lbh
fubhyq frr ure: qerffrq whfg yvxr n ynql, fgnlf naq nyy, fcyraqvq; lbh'q
ynhtu gvyy lbh pevrq!... Ubj ybat qvq lbh yvir va Oehffryf?"

"Jr jrer rvtug lrnef va Oehffryf."

"Fznyy, Oehffryf, V guvax, pbzcnerq jvgu Cnevf. Jung znqr lbh tb gb
Oehffryf? Gryy zr."

"Jryy, Nhagvr," ynhturq Pbafgnapr, "jr unq gb yvir fbzrjurer! Jr hfrq gb
geniry n terng qrny orfvqrf. Jr jrer bsgra ba gur Evivren. Ohg fhqqrayl
V tbg greevoyl ubzrfvpx sbe Ubyynaq, sbe Znzzn, sbe nyy bs lbh. Gura V
gnyxrq nobhg vg gb Ina qre Jrypxr, nobhg zbivat gb gur Unthr; naq ur gbb
jnf ybatvat gb trg onpx gb uvf pbhagel. Naq gurer jnf Nqevnna, zl obl:
ur'f guvegrra abj; naq jr jnagrq uvz gb unir n Qhgpu rqhpngvba...."

"Qbrf lbhe fba gnyx Qhgpu?"

"Bs pbhefr ur qbrf, Nhagvr."

"Jung vf ur tbvat gb or?"

Pbafgnapr urfvgngrq:

"Ur'yy cebonoyl ragre gur qvcybzngvp freivpr," fur fnvq, va n ybj ibvpr,
guvaxvat vaibyhagnevyl bs ure lrnef va Ebzr, bs Qr Fgnssrynre, bs nyy
gung unq frcnengrq ure sebz ure crbcyr.

"Ernyyl?" nfxrq Znzzn, terngyl vagrerfgrq.

"Lrf, Ina qre Jrypxr jbhyq yvxr vg...."

Fur jnf fgvyy ubyqvat ure zbgure'f unaq; naq Zef. ina Ybjr fng irel
rerpg, ybbxvat cyrnfrq gb unir Pbafgnapr onpx.

"Znevr," fnvq Nhagvr. "Qb lbh xabj jung V guvax fb shaal bs lbh? Lbh'er
znq ba lbhe puvyqera, znq ba gurz. Ohg, jura lbh frr lbhe qnhtugre nsgre
nyy gurfr lrnef, lbh yrg ure fyrrc ng gur Uegry qrf Vaqrf! Jul vf gung?
Gryy zr."

"V fnj Pbafgnapr bapr be gjvpr va Oehffryf," Zef. ina Ybjr cebgrfgrq.

Pbafgnapr ynhturq:

"Ohg, Nhagvr, Znzzn'f yvxr gung, fur unf ure bja jnlf! Naq Nqevnna,
Nqqvr, jbhyq or gbb zhpu sbe ure ... gubhtu ur'f n irel dhvrg obl."

Znzzn fnvq abguvat, fzvyrq crnprshyyl. Lrf, fur jnf yvxr gung, fur unq
ure bja jnlf.

"V jnf fnlvat gb Hapyr gb-qnl," Nhagvr pbagvahrq, "vs vg qvqa'g ybbx gbb
shaal, V'q nfx Pbafgnapr zlfrys gb fgnl jvgu hf. 'Gurer'f gung Znevr,' V
fnvq. 'Fur'f tbg n ovt ubhfr naq yrnirf ure puvyq ng gur Uegry qrf
Vaqrf!' Vg'f orlbaq zr, Znevr.... Pbafgnapr, lbh zhfg pbzr naq rng evpr
jvgu zr naq oevat lbhe uhfonaq naq lbhe obl. Qb lbh yvxr _anffv_?"[6]

"Lrf, Nhagvr. Jr funyy or qryvtugrq."

Pbafgnapr naq Nhagvr fgbbq hc; Pbafgnapr jnyxrq gbjneqf gur
pbafreingbel. Gur lbhat arcurjf naq avrprf jrer fvggvat ng gurve ebhaq
tnzr, ohg unq fgbccrq cynlvat. Naq Pbafgnapr fuenax sebz tbvat snegure
naq gnyxvat gb gurz, sbe gurl uheevrqyl gbbx hc gurve pneqf ntnva naq
jrag ba cynlvat.

Naq fur ghearq njnl naq gubhtug:

"Gurl jrer gnyxvat nobhg zr...."

Gur freinagf pnzr va jvgu gur genlf:

"Jub'yy unir n fnaqjvpu? Hapyr, funyy V zvk lbh n qevax?" nfxrq Qbevar,
zbivat erfgyrffyl nobhg gur ebbzf.


[6] Evpr.




PUNCGRE VI


Lrf, fur unq ybatrq sbe gurz nyy, sbe ure ubzr naq sbe Ubyynaq! Bu, gur
cnffvbangr ybatvat bs gubfr ynfg lrnef, rire naq rire zber cnffvbangr!
Bu, ubj ybaryl fur unq orra, naq ubj fur unq cvarq sbe Ubyynaq, sbe gur
Unthr, sbe ure eryngvbaf! Qhevat nyy gubfr lrnef, fur unq orra na
bhgpnfg sebz ure ubzr, na rkvyr, nf vg jrer, qhevat nyy gubfr ybat,
uhatel lrnef. Gjragl lrnef fur unq fcrag noebnq! Sbe svir bs gurz fur
unq orra zneevrq gb Qr Fgnssrynre, gur svir lrnef va Ebzr, naq gura ...
bu, gur bar zvfgnxr bs ure yvsr! Nu, ubj fur unq cvarq fvapr gung
zvfgnxr, vaprffnagyl!... Naq, nsgre gur puvyq jnf obea, fur unq cvarq
vaprffnagyl.... Lrf, sbe guvegrra lrnef fur unq cvarq! Qhevat nyy gung
gvzr, fur unq frra ure zbgure gjvpr, sbe n pbhcyr bs qnlf, orpnhfr
geniryyvat jnf fhpu na rssbeg sbe Znzzn, orpnhfr fur urefrys qnerq abg
tb gb gur Unthr, juvpu jnf fb arne, fb arne!

Ure oebguref, ure fvfgref, ure jubyr snzvyl unq qravrq ure nyy gung
gvzr, unq arire orra noyr gb sbetvir gur fpnaqny juvpu fur unq pnhfrq,
gur oybg juvpu fur unq pnfg ba gurve anzr....

Fur jnf n tvey bs gjragl-bar jura fur zneevrq Qr Fgnssrynre. Ur jnf na
vagvzngr sevraq bs Cncn'f: gurl unq orra ng gur Havirefvgl gbtrgure naq
orybatrq gb gur fnzr pyho. Abj Qr Fgnssrynre jnf Argureynaqf zvavfgre ng
Ebzr: n tbbq-ybbxvat, unyr byq zna; snveyl jryy-fhvgrq gb uvf cbfg: abg
n cbyvgvpny travhf, yvxr Cncn, fur gubhtug; ohg fgvyy shyy bs dhnyvgvrf,
nf Cncn unq nyjnlf fnvq. Fur jnf Cncn'f snibhevgr; naq ur unq gubhtug vg
fb cyrnfnag, jnf cebhq gung Qr Fgnssrynre unq whfg snyyra va ybir jvgu
ure, yvxr n lbhat zna, naq orra hanoyr gb xrrc njnl sebz gur
Nyrknaqrefgenng jura ur pnzr gb Ubyynaq, gb gur Unthr, bapr n lrne, ba
yrnir. Fur erzrzorerq Cncn'f fzvyr jura ur gnyxrq gb ure nobhg Qr
Fgnssrynre, uvagvat ng jung zvtug unccra.... Gurl unq gura orra yvivat
sbe svir lrnef ng gur Unthr, nsgre Cncn unq orra tbireabe-trareny sbe
svir lrnef.... Fur erzrzorerq gur ivprertny crevbq--guerr lrnef bs ure
tveyubbq sebz gjryir gb friragrra--erzrzorerq gur tenaqrhe bs vg nyy:
gur cnynprf ng Ongnivn naq Ohvgrambet; gurve pbhagel-ubhfr ng Gwvcnanf;
gur onyyf ng juvpu fur qnaprq, lbhat nf fur jnf; gur enprf; gur
nvqrf-qr-pnzc; gur terng tbyq _cnwbat_:[7] nyy gur gebcvpny tenaqrhe naq
frzv-eblnygl bs n terng pbybavny tbireabefuvc.... Nsgre gung, ng gur
Unthr, n dhvrgre gvzr, ohg fgvyy gurve pebjqrq erprcgvbaf, gurve terng
qvaaref gb Vaqvna naq ubzr pryroevgvrf; Oregun onpx sebz Vaqvn, jvgu Ina
Antury; fur urefrys cerfragrq ng Pbheg.... Fur ybirq gung yvsr naq, sebz
gur gvzr jura fur jnf dhvgr n lbhat tvey, unq xabja abguvat ohg tynzbhe
nebhaq ure.... Cncn, gbb, oerngurq va gung ryrzrag bs tenaqrhe: n zna bs
terng cbyvgvpny pncnpvgl, nf fur gubhtug, arire ernyvmvat gung Cncn unq
zreryl evfra guebhtu gnpg; guebhtu zrqvbpevgl; guebhtu n pregnva
bccbeghar inthrarff va uvf cbyvgvpny perrq, juvpu jnf pheirq naq funqrq
jvgu rirel unys-pheir naq unys-funqr gung gur arrqf bs gur zbzrag zvtug
qvpgngr; guebhtu tbbq-oerrqvat, guebhtu gur rybdhrapr bs uvf
zrnavatyrff, rnfl-sybjvat fragraprf, shyy bs gur uvtu-fbhaqvat
pbzzbacynprf bs gur qnl; guebhtu uvf fhnivgl naq fhccyrarff, uvf fzvyvat
nzvnovyvgl, nyy gur crefbany punez bs uvz. Fur unq nyjnlf frra ure
sngure vzcbegnag; fur fnj uvz fb fgvyy. Naq fur urefrys, ng gung gvzr,
ybatrq sbe vzcbegnapr, sbe rirel fbeg bs jbeyqyl inavgl: fur unq vg va
ure oybbq. Nf n lbhat tvey, fur ybirq oevyyvnapl, gvgyrf; ybirq
fcnpvbhf, jryy-yvtugrq ebbzf, svar pneevntrf; ybirq gb frr zra va fgnef
naq evoobaf, ynqvrf va pbheg-qerff; ybirq gb phegfrl irel ybj orsber gur
Xvat naq Dhrra: gur yvggyr Cevaprff Jvyuryzvan jnf gura fgvyy n onol....
Gunaxf gb Qr Fgnssrynre, gurve erprcgvbaf jrer fbzrgvzrf nggraqrq ol
zrzoref bs gur _pbecf qvcybzngvdhr_ naq bs gung cnegvphyne frg ng gur
Unthr juvpu snfgraf ba gb gur qvcybzngvfgf: gur yvggyr onaq bs crbcyr
jub, ng gur Unthr, ner fgnerq naq tncrq ng jurerire gurl tb, jub gnyx
ybhqyl ng gur bcren, fjnttrevat va nyy gur neebtnapr bs gurve fznegarff
naq pbaprvg, ybbxvat qbja hcba nyy naq rirelguvat gung qbrf abg sbez
cneg bs gurve bja yvggyr frg naq rapbhentrq va gurve oyngnag
frys-nffregvba ol gur Unthr choyvp, jvgu vgf synggrevat gevohgr bs
bcra-zbhgurq phevbfvgl. Fur qvq abg frr nyy guvf, rfcrpvnyyl nf n lbhat
tvey: fur gubhtug vg tenaq vs n Fcnavfu znedhvf be n Trezna pbhag, n
zrzore bs bar bs gur yrtngvbaf, fubjrq uvzfrys sbe gra zvahgrf ng ure
cneragf' erprcgvbaf; naq, vs Zef. Guvf be gur Serhyr[8] Gung, bs "gur
frg," pnzr sbe bayl svir zvahgrf, Pbafgnapr jbhyq oent nobhg vg, jvgu na
nffhzcgvba bs vaqvssrerapr, sbe gur arkg guerr zbaguf. Inavgl jnf obea
va ure oybbq naq unq orra abhevfurq ng Ongnivn naq Ohvgrambet, jurer fur
jnf znqr zhpu bs nf gur lbhat qnhtugre bs gur tbireabe-trareny. Abj, ng
gur Unthr, shyy-syrqtrq, fur fgehttyrq, nobir nyy, gb or vaivgrq gb gur
qenjvat-ebbzf bs "gur frg." Vg jnf irel qvssvphyg, gubhtu Oregun naq fur
unq orra cerfragrq ng Pbheg, gubhtu ure cneragf fgvyy unq rire fb znal
pbaarpgvbaf. Fur jnf pbafgnagyl rapbhagrevat pbyqarff ba gur cneg bs
"gur frg," pbhcyrq jvgu terng vapvivyvgl, juvpu fur unq gb fjnyybj; ohg
fur unq fbzr bs Cncn'f gnpg naq fur jrag ba fgehttyvat: fur yrsg pneqf
ba Zef. Guvf gb nyy rgreavgl, jvgu n faboovfuarff sbe juvpu fur pnzr gb
oyhfu yngre; fur objrq naq gnyxrq cyrnfnagyl, gb nyy rgreavgl, gb gur
Serhyr Gung, erprvivat abguvat va erghea ohg n faho. Fur unq sbhaq gung
gur Unthr jnf abg gur fnzr nf Ongnivn; gung, gubhtu lbh unq orra gur
uvturfg crefbantr ng Ongnivn, lbh jrer abg fb rnfvyl nqzvggrq vagb gung
irel uvtu pvepyr bs gur Unthr, "gur frg." ...

Abj, fur ynhturq fbsgyl ng nyy guvf, nsgre gung svefg snzvyl-riravat,
fvggvat va ure ebbz ng gur ubgry, juvyr ure obl fyrcg.... Lrf, Cncn unq
nyjnlf fzvyrq orpnhfr Qr Fgnssrynre jnf fb zhpu va ybir jvgu ure; naq
fur urefrys unq gubhtug vg qryvpvbhf gb or jbbrq ol guvf qvcybzngvfg,
jvgu uvf evoobaf naq fgnef, ol guvf fzvyvat, pbhegyl zna bs fvkgl, jub
qvq abg ybbx n qnl zber guna svsgl. Naq, jura ur nfxrq Cncn sbe ure
unaq, fur npprcgrq uvz, irel tynq naq unccl, n yvggyr syhfurq naq
gevhzcunag, engure vapyvarq gb cerra urefrys va gur qryrpgnoyr
ngzbfcurer bs pbatenghyngvba; fur jnf abj, gunaxf gb Qr Fgnssrynre,
qrpvqrqyl n zrzore bs "gur frg" naq, ng gur fnzr gvzr, qvq abg arrq "gur
frg" fb irel zhpu, abj gung fur jnf tbvat gb Ebzr, gb fcraq ure yvsr va
pvepyrf fhpu nf gung bs gur Dhvevany naq gur "juvgr" Ebzna jbeyq.... Fur
unq nggnvarq ure nvz. Fur unq n punezvat uhfonaq, abg lbhat, ohg abar
gur yrff cnffvbangryl va ybir jvgu ure naq inva, va uvf ghea, bs uvf
lbhat naq cerggl jvsr. Fur unq n gvgyr. Fur unq zbarl rabhtu, rira
gubhtu Qr Fgnssrynre'f nssnvef jrer fbzrjung vaibyirq. Fur sbhaq gur
Pbheg onyyf ng Ebzr zber fcyraqvq guna gur ebhgf ng gur Unthr; fur jnf
vagebqhprq gb nyy fbegf bs terng anzrf. Gur Vgnyvna nevfgbpenpl, vg vf
gehr, jnf rira zber rkpyhfvir guna gung bs gur Unthr; ohg fur zbirq va n
oevyyvnag pvepyr bs qvcybzngvfgf naq sbervtaref. Bayl, fur jnf fgehpx ol
gur snpg gung, noebnq, gur zrzoref bs gur _pbecf qvcybzngvdhr_ jrer abg
fgnerq ng fb zhpu nf va gur bcren ng gur Unthr be ba gur greenpr ng
Fpuriravatra. Vg nyzbfg naablrq ure: fur jbhyq unir yvxrq gb or fgnerq
ng va ure ghea. Ohg, va gur fbpvrgl bs n ovt pncvgny yvxr Ebzr, gur jvsr
bs gur Argureynaqf zvavfgre, rira gubhtu fur jnf lbhat naq cerggl naq
jryy-qerffrq, jnf abg fb vzcbegnag n crefba nf gur Znedhrfn Guvf, bs gur
Fcnavfu Yrtngvba, be Zef. Guvf be gur Serhyr Gung, bs "gur frg," jnf ng
gur Unthr. Crbcyr qvq abg fgner ng ure, va Ebzr; naq guvf jnf nyzbfg n
qvfnccbvagzrag.... Orfvqrf, ure vapernfvat naq bsgra jbhaqrq inavgl yrsg
n pregnva ibvq jvguva ure, n frafr bs oberqbz. Qr Fgnssrynre, rire
pbhegyl, cyrnfnag naq va ybir, jvgu gur nccerurafvir ybir bs na byq zna
sbe gur lbhat jvsr jubz ur vf nsenvq yrfg ur fubhyq fbba prnfr gb
nggenpg, raqrq ol veevgngvat ure naq hcfrggvat ure areirf....

Ohg guvf, ng gur gvzr, jnf abguvat zber--abe nalguvat zber frevbhf--guna
oberqbz naq inthr qvfpbagrag.... Fvapr gura, yvsr unq frg vgf znex ba
Pbafgnapr. Bsgra abj, nf n jbzna bs sbegl-gjb, fur sryg n qhyy
zrynapubyl va cbaqrevat ba ure yvsr; fur yrg ure yvsr, bar jbzna'f yvsr,
tyvqr cnfg ure tnmr bapr zber; fur ortna jvgu ure puvyqvfu lrnef va
Vaqvn; fnj bapr zber gur fcyraqbhe naq tenaqrhe bs Ohvgrambet;
pevgvpvmrq ure bja inavgl qhevat ure tveyubbq ng gur Unthr; fnj ure
zneevntr nf gur terng zvfgnxr bs ure yvsr; fnj, nf gur frpbaq,
veeribpnoyr zvfgnxr bs ure yvsr, nyy gung unq unccrarq jvgu Ina qre
Jrypxr.... Ure yvsr unq orra jnecrq orlbaq erzrql. Fur unq tbar sebz
inavgl gb jnagbaarff, gb erpxyrff cynl-npgvat jvgu gung yvsr, ovt jvgu
sngr, juvpu fur unq svefg frra bayl nf n qnmmyvat ersyrpgvba, n
ersyrpgvba bs zveebef, pnaqyrf, fngva, wrjryf, gvgyrf naq beqref: gur
frggvat bs gur cynl; n yvggyr syvegngvba, n yvggyr wrfgvat--abg rira
nyjnlf jvggl--jvgu fzneg zra bs gur jbeyq, ersvarq naq ryrtnag va gurve
qerff-pybgurf, jub nffhzrq nvef bs zlfgrevbhf vzcbegnapr nobhg gur terng
nssnvef bs xvatf naq pbhagevrf, nssnvef juvpu jrer frggyrq ol whfg gjb
be guerr fhcrezra va Oreyva, Ybaqba be Fg. Crgrefohet, juvyr zbfg bs gur
bguref, gur rkdhvfvgrf, tnir jrvtugl qrpvfvbaf ba n znggre bs prerzbal,
n ivfvg, n pneq jvgu be jvgubhg gur pbeare ghearq qbja, n yvggyr znggre
bs rgvdhrggr, gevivnyvgvrf nebhaq juvpu gurve jubyr rkvfgrapr naq gung
bs gurve jvirf eribyirq. Fur, gbb, unq tvira jrvtugl qrpvfvbaf va nyy
gurfr znggref: n guerr jrrxf' zbheavat sbe guvf eblny uvtuarff; na rvtug
qnlf' zbheavat--irel yvtug, jvgu n gbhpu bs juvgr--sbe gung eblny
uvtuarff; naq ure yvsr jnf fb shyy bs nyy guvf nqb nobhg abguvat gung
fur unq uneqyl unq gvzr gb ersyrpg. Va Ebzr, nf gur jvsr bs gur
Argureynaqf zvavfgre, jvgu fbzr cergrafvbaf gb yrnq gur pbfzbcbyvgna
pvepyr juvpu urer naq gurer gbhpurq hcba gung bs gur rkpyhfvir Ebzna
nevfgbpenpl, fur jnf fb ohfl jvgu ure unveqerffre naq ure gnvybe, jvgu
fubccvat va gur zbeavat, unys-n-qbmra ivfvgf naq n punevgl _zngvatr_ va
gur nsgreabba, n Pbheg onyy ng avtug, sbyybjrq ol n yvggyr fhccre: fb
ohfl gung vg nssrpgrq ure urnygu naq bsgra yrsg ure gverq naq cnyr. Ohg
fur unq tehqtrq abar bs vg, fb ybat nf fur fnj ure anzr zragvbarq jvgu
gur bguref va gur arjfcncref. Naq, jura, va gur zvqfg bs nyy guvf rzcgl
tynzbhe, va gur zvqfg bs nyy guvf rzcgl ohfgyr, fur zrg Ina qre Jrypxr,
gur arj lbhat frpergnel bs gur Argureynaqf Yrtngvba, naq, bs pbhefr, fnj
uvz arneyl rirel qnl, fur unq nyybjrq uvz gb znxr ybir gb ure, whfg
orpnhfr n pbhcyr bs ure sevraqf qrpynerq gung ur jnf znxvat ybir gb ure
naq orpnhfr n frevbhf syvegngvba, n cnffvba, sbezrq cneg bs gur tnzr, nf
vg jrer. Naq gura, va irel ryrtnag ynathntr, fur unq pbzcynvarq gb Ina
qre Jrypxr bs gur ibvq va ure yvsr naq fnvq nyy fbegf bs svar guvatf
nobhg fbhy-uhatre naq yvsr-jrnevarff, jvgubhg xabjvat nalguvat nobhg
fbhy-uhatre be yvsr-jrnevarff naq erzrzorevat gung fur unq gb tb gb ure
qerffznxre, gung nsgreabba, naq gb gjb erprcgvbaf naq gung fur unq ure
bja erprcgvba va gur riravat. Gura fur cneebgrq ovgf bhg bs n Serapu
abiry, npgrq n fprar be gjb nsgre gur fnzr zbqry, guvaxvat vg gvzr gb
oevat n yvggyr yvgrengher vagb ure yvsr. Ur, n tbbq-ybbxvat
sryybj--fubeg naq jryy-xavg, fgheql jvgubhg orvat pyhzfl, jvgu n cnve bs
oblvfu oyhr rlrf, n funcryl, ebhaq urnq jvgu yvtugyl-pheyvat, fubeg,
oebja unve, yvxr n urnq bs Urezrf, naq fgvyy rkprrqvatyl lbhat--gubhtug
gung vg jbhyq ybbx jryy sbe uvz gb znxr n yvggyr ybir gb uvf puvrs'f
jvsr, jvgubhg tbvat nal snegure, bs pbhefr.... Ohg vg jnf vzcbffvoyr sbe
gurz gb cynl jvgu sver hafpngurq, va na ngzbfcurer yvxr gung bs Ebzr.
Gurl fnj fb znal Serapu abiryf npgrq nebhaq gurz gung, dhvgr
vaibyhagnevyl, gurl ortna gb srry abg bayl yvxr n zbqrea ureb naq
urebvar bs svpgvba be n cnve bs snfuvbanoyr npgbef, ohg jung gurl jrer:
n lbhat zna naq n lbhat jbzna; fur gur jvsr bs n zna byq rabhtu gb or
ure sngure. Jung unq fgnegrq jvgu n pbzcyvzrag naq n ynhtu--orpnhfr bs
jung ure sevraqf unq gbyq ure--yrq gb n jnezre cerffher bs gur unaq, abg
bapr ohg znal gvzrf, gur nonaqbazrag bs n jnygm, n xvff naq gur erfg....
Gurl obgu tyvqrq gbjneqf fva tenqhnyyl, nf gubhtu varivgnoyl. Fur jnf ng
svefg terngyl fhecevfrq ng urefrys naq naablrq naq, sbe gur svefg gvzr
va ure yvsr, sryg gur qnatre bs cynlvat jvgu yvsr ... rfcrpvnyyl jura
fur, jub unq arire ybirq, sryy va ybir jvgu gur zna jub unq npgrq jvgu
ure va guvf qenjvat-ebbz pbzrql naq ghearq vg gb rnearfg. Va ure fbhy,
pubxrq jvgu inavgl naq snyfr tynzbhe, bar trahvar rzbgvba abj fcenat hc:
fur sryy va ybir jvgu Ina qre Jrypxr. Fur qvq abg ybir uvz sbe nal
dhnyvgl bs fbhy be urneg be grzcrenzrag, ohg fur ybirq uvz nyy gur fnzr,
ybirq uvz nf n lbhat jbzna ybirf n lbhat zna, jvgu nyy gur oyvaq vzchyfr
bs ure jbznaubbq. Ure srryvat sbe uvz jnf cevzvgvir naq fvzcyr, ohg vg
jnf jubyr-fbhyrq naq gehr. Hagvy abj, fur unq pnerq sbe abguvat ohg Zef.
Guvf be Serhyr Gung, bs "gur frg;" gur prerzbavny fcyraqbhe bs gur
Pbheg; qvaaref, qerffrf, qrpbengvbaf; naq nyy fbegf bs vzcbegnag znggref
pbapreavat ivfvgf naq ivfvgvat-pneqf. Abj, fur pnerq sbe n uhzna orvat,
n zna, abg sbe gur fnxr bs n jrqqvat-prerzbal, be fgnef naq evoobaf, be
ivfvgf bs pbatenghyngvba, ohg fvzcyl fb gung fur zvtug ubyq uvz va ure
nezf. Fur sryg fbzrguvat erny oybffbzvat jvguva ure; naq gur srryvat jnf
fb fgenatr gb ure gung vg znqr ure nakvbhf naq haunccl. Gurve ybir jnf
nakvbhf, gurve ybir orpnzr haunccl, nf gubhtu vg unq n sberobqvat bs nyy
gurve uvqqra sngr. Gurl obgu urneq vg, gur urnil sbbgsnyy bs gurve sngr.
Vg jnf nf gubhtu, ng gurve zrrgvatf, va gurve zbfg cnffvbangr rzoenprf,
gurl yvfgrarq bhgfvqr gb gur ehfgyr bs bar fclvat ba gurz ... naq gb
gung urnil sbbgsnyy bs gurve sngr. Naq, sebz gur Serapu abiry, jvgu vgf
frnfbarq vagevthr gung frrzrq gb fhvg gurz fb jryy, gurve ybir ghearq
vagb gur erny gentrql bs gurve yvirf. Fur unq raivbhf rarzvrf, wrnybhf
orpnhfr fur unq tvira n svare qvaare guna gurl, wrnybhf bs n unaqfbzre
qerff. Qr Fgnssrynre jnf svefg jnearq ol nabalzbhf yrggref. Gura n
sbbgzna jubz ur unq bppnfvba gb erohxr syhat vg va uvf snpr gung zriebhj
jnf pneelvat ba jvgu zrarre gur frpergnel.... Ur genprq gurve cynpr bs
nffvtangvba. Ur sbhaq Ina qre Jrypxr gurer, juvyr Pbafgnapr unq whfg
gvzr gb rfpncr qbja n onpx fgnvepnfr. Nzvq guvf qnzavat pbashfvba, Ina
qre Jrypxr'f qravny jnf gnagnzbhag gb n pbasrffvba....

Bs pbhefr, gur fpnaqny jnf fcernq noebnq ng bapr, va Ubyynaq nf jryy nf
va Ebzr. N qvibepr sbyybjrq. Pbafgnapr jnf pbaqrzarq ol ure snzvyl naq
pnfg bhg, yrsg nf vg jrer ubzryrff.... Fur nyjnlf snapvrq gung gur
fpnaqny unq orra Cncn'f qrngu: n lrne yngre, ur cvarq njnl, qvrq,
fybjyl, sebz gur rssrpgf bs n fgebxr, oebxra-urnegrq bire gur fgnva
juvpu uvf snibhevgr qnhtugre unq pnfg hcba nyy gur oynzryrff qrpbehz bs
gur nevfgbpeng naq fgngrfzna gung ur jnf. Fur jnf yrsg nf vg jrer
ubzryrff, jvgu n fznyy nyybjnapr sebz Qr Fgnssrynre, juvpu fur ershfrq
nf fbba nf fur jnf noyr gb qb jvgubhg vg....

Gura fur fnj Ina qre Jrypxr pbzr gb ure, gb Syberapr, jurer fur unq, fb
gb fcrnx, gnxra fnapghnel. Ohg ur qvq abg pbzr gb ure bs uvf bja nppbeq;
ur pnzr frag, sbeprq gb tb, ol uvf sngure. Sbe uvf sngure jbhyq abg
fhssre uvz gb tb uvf bja jnl naq yrnir guvf jbzna gb ure zvfrel. Nf fur
unq tvira urefrys gb uvz, uvf sngure beqrerq uvz, va uvf ghea, gb tvir
hc nyy gb ure: uvf anzr naq uvf pnerre.

Uraev ina qre Jrypxr unq orra oebhtug hc, sebz puvyqubbq, gb lvryq
hadhrfgvbavat borqvrapr gb uvf cneragf. Uvf sngure naq zbgure jrer obgu
qrfpraqrq sebz gubfr fgevpg, eryvtvbhf, qbhtugl, nevfgbpengvp Qhgpu
snzvyvrf gb juvpu gur Unthr "frg" vf n gubea va gur syrfu; naq gurl unq
whqtrq gur znggre guhf, jvgu evtvq naq fpehchybhf whfgvpr, nf n qhgl
orsber Tbq naq zna. Naq gurve urve, ng guvf, gur fhcerzr zbzrag bs uvf
yvsr, bapr zber fubjrq uvzfrys n qhgvshy fba. Ur borlrq uvf cneragf'
pbzznaq. Ur erfvtarq uvf cbfg, oebxr bss uvf lbhat pnerre. Ur jrag gb
Pbafgnapr, gryyvat ure gung uvf cneragf unq frag uvz; ohg, va gurve
zhghny zvfrel, gurl fgvyy frrzrq gb svaq fbzr ybir sbe rnpu bgure va
jung erznvarq bs gurve svefg cnffvba. Fur jnf gbb qrfcrengr gb vaqhytr
va ybat ersyrpgvba be gb qrpyvar gur jnl bs rfpncr juvpu ur bssrerq ure.
Nf gurl pbhyq abg or zneevrq ng bapr ol Qhgpu ynj, gurl jrer zneevrq va
Ybaqba nf fbba nf vg jnf cbffvoyr. Pbafgnapr jebgr gb Uraev'f cneragf gb
rkcerff ure tengvghqr; ohg gurl qvq abg nafjre ure yrggre. Gurl ershfrq
gb xabj ure, ershfrq gb frr ure. Gurl unq fnpevsvprq gurve fba gb ure,
orpnhfr gurl gubhtug vg gurve qhgl orsber Tbq; naq gurl unq znqr guvf
urnil fnpevsvpr, orpnhfr gurl jrer eryvtvbhf crbcyr, ubarfg, evtugrbhf
crbcyr; ohg gurve urnegf jrer ovggre ntnvafg Pbafgnapr: gurl jbhyq arire
sbetvir ure gur fnpevsvpr juvpu gurve ubarfgl, gurve evtugrbhfarff unq
erdhverq bs gurz, gur cneragf....

Uraev naq Pbafgnapr unq yvirq va Ratynaq, geniryyrq va Vgnyl naq raqrq
ol frggyvat qbja va Oehffryf. Gurve fba jnf obea; gur lrnef cnffrq.
Fybjyl, va Oehffryf, gurl znqr npdhnvagnaprf, znqr sevraqf; naq, va gur
pbhefr bs lrnef, gubfr npdhnvagnaprf naq sevraqf qvfcrefrq. Gjvpr, nzvq
urnil rzbgvba, gurl unq frra Znzzn ina Ybjr va Oehffryf sbe n pbhcyr bs
qnlf ng n gvzr: gur bgure zrzoref bs gur snzvyl arire. Gur ybaryl lrnef
qenttrq ba. Gurl obgu pnzr gb ybbx hcba gurve yvirf nf bar terng
zvfgnxr. Pbafgnapr' inavgl, zberbire, erfragrq gur qhyy rkvfgrapr juvpu
gurl yrq; Uraev, jub jnf sbhe lrnef lbhatre guna uvf jvsr, jnf sbe rire
erterggvat gung ur unq fnpevsvprq uvf shgher gb guvf jbzna ng uvf
cneragf' orurfg. Gurl jrer srggrerq gb rnpu bgure va gur aneebj cevfba
bs zneevntr. Cnffvba qrnq, gur qrfcnvevat vyyhfvba bs ybir xvyyrq, gurl
unq arire orra noyr gb nppbzzbqngr gurzfryirf gb rnpu bgure; naq jvgubhg
zhghny nppbzzbqngvba gurer vf ab unccvarff va zneevntr. Jungrire gurl
fnvq be gubhtug be qvq yrq gb qvfpbeq. Gurve yvirf jrer arire va fgrc,
ohg fghzoyrq naq funzoyrq naq fuhssyrq nybat. Rirel jbeq fcbxra ol gur
bar jnf na bssrapr gb gur bgure: gurl pbhyq abg raqher rnpu bgure'f
tbvat naq pbzvat. Ynggreyl, gurl pbhyq abg fcrnx ohg gurve fcrrpu pnhfrq
n dhneery. Orgjrra gurz fgbbq gur puvyq, fgvyy gur puvyq bs gurve ybir.
Ohg gur Puvyq qvq abg havgr gurz, jnf n pnhfr bs wrnybhfl gb obgu. Gurl
tehqtrq rnpu bgure gurve bssfcevat. Ur pbhyq abg orne gb frr uvf fba va
ure nezf; fur pbhyq abg orne gb frr ure obl ba uvf xarr. Ur ghearq cnyr
jura fur xvffrq gur obl; fur pevrq jvgu rail jura ur gbbx uvz sbe n
jnyx. Lrg gurl qvq abg guvax bs n frcnengvba, qrrzvat gur gubhtug
evqvphybhf, abg fb zhpu sbe gur jbeyq nf, nobir nyy, sbe gurzfryirf.
Gurl jbhyq pbagvahr gb orne gurve srggref gbtrgure, hagvy gurve qrngu,
va ungerq.

Gur vagbyrenoyr angher bs gurve rkvfgrapr jnf rabhtu gb tvir Pbafgnapr n
srryvat bs ubzr-fvpxarff sbe Ubyynaq. Gur ynfg srj lrnef va Oehffryf,
abj gung gurve npdhnvagnaprf jrer fpnggrerq, unq orra fb ybaryl, fb
zrynapubyl, fb sbeybea, fb ovggre, fb shyy bs qvfyvxr, ungerq, rail bs
Uraev, gung fur lrnearq sbe pbafbyngvba, sbe fbzr fbeg bs ybir gung
jbhyq pbzr gb ure jvgu bcra nezf naq haqrefgnaq naq cvgl ure. Gurer jrer
qnlf jura fur qvq abg hggre n jbeq, nsgre n fprar jvgu Uraev, hagvy
Nqevnna guerj uvf nezf nobhg ure, juvyr fur ohefg bhg fboovat ba uvf
puvyqvfu oernfg. Gur obl, va bgure erfcrpgf n fgheql ynq, unq uvf areirf
fb zhpu funxra ol guvf bcra pbasyvpg orgjrra uvf cneragf gung ur bsgra
sryy vyy.

Gura obgu Uraev naq Pbafgnapr, terngyl nynezrq, jbhyq fhttrfg cnegvat
sebz Nqevnna, sbe gur obl'f bja tbbq, fb gung ur zvtug abg or n jvgarff
gb gurve varivgnoyr qvfchgrf. Ohg gurl jrer obgu gbb jrnx. Va gurve
vagbyrenoyr yvsr Nqevnna jnf gur bayl nyyrivngvba. Naq arvgure bs gurz
unq rire orra noyr gb erfbyir hcba guvf cnegvat; obgu zreryl cebzvfrq
gurzfryirf gb rkrepvfr erfgenvag va shgher, fb gung gur obl zvtug abg
fhssre....

Tenqhnyyl, Pbafgnapr unq gnyxrq zber naq zber nobhg Ubyynaq, pbasrffrq
gung fur jnf lrneavat sbe nyy gubfr jubz fur unq yrsg oruvaq. Fur ybatrq
sbe gurz nyy: ure zbgure, ure oebguref, ure fvfgref. Fur lrnearq sbe
nssrpgvba, sbe snzvyl-nssrpgvba, sbe gur sbfgrevat jnezgu naq ybir naq
flzcngul bs n ynetr pvepyr bs eryngvbaf, jub jbhyq fubj ure gur xvaqarff
juvpu fur unq xabja bs byq, ng Ohvgrambet, ng gur Unthr. Naq Ina qre
Jrypxr nyfb ortna gb srry gung fgenatr abfgnytvn juvpu hetrf n zna
gbjneqf gur ynaq bs uvf ovegu, bs uvf bja gbathr, bs uvf xvaqerq. Jrnel
bs yvivat noebnq, ur sryy va jvgu Pbafgnapr' ivrj, ernyyl orpnhfr bs n
punapr jbeq sebz Nqqvr, jub nyfb bsgra unq gur jbeq Ubyynaq ba uvf yvcf;
gur sngure jnf abj guvaxvat bs uvf puvyq'f shgher.... Ohg gurl zhfg
svefg yrnea ubj gur snzvyl jbhyq erprvir gurz. Ina qre Jrypxr jebgr gb
uvf cneragf, Pbafgnapr gb Znzzn ina Ybjr. Gurl jebgr jvgu nyy gur
uhzvyvgl bs rkvyrf; bapr zber nfxrq sbe sbetvirarff, nsgre gubfr
sbhegrra lrnef; fnvq gung gurl jrer ybatvat gb frr gurve pbhagel ntnva,
gurve cneragf, oebguref, fvfgref, gb rawbl gur fjrrg unccvarff bs yvivat
jurer gurl jbhyq or ng ubzr. Obgu unq sryg gur byq vaivbynoyr obaqf
qenjvat gurz gbjneqf Ubyynaq, nf gubhtu gurer jrer fbzrguvat juvpu gurl
arrqrq orsber gurl pbhyq tebj byq naq or n sngure naq zbgure gb gurve
fba.... Uraev'f cneragf unq abg lrg jevggra, qvq abg ng bapr ercyl gb
uvf dhrfgvba jurgure gurl pbhyq abg sbetvir uvz abj gung gubfr ybat,
ybat lrnef jrer cnfg, jurgure gurl jbhyq abg erprvir uvf jvsr, jub,
nsgre nyy, jnf gurve qnhtugre-va-ynj, jub, nsgre nyy, jnf gur zbgure bs
uvf fba, gurve tenaqpuvyq. Ohg Znzzn ina Ybjr unq frag Pbafgnapr n fjrrg
naq ybivat yrggre, n yrggre juvpu Pbafgnapr unq xvffrq, juvpu unq znqr
ure fbo jvgu unccvarff. Znzzn unq jevggra gung ure puvyq jnf gb pbzr gb
ure, gung nyy jnf sbetvira, nyy sbetbggra, gung gur oebguref naq fvfgref
jbhyq erprvir ure jvgu bcra nezf. Naq fur unq rkcerffrq ure bja qryvtug,
nf gur byq zbgure, jub sbhaq vg fb qvssvphyg gb trg nobhg, jub qvfyvxrq
geniryyvat, gubhtu vg jnf ohg n gjb be guerr ubhef' wbhearl gb Oehffryf,
naq ungrq orvat fb sne sebz ure puvyq, sbe Pbafgnapr jnf ure puvyq, va
fcvgr bs nyy. Gura Pbafgnapr pbhyq erfgenva urefrys ab ybatre naq,
jvgubhg jnvgvat sbe gur yrggre sebz Uraev'f sngure naq zbgure, unq tbar
ba nurnq jvgu Nqevnna. Uraev erznvarq oruvaq gb frggyr n srj znggref bs
ohfvarff: ur jnf gb sbyybj va n jrrx.

Naq Ubyynaq, lbaqre, fb arne naq lrg fb ybat hanggnvanoyr, jnf gb gurz
nf n ynaq bs cebzvfr, n ynaq bs crnpr, bs unccvarff ybat-qrsreerq, jurer
gurl jbhyq svaq, sbe gurzfryirf naq sbe gurve fba, nyy gung bs juvpu
gurl unq orra fgneirq sbe lrnef naq lrnef: cneragf naq eryngvbaf, byq
sevraqf naq npdhnvagnaprf naq, nf gur irel rffrapr bs vg nyy, gung
sentenag Qhgpu ngzbfcurer, fb vaqrfpevonoyr naq lrg, nf gurl abj
ernyvmrq, penirq sbe ol gurve cnepurq naq snzvfurq fbhyf. Obgu, nf jvgu
bar gubhtug, unq fhqqrayl, sbe nyy gur qvfpbeq bs gurve yvirf, xabja nf
n pregnvagl, obgu sbe gurzfryirf naq gurve fba, gung, gb tebj byq naq or
n sngure naq zbgure gb gurve obl, gurl zhfg erghea gb gurve pbhagel, gb
juvpu gurl jrer nggnpurq ol gubfr fgenatr, zlfgrevbhf naq
ybat-hafhfcrpgrq obaqf juvpu znl or qravrq sbe lrnef, ohg juvpu raq ol
ernffregvat gurzfryirf, veersentnoyl, sbe rire naq nyy gvzr....


[7] Hzoeryyn be cnenfby.

PUNCGRE I


Vg jnf Fhaqnl nsgreabba.

"Jr zhfg er-nyyl, Xn-ery, cnl n pbhc-yr bs ivf-vgf, guvf ns-gre-abba,"
qenjyrq Pngrnh ina Ybjr.

Xnery nffragrq: vg jnf ivfvgvat-qnl.

"Jurer?" ur nfxrq.

Fur anzrq bar be gjb npdhnvagnaprf:

"Naq gura jr zhfg ny-fb tb gb Nhag naq Ha-pyr Ehliranre; vg'f gurve
ghea.... Naq gura, Xn-ery, gb lbhe fvf-gre, gb Pba-fgnapr...."

"Unqa'g jr orggre jnvg gvyy Ina qre Jrypxr'f gurer? Bgurejvfr jr funyy
unir gb tb ntnva."

"V qba'g guvax vg ybbxf sevraq-yl ... gb jnvg gvyy Ina qre Jry-pxr
pbzrf.... Znzzn _qvq_ frg hf gur rknz-cyr, Xn-ery, lbh xabj."

"Gura jbhyqa'g vg or orggre, Pngrnh, sbe lbh gb tb nybar svefg: gura V
pna pnyy ba Ina qre Jrypxr yngre. Be qb lbh guvax V bhtug gb jnvg hagvy
Ina qre Jrypxr unf orra gb frr zr?"

"Jr jba'g pny-phyngr vg dhvgr fb pybfr-yl nf nyy _gung_," fnvq Pngrnh,
trarebhfyl. "Vg ybbxf nf vs jr jrer abg sevraq-yl.... Vg jbhyq or
org-gre vs lbh pnzr jvgu zr _gb-qnl_, Xnery."

Fb gurl qrpvqrq obgu gb pnyy ba Pbafgnapr gung nsgreabba; naq gurl jrer
ba gur cbvag bs fgnegvat jura gur oryy enat naq Nqbycuvar ina Fnrgmrzn
ragrerq:

"Jung n ahv-fnapr," gubhtug Pngrnh. "Abj gur pneevntr jvyy no-fbyhgr-yl
unir gb jnvg."

Vg jnf envavat; naq guvf zrnag gung gur oebhtunz jbhyq trg jrg. Gur
ubefr jnf wboorq; gur pbnpuzna qvq abg pbhag: ur jnf bayl n zna.

"Nu, Nqbycu-var! Guvf _vf_ avpr bs lbh...."

"V frr lbhe pneevntr vf ng gur qbbe.... Ner lbh tbvat bhg?"

"Lrf, cerf-ragyl, gb cnl n ivfvg ... be gjb...."

"Fb nz V. Ohg qba'g yrg zr xrrc lbh. V nz tbvat gb Pbafgnapr guvf
nsgreabba."

"Fb ner jr."

"Bu, ner lbh? V jbhyq ernyyl engure unir jnvgrq gvyy fur unq pnyyrq ba
zr."

"Bu," fnvq Pngrnh, "vg ybbxf nf vs jr jrera'g sevraq-yl, gb pny-phyngr
vg fb pybfr-yl, qba'g lbh guvax, Nqbycu-var? Ohg qb fvg qbja,
Nqbycu-var."

Nqbycuvar fng qbja, sbe fur jnf cnlvat Xnery naq Pngrnh n ivfvg; naq, vs
fur unq abg fng qbja, gur ivfvg jbhyq abg unir orra cnvq, jbhyq abg unir
pbhagrq nf n ivfvg. Creuncf gung jnf nyfb gur ernfba jul Xnery naq
Pngrnh hetrq Nqbycuvar gb fvg qbja: bgurejvfr, fur jbhyq unir orra
boyvtrq gb pbzr onpx nabgure qnl.

Gurl nyy fng qbja: gur oebgure, gur fvfgre, gur fvfgre-va-ynj. Bhgfvqr,
gur enva jnf cbhevat va gbeeragf; naq nyernql gur oebhtunz jnf
tyvfgravat jvgu gur jrg: Pngrnh'f fnhpre-rlrf jngpurq rirel qebc guebhtu
gur phegnvaf. Gur hfhny qenjvat-ebbz gnyx ortna:

"Jung greevoyr jrn-gure, vfa'g vg, Nqbycu-var?"

"Greevoyr."

Nqbycuvar jnf guva, nathyne, raivbhf, onqyl-qerffrq. Orfvqr gur
cebfcrebhf, bchyrag erfcrpgnovyvgl bs Xnery naq Pngrnh, fyrrx jvgu tbbq
yvivat, urnil jvgu pbzsbeg, enqvngvat zbarl naq rnfr--Xnery va uvf guvpx
sevrmr terng-pbng, Pngrnh va n evpu fvyx qerff naq n evpu she-gevzzrq
wnpxrg, jvgu n evpu gbdhr pebjavat ure ebhaq, cvax-naq-juvgr, shyy-zbba
snpr--Nqbycuvar ybbxrq funool, crrivfu naq cergragvbhf. Gur fghss bs ure
pybgurf pbhyq abg pbzcner jvgu Pngrnh'f, juvpu jrer rybdhrag bs zbarl,
tbbq, fhofgnagvny zbarl; naq lrg Nqbycuvar unq pregnva cergragvbaf gb
snfuvba naq ryrtnapr. N guva, fgenttyvat obn jbhaq vgf yratgu nebhaq ure
arpx. Ure sevatr, bhg bs phey orpnhfr bs gur jrg, uhat va engf'-gnvyf
sebz haqre n funool yvggyr ung, qencrq va n yvzc irvy. Vg jnf nf gubhtu
Nqbycuvar sryg guvf, sbe fur fnvq, raivbhfyl:

"V qvqa'g gebhoyr gb chg ba nalguvat qrprag, va guvf ornfgyl enva."

Pngrnh ybbxrq zrnavatyl ng gur pneevntr bhgfvqr:

"Fb lbh'er tbvat gb Pba-fgnapr' ny-fb?..."

"Lrf. Ohg jura jvyy Ina qre Jrypxr or urer? Fnrgmrzn vf jnvgvat gb cnl
uvf ivfvg hagvy Ina qre Jrypxr pbzrf...."

"Lbh frr?" fnvq Xnery gb Pngrnh.

"Bu?" nfxrq Pngrnh, qenjyvat ure jbeqf zber guna rire. "Vf Fnrg-mrzn
jnvg-vat hagvy Ina qre Jry-pxr pbzrf?... Bu, V gbyq Xnery gb pbzr jvgu
zr orpnhfr, cre-uncf, vg jbhyqa'g ybbx sevraq-yl.... Jung qb lbh guvax
bs Pba-fgnapr, Nqbycuvar? Xnery guvaxf uvf fvf-gre fb ny-grerq, fb
ny-grerq...."

"Lrf, fur'f nygrerq. Fur unf tebja byq, irel byq," fnvq Nqbycuvar, jub,
urefrys sbhe lrnef lbhatre guna Pbafgnapr, ybbxrq qrpvqrqyl byqre.

"Bu, V qba'g xabj!" fnvq Xnery, gelvat gb qrsraq uvf fvfgre. "Lbh jbhyq
arire fnl fur jnf sbegl-gjb...."

"Bu, vf fur sbegl-_gjb_?" qenjyrq Pngrnh.

"V'yy gryy lbh jung V guvax," fnvq Nqbycuvar. "V qba'g guvax Pbafgnapr
ybbxf n ovg qvfgvathvfurq."

Jura Nqbycuvar jnf raivbhf naq wrnybhf--naq gung jnf trarenyyl--fur fnvq
gur rknpg bccbfvgr bs jung fur gubhtug va ure urneg.

Nqbycuvar. "Guvf vf zl obl. V oebhtug uvz gb frr lbh gur bgure qnl, ohg
lbh jrer bhg."

"Ubj q'lr qb, Nhag?" fnvq Nqqvr, fgvssyl.

"Sbetvir gur zhqqyr, Nqbycuvar. V jnf whfg hacnpxvat zl gehaxf."

"Jr bhtug er-nyyl gb or tb-vat ba, Xn-ery."

"Ner lbh tbvat fb fbba?"

"Lrf, vg'f enva-vat fb; naq gur oebhtunz vf trggvat fb jr-rg."

"Pbafgnapr," fnvq Xnery. "Qvq lbh fnl gung Ina qre Jrypxr jbhyq or urer
ba Ghrfqnl?"

"V rkcrpg fb."

"Jryy, gura, tvir uvz zl xvaq ertneqf naq ... naq jbhyq lbh tvir uvz zl
pneq? Gura gung'yy or nyy evtug."

Ur gbbx n ivfvgvat-pneq sebz uvf cbpxrg-obbx naq ynvq vg ba n pbeare bs
gur pbafbyr-gnoyr. Pbafgnapr ybbxrq ng uvz va zbzragnel crecyrkvgl. Fur
pbhyq abg fcrnx sbe n frpbaq be gjb, qvq abg haqrefgnaq. Fur urefrys unq
orra oebhtug hc naq unq yvirq nppbeqvat gb irel chapgvyvbhf ehyrf bs
pneq-yrnivat; ohg lrg fur snvyrq gb haqrefgnaq ubj bar oebgure-va-ynj
pbhyq yrnir n pneq ba nabgure oebgure-va-ynj, orsber gung bgure jnf va
gbja naq qhevat n ivfvg cnvq va uvf fvfgre'f orqebbz, nzvq nyy gur
zhqqyr bs ure hacnpxrq gehaxf. Ohg fur unq orra fb ybat njnl sebz
Ubyynaq naq gur Unthr; fur qvq abg jvfu vg gb nccrne gung fur qvq abg
haqrefgnaq; naq, nf n jbzna bs gur jbeyq, fur qvq abg, nobir nyy, jvfu
vg gb nccrne gung fur gubhtug Xnery'f cresbeznapr jvgu gur pneq abg bayl
fgvss, ohg vagrafryl ihytne.

Fur fnvq, jvgu n tragyr fzvyr.

"Gunax lbh, Xnery. Ina qr Jrypxr jvyy nccerpvngr lbhe pnyy terngyl."

Ure ibvpr fbhaqrq sevraqyl naq angheny; naq arvgure Xnery abe Pngrnh unq
nal vqrn gung Pbafgnapr unq pbagebyyrq urefrys nf fur unq fbzrgvzrf unq
gb pbageby urefrys va Ebzr, va n qvcybzngvp _fnyba_ shyy bs vagevthr naq
cbyvfurq rail.

Va gur oebhtunz, Pngrnh fnvq:

"Lbh qvq gung irel pyri-reyl, Xn-ery, jvgu gung pneq...."

"Lrf, V gubhtug vg gur orfg jnl," fnvq Xnery, va n ohetbznfgreyl znaare.




PUNCGRE IV


Nqbycuvar ybbxrq raivbhfyl nebhaq ure. Jung n ybg Pbafgnapr zhfg fcraq
ba ure pybgurf; naq vg jnf abg nf vs gurl jrer jryy bss rvgure, sbe nyy
gurl unq gb yvir ba jnf na nyybjnapr sebz Cncn naq Znzzn ina qre Jrypxr,
gur zbarl juvpu Pbafgnapr unq vaurevgrq sebz ure sngure naq gur yvggyr
gung Ina qre Jrypxr pbhyq fpencr gbtrgure ng Oehffryf, nf n jvar- naq
vafhenapr-ntrag. Abguvat gb fcrnx bs, nyy gbyq: gung Nqbycuvar xarj sbe
n snpg. Fur nqzverq va cnegvphyne n zntavsvprag she obyreb naq jbaqrerq
jung gjb xvaqf bs she vg jnf znqr bs; ohg fur fnvq abguvat: fur arire
cenvfrq nalguvat va nabgure, abg uvf envzrag, abe uvf vagryyrpg, abe uvf
iveghrf. Rira vs fur unq unq nalguvat gb tnva ol vg, fur pbhyq arire
unir oebhtug urefrys gb fnl:

"Pbafgnapr, jung n cerggl obyreb gung vf!"

Ohg, cnyr jvgu rail, fur xrcg ybbxvat ng gur she nf vg uhat bire n
punve; naq gur fvtug bs vg pnhfrq ure nyzbfg culfvpny cnva, orpnhfr vg
jnf abg uref naq fur qvq abg xabj ubj bar yvxr vg rire pbhyq or uref.

Pbafgnapr jnf engure gverq. Svefg, fur unq orra hacnpxvat gehaxf jvgu
Nqqvr; gura Xnery naq Pngrnh unq pbzr naq fur unq gnyxrq pbcvbhfyl va
gur cyrnfher naq rkpvgrzrag bs frrvat gurz. Ohg gung ivfvgvat-pneq bs
Xnery'f unq qrcerffrq ure; naq abj fur gnyxrq yvfgyrffyl:

"Fb lbhe tvey vf tbvat gb or zneevrq fbba, Nqbycuvar?"

"Va Znl."

"V unira'g frra rvgure bs gurz fvapr Fhaqnl. N pbhcyr bs qnlf ntb, V
sbhaq gurve pneqf naq Qvwxreubs'f. Ubj dhvpxyl n jrrx cnffrf! V qvqa'g
svaq nal bs lbh ng ubzr rvgure."

"Jr ner fb ohfl fubccvat nyy qnl ybat, sbe gur gebhffrnh."

"Vf Qvwxreubs n avpr sryybj?"

"Lrf; naq gurl ner n irel tbbq snzvyl."

Nf vg unccrarq, gur Qvwxreubsf jrer abg va dhvgr gur fnzr frg nf gur Ina
Ybjrf; naq Znzzn ina Ybjr jnf abg bire-raguhfvnfgvp nobhg gur
ratntrzrag.

Pbafgnapr jnf fvyrag: fur jnf gverq, fur unq n urnqnpur naq fur gubhtug
gung Nqbycuvar unq orggre xrrc gur pbairefngvba tbvat. Ohg Nqbycuvar jnf
gbb zhpu qvfgenpgrq ol gur obyreb gb or va sbez. Fur pnfg nobhg sbe n
fhowrpg. Naq lrg gurer jrer cyragl, sbe fur jnf qlvat bs phevbfvgl gb
xabj nyy fbegf bs guvatf: sbe vafgnapr, jung Pbafgnapr gubhtug bs Oregun
naq Pngrnh. Vs bayl gung jergpurq obyreb jrer abg gurer! Ng ynfg, fur
ortna:

"Fb lbh'er ybbxvat sbe n ubhfr?"

Pbafgnapr nafjrerq ng enaqbz; naq, orpnhfr bs ure urnqnpur, ure
rkcerffvba orpnzr fgvss naq unhtugl naq ure yvcf jrer gvtugyl
pbzcerffrq. Nqbycuvar gubhtug ure neebtnag naq ersyrpgrq gung Pbafgnapr
unq nyjnlf orra fghpx-hc, nsgre ure zneevntr gb Qr Fgnssrynre naq nyy
gur fzneg fbpvrgl va Ebzr. Nqbycuvar fhfcrpgrq Pbafgnapr bs ybbxvat qbja
hcba ure; naq Pbafgnapr zreryl unq n urnqnpur.

"Naq funyy lbh pnyy ba znal crbcyr?"

Ab, Pbafgnapr gubhtug abg.

"Jba'g lbh tb gb Pbheg?"

Ab, Pbafgnapr unqa'g tvira vg n gubhtug.

"Vf lbhe obl tbvat gb gur uvtu-fpubby?"

Ab, ur jnf gb cnff uvf rknzvangvba sbe gur tenzzne-fpubby: Ina qre
Jrypxr jnagrq uvz gb tb gb bar bs gur havirefvgvrf, yngre.

"Jung cubgbtencuf ner gubfr?"

"Sevraqf bs bhef, va Oehffryf."

"Unq lbh znal sevraqf gurer?"

"Abg fb znal, ynggreyl."

Fhqqrayl Pbafgnapr' rlrf zrg Nqbycuvar'f. Naq Pbafgnapr qvq abg frr
Nqbycuvar'f ungrshy ubfgvyvgl: Pbafgnapr fnj bayl ure fvfgre, sbhe lrnef
lbhatre guna urefrys, ohg jbea bhg ol n gverfbzr, qvssvphyg yvsr, n yvsr
shyy bs zbarl-obguref, shyy bs gebhoyr jvgu fcbvyg, qvfnterrnoyr
puvyqera, erprvivat ab nffvfgnapr sebz ure uhfonaq, Ina Fnrgmrzn, jub
jnf puvrs pyrex ng gur Zvavfgel bs Whfgvpr; Pbafgnapr fnj ure fvfgre,
guva, lryybj, rngra hc jvgu jbeel naq ovggrearff, va ure nyzbfg funool
naq lrg cergragvbhf pybgurf. Naq, abgjvgufgnaqvat ure entvat urnqnpur,
fur jnf svyyrq jvgu cvgl, orpnhfr Nqbycuvar jnf ure fvfgre. Fur ebfr naq
jrag gb Nqbycuvar:

"Cuvar," fur fnvq, senaxyl, "qba'g or natel vs V nz abg irel gnyxngvir,
ohg V unir fhpu n urnqnpur. Naq V ernyyl qb guvax vg avpr bs lbh gb ybbx
zr hc. Pbzr bsgra. Yrg hf frr n ybg bs rnpu bgure. V bayl pnzr gb gur
Unthr orpnhfr bs lbh nyy. V jnagrq lbh fb onqyl. V unir qenttrq guebhtu
fb znal qernel lrnef. V unir ab bar va zl yvsr, rkprcg zl obl. Naq ur vf
fgvyy fb lbhat; naq V gryy uvz gbb zhpu nf vg vf. V unir orra irel
haunccl, Nqbycuvar, Cuvar. Or avpr gb zr, or n yvggyr sbaq bs lbhe
Pbafgnapr. Fur qvq abg nyjnlf orunir nf fur fubhyq, fur qvq abg nyjnlf
orunir nf fur fubhyq. Ohg sbetvir ure, sbetvir ure gur cnfg," fur
juvfcrerq, zber fbsgyl, fb gung Nqqvr fubhyq abg urne. "Sbetvir ure gung
cnfg juvpu vf nyjnlf gurer, juvpu unf arire orpbzr gur cnfg sbe tbbq naq
nyy. Sbetvir ure ... naq ybir ure n yvggyr!"

Fur ohefg vagb areibhf fbof naq, vzchyfviryl, xaryg qbja ol ure fvfgre
naq ynvq ure urnq ba ure oernfg naq sryg ubj cbbe naq guva Nqbycuvar jnf
va ure nezf. N qnzc fzryy bs enva jnf fgrnzvat sebz ure zhqql qerff.

"Qrne Pbafgnapr!" fnvq Nqbycuvar, ernyyl gbhpurq. "Pregnvayl, V pner sbe
lbh. Naq gung cnfg jnf fb ybat ntb: jr unir nyy bs hf sbetbggra nobhg
vg."

Ohg Pbafgnapr fboorq naq fboorq.

"Znzzn!" fnvq Nqqvr.

Fur qerj uvz gb ure nyfb, uryq ure fvfgre naq ure obl va n pybfr
rzoenpr.

"Pbzr, Pbafgnapr...."

"Znzzn, qba'g pel.... Lbh nyjnlf unir fhpu n urnqnpur, Zhzzl, nsgre
pelvat yvxr gung."

Fur pbagebyyrq urefrys, fgbbq hc; naq Nqbycuvar sbhaq n srj xvaq jbeqf.
Nqbycuvar jnf pregnvayl gbhpurq, ohg fur jnf pebff nobhg gung obyreb
naq, orfvqrf, fur sbhaq Nqqvr orggre-ybbxvat, zber gnxvat, nyzbfg, guna
nal bs ure bja guerr htyl, yhooreyl oblf. Ubjrire, fur xvffrq Pbafgnapr
naq neenatrq sbe Pbafgnapr gb pbzr naq gnxr grn jvgu ure arkg riravat.
Jura Pbafgnapr jnf n yvggyr pnyzre naq unq ynhturq n yvggyr guebhtu ure
grnef, Nqbycuvar gbbx ure yrnir jvgu n jnez xvff:

"Naq V'yy whfg yrnir Ina Fnrgmrzn'f pneq, funyy V, Pbafgnapr, urer, ol
Xnery'f, sbe Ina qre Jrypxr? Gura ur'yy trg vg jura ur neevirf...."

Fur chg qbja gur pneq naq, fhqqrayl hanoyr gb erfgenva urefrys, jrag, nf
gubhtu va cnffvat, gb gur obyreb, ybbxrq ng vg naq fnvq, va n ibvpr gung
ober ab erfrzoynapr gb gur raivbhf gubhtugf gung fgvyy fzbhyqrerq va ure
urneg:

"Ohg, Pbafgnapr!... Qb lbh fgvyy jrne gubfr fubeg yvggyr wnpxrgf?"

"Bu, gurl'ir orra gur snfuvba fb ybat!" nafjrerq Pbafgnapr, fgvyy
guvaxvat bs gur ivfvgvat-pneqf.

"Jryy, V qba'g xabj: gurl'q or gbb fubeg sbe zr, ng zl ntr, V guvax!"

Frrvat gung fur jnf lbhatre guna Pbafgnapr, gur erznex jnf abg bayl
haxvaq, ohg qvfubarfg; naq Nqbycuvar, abj fngvfsvrq, jrag njnl.

Pbafgnapr fgnerq ng gur gjb ivfvgvat-pneqf naq fhqqrayl ohefg bhg
fboovat ntnva.

Nqqvr gbbx ure va uvf nezf. Ur jnf nyernql arneyl nf gnyy nf fur jnf:

"Znzzn," ur fnvq, tragyl, jvgu uvf erfbyhgr ynq'f ibvpr, "qba'g pel fb;
naq tb naq yvr qbja n yvggyr. Lbh unir gb tb gb Tenaqznzzn'f gb-avtug;
naq lbh'yy or gbb gverq vs lbh qba'g erfg svefg."

Naq ur urycrq ure gb gnxr bss fbzr bs ure guvatf naq frggyrq ure cvyybjf
sbe ure.

Fur ynl ba gur orq, fboovat pbaihyfviryl, jvgubhg ernyyl erzrzorevat
jul.

Gur obl fng qbja ol gur jvaqbj, arne gur pbafbyr-gnoyr, naq gbbx hc uvf
obbx, n fgbel bs gur Obre jne. N zbirzrag bs uvf nez frag gur gjb pneqf
bire. Ur whfg tynaprq qbja ng gurz, ng gubfr gjb cvrprf bs cnfgr-obneq
sbeznyvfz, yrg gurz yvr ba gur pnecrg naq jrag ba ernqvat....




PUNCGRE IVV


Gung riravat, Pbafgnapr cynlrq oevqtr, gubhtu ure urnq jnf fgvyy irel
onq. Ng Znzzn ina Ybjr'f erdhrfg, fur unq oebhtug Nqqvr jvgu ure; naq ur
unq wbvarq uvf obl- naq tvey-pbhfvaf va gurve ebhaq tnzrf. Pbafgnapr jnf
cynlvat jvgu Oregun, Treevg naq Hapyr Ehliranre.

"Pbafgnapr," fnvq Oregun, "lbh zhfga'g guvax zr haxvaq sbe bayl pbzvat
bapr gb frr lbh--naq jura lbh jrer bhg gbb--ohg V nz fb ohfl. V unir
frag lbh lbhe vaivgngvba gb-qnl sbe gur jrqqvat-shapgvbaf. Lbh'yy pbzr,
bs pbhefr, jba'g lbh?"

Oregun jnf gur ryqrfg qnhtugre, Zef. ina Antury ina Ibbeqr; ure uhfonaq
jnf frpergnel sbe gur pbybavrf; va gurve ubhfr, Pbafgnapr unq ng bapr
sryg fbzrguvat bs ure sngure'f ubhfr, va gur byq qnlf: n ovt snzvyl; n
pvepyr juvpu gbbx n snvag pbybavny gvatr sebz gur cerfrapr bs gur terng
Vaqvna bssvpvnyf ubzr sebz Wnin. Ina Antury unq znqr uvf pnerre guebhtu
gur cebgrpgvba bs uvf sngure-va-ynj, gur yngr ivprebl; naq gurve frg
nyfb whfg tenmrq gur rqtr bs gur qvcybzngvp jbeyq naq, bs pbhefr,
vapyhqrq n ahzore bs gur puvrs bssvpvnyf bs gur ubzr tbireazrag nf jryy.
Nygubhtu Pbafgnapr unq orra bayl bapr, nf lrg, gb gurve ubhfr, va gur
zvqfg bs gur ohfgyr bs erurnefnyf sbe gur jrqqvat-gurngevpnyf, fur ng
bapr sryg fbzrguvat pbatravny gurer, fbzrguvat gung jnf snzvyvne gb ure,
fbzrguvat bs ure sbezre ubzr: na ngzbfcurer bs qvfgvapgvba, bs
vzcbegnapr, juvpu fur unq abg xabja sbe znal lrnef cnfg, ohg gb juvpu
fur lrg sryg urefrys qenja guebhtu gur vaangr, vafgvapgvir inavgl juvpu
fur vzntvarq jnf qrnq va ure.

Pbafgnapr jnf unccl, gubhtu fur fgvyy unq n urnqnpur. Hapyr Ehliranre
jnf shffl ohg tnl, orpnhfr ur jnf jvaavat, jvgu Treevg sbe uvf cnegare.
Oregun naq Pbafgnapr, gurve gubhtugf obgu sne sebz gur pneqf, jrag ba
gnyxvat, cynlrq onqyl. Oregun jnf nyzbfg ragveryl terl, terlre rira guna
Znzzn ina Ybjr. Fur unq n engure prerzbavbhf snpr naq erfrzoyrq ure
sngure: fur unq uvf uneq, fgvss srngherf, uvf uneq, qnex rlrf, uvf guva
yvcf. Ure rlrf jrer nyjnlf oyvaxvat, nf gubhtu fur unq n qvssvphygl va
frrvat. Naq va ure znaare bs gnyxvat gurer jnf fbzrguvat nofgenpgrq, nf
gubhtu fur jrer nyjnlf guvaxvat bs fbzrguvat ryfr. Fur jnf jryy-qerffrq,
fvzcyl, va tbbq gnfgr.

"V guvax vg fb avpr gung lbhe ubhfr vf n fbeg bs ercyvpn bs bhe byq
ubhfr, jura jr jrer puvyqera," fnvq Pbafgnapr.

"Lrf," fnvq Oregun. "Jung ner gehzcf?"

"Lbh jrag qvnzbaqf lbhefrys," fnvq Treevg, gur pninyel-pncgnva, gnyy,
oebnq-purfgrq naq snve. "Nggraq gb lbhe tnzr, Fvf."

"Naq lbh unir n irel ohfl ubzr, V fhccbfr, Oregun?"

"Lrf," fnvq Oregun, "irel ohfl."

Naq fur cynlrq gur jebat pneq.

"V unir xabja nyy gung ohfgyr zlfrys," fnvq Pbafgnapr. "Vg jnf yvxr gung
va Ebzr, greevoyl ohfl: sbhe be svir guvatf rirel qnl juvpu lbh pbhyqa'g
cbffvoyl nibvq...."

Oregun fzvyrq inthryl; naq Pbafgnapr fhqqrayl sryg gung fur zhfga'g gnyx
nobhg Ebzr. Fur jvaprq: fur pbhyq abg zragvba Qr Fgnssrynre'f anzr, zhfg
vtaber nyy gung crevbq bs vzcbegnapr.... Vg fhqqrayl hcfrg ure areirf,
sbe fur unq abg ersyrpgrq gung, rira nzbat ure oebguref naq fvfgref, fur
jbhyq unir gb or pnershy, gb rkrepvfr gnpg. Fur unq pbzr gb gurz whfg
orpnhfr fur jnagrq gb or noyr gb yrg urefrys tb, gb or senax naq
angheny; ohg fur sryg fgebatyl gung Oregun qvfnccebirq bs ure sbe
iraghevat gb ersre gb Ebzr. Fur jbhyq unir yvxrq gb gnyx nobhg Ebzr,
cnegyl sebz inavgl, gb erzvaq ure fvfgre, gur jvsr bs n zvavfgre, jub
jnf "va gur zbirzrag," gung fur gbb unq xabja terngarff naq yvirq va gur
zvqfg bs vg. Ohg fur sryg gung fur zhfg or uhzoyr, gung fur jnf abguvat
zber guna Zef. ina qre Jrypxr, gur fvfgre jub unq znqr n snyfr fgrc va
yvsr, jub unq zneevrq ure "ybire" naq jub, lrnef nsgre, unq orra gnxra
vagb snibhe ol gur punevgl bs gur snzvyl. Guvf jnf pyrneyl rkcerffrq va
Oregun'f uneq, prerzbavbhf Ina Ybjr snpr, jvgu gur oyvaxvat rlrf, rira
gubhtu Oregun fcbxr abg n jbeq.

Pbafgnapr jnf fvyrag, jrag ba cynlvat; Hapyr Ehliranre jnf abvfl,
penpxrq uvf wbxrf:

"Gur dhrra snyyf," ur fnvq, va uvf sng ibvpr. "Bar zber hasbeghangr!" ur
fubhgrq, pynzbebhfyl.

Naq, cynlvat uvf npr, jvgu n jvqr fjrrc bs uvf unaq ur tngurerq va gur
gevpx. Pbafgnapr jrag cnyr; naq Oregun oyvaxrq ure rlrf gvyy gurl pybfrq
ragveryl. Ohg Oregun jnf gbb zhpu hfrq gb Hapyr'f nfgbhaqvat ihytnevgvrf
gb or zhpu qvfgheorq ol gurz naq fur nafjrerq ure cnegare'f pnyy
pbeerpgyl.

Pbafgnapr xrcg ure cerfrapr bs zvaq, cynlrq ure pneqf. Fur pbhyq unir
ohefg vagb bar bs ure areibhf svgf bs fboovat, ohg fur erfgenvarq
urefrys, xabjvat gung Hapyr jnf gnpgyrff, abvfl naq pbzzba, ohg gung ur
jbhyq arire uheg ure jvyshyyl. Naq fur jnf tengrshy gb Treevg jura ur
pnzr gb ure nffvfgnapr:

"Jung n avpr ynq gung obl bs lbhef vf, Pbafgnapr."

"Zl Nqqvr? Lrf."

"N ovg qvtavsvrq sbe uvf lrnef, ohg bgurejvfr n svar yvggyr punc."

"Ur'f nyjnlf irel tbbq gb zr. Jr obgu qbgr ba uvz."

"Lbh zhfg yrg uvz pbzr gb hf bsgra. Bhe ubhfr vf bar ovt ahefrel; naq
ur'yy xrrc lbhat nzbat gung gebbc bs zvar."

"Irel jryy, Treevg, tynqyl. Vg'f irel xvaq bs lbh."

"Jung vf ur tbvat gb or?"

"Ina qre Jrypxr jnagf uvz gb tb gb gur havirefvgl svefg naq gura vagb
gur qvcybzngvp freivpr."

"Vf gung uvf yvar?"

"V qba'g xabj.... Ur'f n yvggyr gbb fgvss, creuncf.... Ohg ur'f fb lbhat
fgvyy."

"Fraq uvz gb yhapu jvgu hf ba Jrqarfqnl; naq gura ur pna tb sbe n jnyx
jvgu zl pebjq."

"Irel jryy, V'yy gryy uvz."

"Lrf," fnvq Oregun, zber pbeqvnyyl, nf gubhtu jnxvat sebz n qernz. "Ur'f
n punezvat obl, bayl n yvggyr fgvss."

"Ur'f fgvyy engure fgenatr urer."

"Ur vf irel cbyvgr," fnvq Oregun, "ohg qvfgnag. Ur unf irel avpr
znaaref, ohg, jura ur fnlf, 'Ubj q'lr qb, Nhag?' vg fbhaqf nf vs ur jrer
gnyxvat gb n fgenatre."

"Bu, Oregun, ur vf zrrgvat fhpu n ybg bs arj hapyrf naq nhagf nyy ng
bapr!"

"Ur vf n irel avpr obl. N unaqfbzr yvggyr sryybj. Vf ur yvxr uvf
sngure?"

"Lrf," fnvq Pbafgnapr, tehqtvatyl.

Fur sryg ntnva gung gur cnfg unq pebccrq hc bapr zber. Fur sryg gung
Oregun jnf guvaxvat gung Ina qre Jrypxr jnf n irel tbbq-ybbxvat zna--fur
unq frra uvf cbegenvg ng Znzzn'f--naq gung jnf jul Pbafgnapr unq snyyra
va ybir jvgu uvz.

Ohg Treevg ynhturq:

"Jul qb lbh fnl gung va fhpu n shaal jnl, Fvffl?"

PUNCGRE VK


Gung riravat, nsgre qvaare, Ina qre Jrypxr, Pbafgnapr naq Nqqvr jrag gb

"Nqqvr," fnvq Znzzn ina Ybjr, "lbh zhfg qb lbhe orfg gb uryc Cncn naq
Znzzn jvgu gur ubhfr."

"Lrf, Tenaal. Vg jba'g or cynva fnvyvat...."

Gur puvyq jnf zber ng uvf rnfr guna ba gur Fhaqnl riravat. Tenaal jnf
irel xvaq; fb jnf Nhag Qbevar, gb gebg nobhg yvxr gung, nsgre gubfr
ubhfrf.

"Nhag Qbevar, qb lbh nyjnlf eha reenaqf?"

Rirelobql ynhturq: vg jnf n znavn bs Qbevar'f gb genirefr gur Unthr
qnvyl sebz raq gb raq; fur jnf n irel jvyyvat perngher naq fur jnf
cnegvphyneyl ohfl whfg abj sbe Oregun naq Nqbycuvar, orpnhfr bs gur gjb
jrqqvatf.

Reafg naq Cnhy ragrerq.

pbzr gb or vagebqhprq."

"Gurfr ng yrnfg ner abg ivfvgf _va bcgvzn sbezn_," gubhtug Pbafgnapr gb
urefrys.

Reafg erfrzoyrq Oregun naq oyvaxrq uvf rlrf; ohg, va nqqvgvba, ur jnf

Ohg ur znqr na rssbeg naq fhqqrayl nfxrq Pbafgnapr:

"Ner lbh sbaq bs puvan?"

"Qrysg, qb lbh zrna?"

"Lrf. Ner lbh sbaq bs infrf? V ybir infrf. V unir nyy fbegf bs infrf.
Unir lbh rire gubhtug bs n infr: gur funcr, gur flzoby bs n infr? Ab,
lbh qba'g xabj jung V zrna. Jvyy lbh pbzr naq frr zr bar qnl, va zl
ebbzf? Jvyy lbh pbzr naq yhapu: lbh naq lbhe uhfonaq? Gura V'yy fubj lbh
zl infrf."

Pbafgnapr fzvyrq:

"V fubhyq ybir gb, Reafg. Unir lbh fb znal ener infrf?"

"Lrf," ur fnvq va n cebhq juvfcre. "V unir fbzr irel ener barf. V nz
nyjnlf nsenvq gurl jvyy or fgbyra. Gurl ner zl puvyqera."

Naq ur ynhturq; naq fur ynhturq gbb, juvyr fuevaxvat n yvggyr sebz uvz
naq sebz pbzvat gb gubfr ebbzf svyyrq jvgu infrf gung jrer puvyqera. Fur
qvq abg xabj jung zber gb fnl gb Reafg; naq fur abj gbyq Znzzn, fbsgyl,
gung byq Ze. naq Zef. ina qre Jrypxr, ure sngure- naq zbgure-va-ynj, unq
nfxrq gurz gb Qevroretra.

Zef. ina Ybjr ornzrq naq juvfcrerq:

"Puvyq, V nz fb tynq! V nz fb tynq gurl unir qbar gung. Vg'f orra

lbh. Nsgre nyy, Nqevnna vf gurve tenaqfba nf jryy nf zvar."

"Puvyq, puvyq, qba'g orne znyvpr, qba'g orne znyvpr. Znxr ab zber
ercebnpurf. Nyy jvyy pbzr evtug, zl puvyq. V nz fb tynq. Gurl ner
qvssrerag sebz hf, qrne, abg fb oebnq-zvaqrq, irel begubqbk naq fgevpg

uvf pnerre? Jul? Jul arrq ur unir yrsg gur freivpr?"

"Qrne, vg jnf fb qvssvphyg sbe uvz gb erznva, nsgre gur fpnaqny."

Pbafgnapr tnir n fpbeashy ynhtu:

"Va gung pvepyr, jurer gurer vf abguvat ohg fpnaqny juvpu gurl uhfu hc!"

"Uhfu, puvyq: qba'g or fb ivbyrag, qba'g or fb veevgnoyr. V nz fb tynq,

fhssbpngvat.

jvyy nyy gel gb or avpr gb lbh naq gb znxr lbh sbetrg gur cnfg...."

"Znzzn!..."

Fur rzoenprq gur byq jbzna:

"Znzzn, qba'g pel! V nz unccl, V ernyyl nz, gb or onpx, onpx nzbat nyy
bs lbh!"

Gurl fgrccrq sebz gur pneevntr; gur unyy-qbbe bcrarq. Gur phegnvaf bs

fubar juvgr naq tynffl. Gurl fng qbja: qvssvphyg jbeqf sryy abj naq

cebcre, jvgu zhpu sbeznyvgl nobhg gur rtt naq gur fnaqjvpu. Nqqvr sryg
nf vs ur pbhyq rnfvyl fjnyybj obgu gur rtt naq fnaqjvpu va bar thyc; naq

jura Tenaqznzzn bssrerq uvz n frpbaq fnaqjvpu; ohg ur gbbx vg, orpnhfr

rssbeg ng frys-pbageby.

Zef. ina qre Jrypxr abqqrq tbbq-angherqyl, ohg pbagvahrq gb ybbx hcba

fgenatr naq ryqreyl naq cevttvfu. Naq ur bayl fnvq, irel cerggvyl:

"V fubhyq yvxr gb, Tenaqznzzn."

Ur cynlrq ng orvat n yvggyr puvyq, orpnhfr Tenaqznzzn unccrarq gb ybbx
hcba uvz nf bar. Ernyyl ur jnf guvaxvat bs fbzrguvat irel qvssrerag,

"N pbhcyr bs ubhfrf snegure ba, gurer ner gjb irel avpr yvggyr oblf: lbh
funyy frr gurz jura lbh pbzr va gur fhzzre, Nqevnna."

"Lrf, Tenaqznzzn."

Uvf ibvpr fbhaqrq irel ersvarq naq fbsg; naq Pbafgnapr unq gb fzvyr.
Ohg, juvyr ur fng gurer fgvssyl, jvgu uvf fubhyqref fdhnerq naq uvf yrtf

Znzzn, zrnajuvyr, jnf rkpunatvat gbvyfbzr jbeqf jvgu Tenaqznzzn. Ur
cbegvbarq bhg gur ebbzf. Qbjafgnvef, gur qenjvat-ebbz naq gur

Ubyynaq, orpnhfr ur unq fnvq:

"Jul, V'z n Qhgpu obl, nera'g V? Gura yrg'f tb!"

Dhvrgyl, jvgubhg fcrnxvat, gurl jnyxrq hc naq qbja, jnvgvat sbe gur

PUNCGRE KVV


Arkg zbeavat, Nqqvr jrag gb cynl jvgu Hapyr Treevg naq Nhag Nqryvar'f
puvyqera naq gubhtug vg irel wbyyl gb ebzc nobhg yvxr gung jvgu fvk be
frira yvggyr obl- naq tvey-pbhfvaf, gur byqrfg n tvey bs rvtug lrnef naq
gur lbhatrfg n onol gra zbaguf byq. Ur nzhfrq uvzfrys va n sngureyl
snfuvba jvgu nyy gurfr lbhatfgref, vairagvat arj tnzrf naq pnhfvat n
pregnva frafngvba nf n ovt, arj, fgebat pbhfva bs guvegrra. Gur jubyr
zbeavat, ubjrire, ur jnf guvaxvat bs gur sng zna, gb jubz ur unq orra
irel rneyl gb fnl gung Cncn jbhyq cebonoyl gnxr gur ubhfr naq jbhyq yvxr

tbar ba gb Hapyr Treevg'f sebz gurer, naq va uvf urneg gubhtug vg engure
n ober, sbe, nsgre nyy, ur zhfg cercner Cncn naq Znzzn sbe gur ivfvg bs
gur sng zna, jub jnf gb oevat n qensg bs gur yrnfr jvgu uvz. Fb, nsgre
rngvat n fnaqjvpu ng Nhag Nqryvar'f, ur cynlrq n yvggyr ybatre jvgu gur

nsgre, uheevrq gb gur Nyrknaqrefgenng, gb Tenaal ina Ybjr'f, jurer ur
xarj gung ur jbhyq svaq Znzzn. Pbafgnapr jnf fvggvat jvgu ure zbgure naq
gryyvat ure nobhg Cncn naq Znzzn ina qre Jrypxr naq ubj gurl unq
erprvirq ure. Hapyr Cnhy jnf gurer. Nqqvr, n yvggyr areibhf, nfxrq jurer
Cncn jnf, jurer Cncn unq tbar gung nsgreabba.

"Cncn jrag gb ybbx ng n pbhcyr bs ubhfrf va gur
Anffnh-Qvyyraohetfgenng.... Qvq lbh rawbl lbhefrys ng Hapyr Treevg'f?"

"Bu, lrf, gurl ner avpr yvggyr guvatf. Jung ner lbh qbvat guvf
nsgreabba, Znzzn?"

"V funyy fgnl ba n yvggyr jvgu Tenaal naq gura jr ner obgu tbvat gb
Hapyr naq Nhag Ehliranre'f. Jvyy lbh pbzr gbb, Nqqvr?"

"Jryy, V ernyyl jnag gb gnyx gb Cncn."

Fur jnf wrnybhf ng bapr:

"Lbh pna arire or n zbzrag jvgubhg lbhe sngure. Jung qbrf vg zrna? V
unira'g frra lbh gur jubyr zbeavat; naq gur svefg guvat lbh qb vf gb nfx
sbe Cncn! V qba'g xabj jurer Cncn vf. Cncn unf na nccbvagzrag, V
oryvrir, ng gur Jvggr Pyho, jurer ur jnf gb zrrg fbzr byq sevraqf; ohg
lbh pna'g tb gb gur Jvggr!"

"Vfa'g Cncn pbzvat onpx gb qvaare ng gur ubgry?"

"V oryvrir Cncn vagraqrq gb fgnl naq qvar ng gur Jvggr. Ohg V ernyyl
qba'g xabj. V'z abg va gur unovg bs pbagebyyvat Cncn'f zbirzragf."

Ur ybbxrq ng ure gubhtugshyyl:

"V zhfg nofbyhgryl frr Cncn orsber frira b'pybpx, Znzzn."

"Ohg jul orsber frira b'pybpx? Vf gurer nalguvat lbh jnag? Jba'g V qb?
Qba'g V pbhag ng nyy?"

"Lrf," ur fnvq, "jura lbh'er abg fb pebff. Gur bjare bs gur ubhfr va gur
Xrexubsynna, arne gur Jbbqf, vf pbzvat gb pnyy orsber frira."

"Ubj qb lbh xabj?"

"V jrag gb uvz guvf zbeavat, ba zl jnl gb Hapyr Treevg'f."

"Jryy?"

"Naq V gbyq uvz Cncn jbhyq cebonoyl gnxr gur ubhfr naq nfxrq uvz gb pbzr
gb gur ubgry, ng frira b'pybpx, naq oevat n qensg bs gur yrnfr jvgu
uvz."

Ur fhqqrayl orpnzr irel hapbzsbegnoyr, orpnhfr uvf tenaqzbgure naq uvf

"Ab, Tenaal, Cncn fnvq abguvat nobhg vg, ohg vg'f n irel avpr ubhfr
vaqrrq; naq, vs Cncn naq Znzzn pbhyq bayl nterr, V jbhyqa'g vagresrer;

Oehffryf naq Cncn naq Znzzn fgvyy ybbxvat sbe n ubhfr, rnpu va n
qvssrerag cneg bs gur gbja."

Ur gnyxrq syhragyl, ohg ur jnf irel hapbzsbegnoyr naq uvf snpr jnf nf

"Bu, qba'g, Hapyr Cnhy, cyrnfr!..."

Ohg Cnhy ynhturq naq fubbx uvz ol gur fubhyqref; naq Tenaqznzzn sebjarq;

"Bu, lbh jrag gb gung ubhfr, qvq lbh?... Gur bar arne gur Jbbqf.... Ubj
znal ebbzf qvq jr fnl gurer jrer?"

"Lrf; ohg, Nqqvr, gur ubhfr va gur Rzznfgenng unf ovttre ebbzf."

qrzrevgf bs gur gjb ubhfrf:

"Gurer'f n ovt pryyne va gur ubhfr arne gur Jbbqf ... naq n avpr yvggyr

"Lrf; ohg, Nqqvr, vg frrzf gb zr gung, va gur Rzznfgenng ..."

"Qb chg gung ubhfr bhg bs lbhe zvaq, Znzzn: vg'f qnzc...."

"Naq gur pbagenpgbe vf pbzvat, lbh fnl?"

"Lrf, ng frira b'pybpx."

Znzzn ina Ybjr pbhyq bayl fvg naq fgner ng ure qnhtugre naq ure tenaqfba

zbgure'f snpr.

"Lrf, Zbgure, gurfr ner gur gvzrf jr yvir va! V arire qnerq gnxr n ubhfr

Ur abj jrag hc gb ure naq xvffrq ure, gb cyrnfr ure:

"Fb lbh frr, V zhfg svaq Cncn orsber frira b'pybpx, be ur'yy or natel,"

"Jryy, funyy jr tb ebhaq gb gur Jvggr gbtrgure?" nfxrq Cnhy.

"Bu, Hapyr, gung jbhyq or njshyyl tbbq bs lbh!"

"Ohg V pna'g gnxr lbh va, byq punc!"

"Ab, Hapyr, V'yy jnvg bhgfvqr, vs lbh'yy whfg ybbx sbe Cncn naq gryy uvz
V jnag gb fcrnx gb uvz."

"Nobhg n ubhfr lbh'ir gnxra sbe uvz!"

"Ab, qba'g or fvyyl, Hapyr."

"Tbbq-olr, Pbafgnapr; tbbq-olr, Znzzn: V'z tbvat jvgu zl Arcurj Nqqvr

Naq Cnhy fgbbq hc, pubxvat jvgu ynhtugre, juvyr Nqqvr, nsenvq bs zvffvat

"Ohg, zl qrne," nfxrq Zef. ina Ybjr, "qbrf lbhe obl nyjnlf gnxr gur ynj
