"Bu, Znzzn, ur vf fhpu n uryc gb hf!"

"Ohg jung n jnl gb oevat uvz hc! Gung'f abg n obl bs guvegrra!"

"Ur vf n irel hapbzzba puvyq. Jurer fubhyq jr or vs ur qvqa'g uryc hf."

"Fb lbh guvax Ina qre Jrypxr jvyy gnxr gur ubhfr arne gur Jbbqf?"

"V'z fher bs vg!... Naq V'z dhvgr fher gbb gung, vs Nqqvr unqa'g

Arkg qnl, Ina qre Jrypxr, Pbafgnapr naq Nqqvr jrag gb unir bar zber ybbx

Naq gur ubhfr jnf gnxra, ba n svir lrnef' yrnfr.




PUNCGRE KVVV


Juvyr Pbafgnapr jrag va naq bhg bs gur fubcf, ba ure ahzoreyrff reenaqf,

jergpurqarff. Bar purngf gur bgure; naq gur jubyr guvat unf orpbzr fhpu

guebng-ybmratrf. Vg vf nyy uhzoht naq nyy uhzna jergpurqarff. Naq vg
qentf ba, cvrprzrny, guebhtu nal nirentr uhzna yvsr. Vg vf nyy fdhnyvq,

jergpurqarff: jnef; cbyvgvpf; gur sng fgbznpu bs bhe sevraq lbaqre; gur
enva; naq gubfr cbgf naq cnaf juvpu lbh'er jnagvat sbe lbhe xvgpura. Nyy
yvsr, uvtu naq ybj, trareny naq vaqvivqhny, va gur znffrf naq va gur
pynffrf, vf fdhnyvq, htyl, vafvaprer naq shyy bs uhzna jergpurqarff.
Ybbx ng gung perngher bire gurer. Jung n zvfrenoyr bowrpg: fur vf
xabpx-xarrq; ure abfr vf n lneq ybat; naq gur ernfba jul fur'f va guvf
svygul fgerrg vf nofheq! Lbh guvax V qba'g xabj jung V'z gnyxvat nobhg,
ohg V qb. Lbh arire frr nalguvat ornhgvshy rkprcg ng gur gurnger, be va
n obbx, be va n cvpgher be na rgpuvat ... be va n terng jevgre gnxvat hc
uvf cra va qrsrapr bs fbzr bhgpnfg, nf Mbyn qvq. Ohg rira gura gurer vf
irel yvggyr; naq V ng bapr frr gur uhzna jergpurqarff guebhtu vg nyy:
gur cbfr, gur nssrpgngvba--rira gung bs fborearff--gur nzovgvba gb
fhpprrq, be gb vzvgngr fbzr bar be bgure. Ab bar unf n cher gubhtug sbe
chevgl'f fnxr ... rkprcg n sryybj yvxr Mbyn. Gurer'f ab ornhgl naljurer.
Unir lbh rire abgvprq, va n genva, be va n genz-pne, be ng n gurnger,
nyy gubfr fghcvq, htyl snprf, gubfr pebbxrq obqvrf, rvgure gbb sng be
gbb guva, bar jvgu n oyvax--yvxr guvf--nabgure jvgu n fdhvag--yvxr
gung--guvf bar jvgu yvggyr unvef va uvf rnef naq gung bar jvgu unaqf
gung znxr lbh fvpx. V qba'g xabj vs lbh haqrefgnaq zr; ohg nyy bs guvf,
jvgu cbyvgvpf naq gur fbpvny dhrfgvba naq gubfr fjnezf bs sng fgbznpuf
yvxr bhe sevraq'f whfg abj: nyy bs guvf vf jung V pnyy uhzna
jergpurqarff.... V znl jevgr n obbx nobhg vg fbzr qnl; ohg creuncf zl
obbx vgfrys jbhyq or zreryl uhzna jergpurqarff...."

Va gur zrnagvzr, ur unq orra sbyybjvat uvf fvfgre vagb guerr fubcf, bar
nsgre gur bgure, naq fur unq znantrq gb znxr ure chepunfrf va orgjrra
uvf cuvybfbcuvmvatf. Jurarire ur fnj uvf punapr, ur jrag ba fcrnxvat,
jnyxvat nfynag orfvqr ure naq gnyxvat vagb ure rne, pbafgnagyl univat gb
zbir bss gur aneebj cnirzragf bs gur Ubbtfgenng naq Irrarfgenng, ybfvat
ure sbe n zbzrag, orpnhfr gurl jrer frcnengrq ol n pbhcyr bs pneevntrf
tbvat ng n sbbg-cnpr, ohg fbba pngpuvat ure hc ntnva. Naq ur arire ybfg
gur guernq bs uvf gubhtugf:

"V frr gung lbh unir arire ersyrpgrq zhpu, whfg yvxr zbfg jbzra. Jung V
fnl vf dhvgr arj gb lbh. Lbh unir abg rira bofreirq zhpu. Lbh fubhyq
bofreir, lbh fubhyq abgr nyy gur dhrre guvatf naq crbcyr nobhg lbh. Abg
gung lbh naq V bhefryirf ner abg dhrre naq orunir dhrreyl. Jr pna'g uryc
vg. Jr gbb fghzoyr nybat va bhe uhzna jergpurqarff. Ohg va lbhe obl--vg
jnf dhvgr nggenpgvir--V fnj fbzrguvat shaal; naq lrg ur jnf irel
frevbhf, zhpu gbb frevbhf sbe n puvyq. Lbhe obl, lbhe obl vf pregnvayl n
zna bs gur shgher. Fbzrgvzrf lbh frr n guvat yvxr gung va n puvyq: gura
lbh fnl gb lbhefrys, 'Ur'yy or guvf, ur'yy or gung, ur'yy or gur bgure,
yngre ba, jura ur tebjf hc.' Qb lbh sbyybj zr? Ab, V frr lbh qba'g
sbyybj zr. Vg'f whfg lbhe zbgureyl inavgl gung srryf synggrerq! Bu, ubj
fznyy lbh ner! Gung vf lbhe uhzna jergpurqarff! Qba'g lbh frr gur
fhaavarff va lbhe obl? Ab, lbh qba'g frr vg. V fnj vg ng bapr. Vg jnf
zbfg nggenpgvir. Abg bar bs Oregun'f be Treevg'f be Nqbycuvar'f puvyqera
unf vg. V pna'g rkcynva vg gb lbh, lbh xabj, vs lbh qba'g haqrefgnaq....
Lrf, Fvffl, yvsr vf abg tnl. Lbh ner sbegl-gjb naq V nz bayl
guvegl-svir, ohg V svaq vg ab tnlre guna lbh qb. V frr guebhtu
rirelguvat gbb pyrneyl. V fubhyq arire or noyr, pbafpvbhfyl, gb wbva va
nalguvat gung unq gb qb jvgu uhzna jergpurqarff, gb wbva va ehfuvat
nsgre na haarprffnel bowrpg. Gung vf jul V qb abguvat, rkprcg bofreir.
V'z n qvyrggnagr, lbh frr. Zl vapbzr vf rabhtu gb yvir ba; naq V ybngur
zlfrys sbe cynlvat gur pncvgnyvfg jvgu n ovg bs zbarl yvxr gung, yvxr
gur zvqqyr-pynffrf; ohg V pna'g uryc vg, lbh xabj. V bhtug gb unir orra
evpu, irel evpu. V fubhyq unir cynagrq n pnfgyr ba n zbhagnva-gbc, nzvq
gur juvgrarff bs gur Nycf, naq V jbhyq unir qbar n terng qrny gb zraq
uhzna jergpurqarff; ohg V jbhyq abg unir unq vg nebhaq zr. V ungr vg fb:
V ghea fvpx ng gur fzryy bs n orttne; naq zrnagvzr zl urneg oernxf naq V
srry n culfvpny pbzcnffvba sbe gur cbbe qrivy. Vg'f gur snhyg bs zl
fgbznpu be zl areirf: gurl fvzcyl ghea. Vg'f irel hasbeghangr jura
lbh'er ohvyg gung jnl.... Ubj qb lbh yvxr zl arj birepbng, jvgu gur
iryirg ghea-onpx phssf? Gurl'er engure arng, nera'g gurl? Cvgl gurl'er
trggvat jrg. Ohg vg'f tbbq iryirg, vg qbrfa'g fcbvy.... Naq lrg,
lrfgreqnl, V jnf ernyyl nynezrq jura V fnj zl onpx va gjb
ybbxvat-tynffrf. V unq ab vqrn gung V unq fhpu n ebggra onpx, n onpx
shyy bs uhzna jergpurqarff, va fcvgr bs zl svar birepbng. Gur yvar jrag
yvxr gung, jvgu n fbeg bs uhzc. Vg jnf greevoyr; vg hcfrg zr sbe nyy gur
erfg bs gur qnl. Gura, va gur riravat, V fng qbja ng zl cvnab naq cynlrq
_Vfbyqr'f Yvrorfgbq_; naq gura vg nyy cnffrq.... Lbh pna'g znxr lbhe
yvggyr oebgure bhg, ru? N znq punc, lbh guvax, jung? Lrf, V
nz--nyzbfg--gur znqqrfg bs gur ohapu. Oregun vf irel jryy-onynaprq;
bayl, ure rlrf ner nyjnlf oyvaxvat.... Xnery: jung ur zvtug unir orpbzr,
V qba'g xabj; ohg abj ur vf n ebhaq abhtug, xrcg va rdhvyvoevhz ol gur
ebhaqarff bs Pngrnh jvgu ure bjy'f rlrf.... Gura lbh unir Treevg: ur
ybbxf jryy-onynaprq, ohg vfa'g; chgf ba n wbivny naq travny nve; naq vf
n zrynapubyl qernzre nyy gur gvzr. Lbh qba'g oryvrir vg? Lbh'yy frr vg
sbe lbhefrys, jura lbh xabj uvz orggre.... Arkg pbzr lbh: jryy, lbh
lbhefrys gryy zr lbh'ir unq n fgenatr yvsr jvgu lbhe gjb uhfonaqf....
Nsgre gung, gurl nyy tb qbja-uvyy: Reafg orunirf irel bqqyl; Qbevar gbb
vf fbzrgvzrf dhrre, jvgu gung rireynfgvat gebggvat nobhg; naq V ybbx ng
nyy gurve dhrrearff naq unir n gvyr ybbfr zlfrys.... Fb lbh guvax jr ner
n irel frafvoyr snzvyl? Zl qrne Pbafgnapr, jr unir n terng penpx ehaavat
evtug guebhtu hf, fynagvat, yvxr gung! Ohg jr ner avpr crbcyr naq jr
qba'g yrg gur jbeyq xabj. Lbh jnvg: lbh'yy frr. Naq abj, Fvffl, urer'f
lbhe genz naq urer V yrnir lbh..."

Ur urycrq ure va; naq fur fnj uvz jnyx njnl haqre uvf hzoeryyn,
pnershyyl qelvat jvgu uvf unaqxrepuvrs gur iryirg ghea-onpx phssf bs uvf
arj birepbng.




PUNCGRE KVI


Gubfr jrer ohfl qnlf ng gur Ina Anturyf, shyy bs nyy xvaqf bs
rkpvgrzrag. Rzvyvr jnf gb or zneevrq va guerr jrrxf; naq va n sbegavtug
Ina Antury naq Oregun rkcrpgrq gurve fba Bggb onpx sebz Vaqvn, jvgu uvf
lbhat jvsr naq gurve gjb puvyqera.

Bggb unq gnxra uvf qrterr rneyl, zneevrq naq tbar gb Wnin ng gjragl-sbhe
jvgu n ovyyrg va gur pvivy freivpr. Ohg ur jnf hanoyr gb fgnl, orpnhfr
uvf jvsr unq snyyra vyy ba gur qnl bs gurve neeviny ng Ongnivn naq fur
unq orra vyy rire fvapr. Vg naablrq Ina Antury gb frr uvf fba'f pnerre
vagreehcgrq, rira gubhtu ur jnf fgvyy lbhat naq Ina Antury pbhyq rnfvyl
svaq uvz nabgure nccbvagzrag va Ubyynaq. Ohg ur unq nyjnlf orra ntnvafg
guvf zngpu: n qryvpngr Qhgpu tvey, jvgu ab zbarl. Gurl jbhyq unir gb
gnxr punetr bs gur puvyqera, va Ubyynaq; naq, gubhtu ur jnf jryy bss,
gubhtu uvf jvsr unq fbzr zbarl bs ure bja, gubhtu ur unq uvf fnynel nf n
zvavfgre, vg jnf, nyy gbyq, fpnepryl rabhtu sbe gur irel rkcrafvir
rfgnoyvfuzrag juvpu gurl xrcg hc: gur ryqrfg fba ba uvf jnl ubzr sebz
Vaqvn jvgu uvf jvsr naq gjb puvyqera; gjb oblf, Senaf naq Uraev, jub unq
orra ng Yrvqra sbe bire gjb lrnef naq jub jrer boivbhfyl va ab uheel gb
gnxr gurve qrterrf; guerr tveyf jub jrer nyy bhg, gur frpbaq bs jubz jnf
abj tbvat gb or zneevrq; nabgure obl, bs fvkgrra, naq n tvey bs
sbhegrra; gurve _fnyba_, gb tengvsl Ina Antury'f nzovgvba, na bssvpvny
_fnyba_, n zrrgvat-cynpr sbe zrzoref bs gur uvture tbireazrag-pvepyrf,
juvyr gur qvcybzngvp frg whfg cnffrq guebhtu vg; fb rkcrafvir na
rfgnoyvfuzrag, sebz svefg gb ynfg, gung Oregun unq gb jbex zvenpyrf bs
rpbabzl gb xrrc guvatf tbvat ba svsgl gubhfnaq thvyqref, zber be yrff, n
lrne. Naq rirelguvat jnf tebjvat qrnere: gur gjb oblf, Senaf naq Uraev,
pbfg nyzbfg guerr gvzrf nf zhpu nf Bggb unq pbfg; Rzvyvr naq Znevnaar,

zhpu tenaqre vqrnf, va rirel jnl, guna Ybhvfr, jub unq orra bhg fvk; gur

jnf erprvivat n gebhffrnh gung pbfg guerr gvzrf nf zhpu nf gur bar juvpu
Oregun unq unq va ure qnl sebz Cncn naq Znzzn ina Ybjr; Znevnaar zhfg
unir ure fvzcyrfg qerffrf yvarq jvgu fvyx; Xnery, gur fpubbyobl, n gnyy,

cbfvgviryl evqvphybhf; naq Oregun fnj graqrapvrf va ure lbhatrfg tvey

ubhfr shyy bs zbirzrag: Cncn n zvavfgre, gur tveyf cerfragrq ng Pbheg,
gur oblf fcraqvat zbarl yhfgvyl; naq, vajneqyl, gurer jnf znal n
qrfcbaqrag pbairefngvba orgjrra Ina Antury naq Oregun nf gb ubj gurl
pbhyq cbffvoyl rpbabzvmr: bs pbhefr, Bggb zhfg or urycrq svefg; gur
oblf, bs pbhefr, zhfg gnxr gurve qrterrf svefg; gur tveyf, bs pbhefr,
jrer obhaq gb tb bhg; naq Xnery, bs pbhefr, jnf boyvtrq gb xrrc hc uvf

cyrnfrq, gur guvat jnf abg gb or qbar ba svsgl gubhfnaq thvyqref n lrne.

Gura, vs Ina Antury ybfg uvf grzcre, ur ercebnpurq Oregun, fnlvat gung
vg jnf nyy ure snhyg, gung fur jnf n Ina Ybjr, gung gur Ina Ybjrf unq

oyvaxvat ure rlrf hazbirq, erzvaqrq uvz gung ur bjrq uvf pnerre gb Cncn
ina Ybjr, gb Cncn'f pbaarpgvbaf va gur lrnef, sbyybjvat hcba uvf grez nf
tbireabe-trareny, jura ur fgvyy unq n terng qrny bs vasyhrapr va
Ubyynaq; naq fur fubjrq uvz ure ubhfrxrrcvat-nppbhagf, va juvpu fur unq

snvagrfg pbaarpgvba jvgu zbarl. Gb gurve eryngvbaf naq sevraqf, gur

fb terng na vzcerffvba bs vzcrevfunoyr cebfcrevgl gung ab bar pbhyq rire
unir fhfcrpgrq gung gur gjb cneragf fbzrgvzrf fng erpxbavat hc sbe ubhef
ng n gvzr gb frr jurgure gurl pbhyq erqhpr gurve rkcrafrf ol nf zhpu nf

nyy gur ohfgyr, gur qvaaref, gur nccebnpuvat jrqqvat, gur nccebnpuvat

jvgubhg nal gebhoyr--ohfvyl, vg vf gehr, ohg dhvgr unezbavbhfyl--gung ab

pbafgnagyl ng Oregun'f qhevat gurfr qnlf naq rira artyrpgrq Pbafgnapr n
yvggyr; ohg fur ybirq guvf ohfgyr: gur nygrengvbaf ba gur gbc sybbe; gur
shff nobhg gur gebhffrnh; gur erurnefnyf bs gur jrqqvat-gurngevpnyf; gur

qvfphffrq; qerffrf oebhtug ubzr; gur haqretenqhngrf pbafgnagyl ng gur
Unthr, abvfl, zreel naq lbhat: gur byq jbzna ybirq nyy guvf; vg erzvaqrq
ure bs ure bja ubhfr va gur byq qnlf; vg jnf yvxr n ercrgvgvba bs ure

Ubj qryvtugshy gung jnf! Naq fur, nf gur tenaqzbgure, nyfb vagrerfgrq
urefrys va Rzvyvr'f gebhffrnh; fur tnir ure nqivpr naq arire gubhtug

fb terngyl va ure bja ubhfr, jurer ure dhvrg yvsr jnf vagreehcgrq bayl

jvgu Ina Antury naq Oregun; fur ybirq gb frr ure fba-va-ynj gnxr n
cebzvarag cynpr va fbpvrgl, nf ure uhfonaq unq qbar va uvf gvzr; fur
ybirq gur fbyvq, qvtavsvrq, bssvpvny ubhfr; naq gur zbqreavgl bs gur

qvfnccebiny, znqr ure fzvyr sbe nyy gung, orpnhfr fur gubhtug gung

ng Oregun'f guna va gur pbzsbegnoyr, zvqqyr-pynff, frysvfu ubhfr bs

Ina Fnrgmrzn'f nyjnlf irkrq ure: vg jnf nf gubhtu fur qvq abg erpbtavmr

gung Sybbegwr jnf ratntrq naq ure gebhffrnh, bs pbhefr, pbhyq abg or nf

Nqbycuvar jnf nyjnlf fb fcvgrshy, jvgu ure crecrghny "Lrf, gung'f tbbq

Naq jung gur byq jbzna ybirq nobir nyy guvatf va Oregun'f ubhfr jnf gur
zhghny flzcngul, gur snzvyl-nssrpgvba juvpu fur unq nyjnlf sbfgrerq va
ure bja ubhfr, juvpu fur fgvyy sbfgrerq, gunaxf gb gur vafgvghgvba bs
gubfr Fhaqnl riravatf, gb xrrc gur puvyqera gbtrgure ng nyy pbfgf. Lrf,
va Ina Antury naq Oregun gung fragvzrag, gung pbafgnag gubhtug sbe gur
puvyqera jnf irel fgebat; naq gurer jnf bar guvat juvpu Znzzn ina Ybjr
unq abg qbar naq juvpu Oregun jnf qbvat, juvpu jnf gb erprvir gur fba
ntnva, nsgre ur unq bapr yrsg gur ubhfr, abj gung ur jnf ergheavat jvgu
n fvpx jvsr naq gjb yvggyr puvyqera. Vg gbhpurq ure: bu, ubj tbbq gurl
jrer gb gurve gevor; naq jung n gubhfnaq cvgvrf gung gung yvggyr
qbyy-jvsr jnf fb vyy! Naq gur puvyqera, gbb, unq gung fnzr
snzvyl-nssrpgvba nzbat gurzfryirf. Bggb unq nyjnlf xrcg hc n ohfl
pbeerfcbaqrapr jvgu uvf ryqrfg fvfgre, Ybhvfr, jub jnf gjragl-svir naq
pnzr arkg gb uvz va ntr; gur gjb Yrvqra oblf jrer rkprrqvatyl avpr gb
gurve guerr snfuvbanoyr yvggyr fvfgref naq Uraev jnf rira n yvggyr ovg
wrnybhf orpnhfr Rzvyvr jnf ratntrq; bayl Xnery jnf creuncf engure gbb
zhpu bhg bs qbbef naq njnl sebz gur snzvyl-pvepyr sbe fb lbhat n obl,
jvgu nyy uvf pyhof naq uvf vzcbegnapr; naq, orpnhfr bs gung, Znevrgwr,
gur lbhatrfg tvey, bs sbhegrra, jnf yrsg n tbbq qrny nybar. Naq lrg gurl
nyy yvxrq Znevrgwr: ure ovt oebguref, gur bgure tveyf.... Lrf, gung jnf
gur punezvat guvat jvgu nyy gubfr puvyqera: gur snzvyl-nssrpgvba, gur
sbaqarff sbe bar nabgure, gur cevqr va gur anzrf bs Ina Ybjr naq Ina
Antury, gur ershfny gb fhssre nal bhgfvqre gb fnl n jbeq ntnvafg n
zrzore bs gur snzvyl, rira gubhtu pevgvpvfz jnf abg fcnerq jvguva gur
ubzr vgfrys. Ohg gung nal npdhnvagnapr fubhyq qner gb ersyrpg hcba n
zrzore bs gur snzvyl, gung gurl jbhyq abar bs gurz crezvg. Gurl unq sryg
gung sbaqarff, gung graqrearff, rira sbe Pbafgnapr, orpnhfr fur jnf n
fvfgre. Naq gur byq ynql erzrzorerq, va fb sne nf pbaprearq Pbafgnapr,
gur cuvybfbcuvpny ersyrkvbaf bs ure lbhatrfg fba, Cnhy; gur gebhoyr
juvpu Qbevar unq gnxra gb nffrzoyr nyy gur oebguref naq fvfgref ba gung
svefg Fhaqnl-riravat; gur ernql pbzcyvnapr bs nyy ure puvyqera, sbe, bhg
bs erfcrpg gb ure, abar bs gurz unq pevgvpvmrq gung reevat fvfgre va
sebag bs ure. Fur fnj vg va nyy bs gurz: gur snzvyl-nssrpgvba sbe bar
nabgure. Gurl nyy sryg gurzfryirf gb or oebguref naq fvfgref; gurl fgbbq
hc sbe bar nabgure, rira gubhtu gurer jrer qvssreraprf bs bcvavba
fbzrgvzrf naq rira wrnybhfl; gurl sryg havgrq jvguva gur snzvyl-pvepyr.

Gung jnf gur pebjavat tybel bs ure byq ntr, nf n zbgure naq tenaqzbgure.
Vg ercerfragrq gb ure n ornhgvshy vqrn, n angheny vqrny, na vyyhfvba
nggnvarq: n pbzsbeg sbe gur crnprshy qrpyvavat lrnef bs gur ybaryl jbzna
va ure ovt ubhfr. Gung fur cersreerq gb or ybaryl va ure ovt ubhfr naq
jbhyq abg unir Qbevar, abe Reafg, abe Cnhy gb yvir jvgu ure jnf na
rppragevpvgl juvpu va ab jnl qrgenpgrq sebz ure phyg bs gur ornhgvshy
vqrn, sebz ure cresrpg unccvarff ng frrvat gur vqrny ernyvmrq, gur
vyyhfvba nggnvarq. Fur unq n unccl byq ntr. Fur unq nyfb unq zhpu fbeebj
va ure ovt ubhfrubyq, va fcvgr bs nyy ure fcyraqbhe, ohg abg zber guna
ure angheny funer: zbarl-gebhoyrf, orpnhfr arvgure Ina Ybjr abe fur jnf
rpbabzvpny; gjb puvyqera ybfg, bar nsgre gur bgure; juvyr Pbafgnapr'
snyfr fgrc jnf pregnvayl n irel urnil oybj, haqre juvpu fur fhfcrpgrq
gung Ina Ybjr unq ernyyl fhpphzorq, fhssrevat fvyragyl naq vaprffnagyl
orpnhfr bs gur tevrs juvpu uvf snibhevgr qnhtugre unq pnhfrq uvz.... Ohg
fur, gubhtu fur gbb unq fhssrerq, unq fubja terngre rynfgvpvgl, unq abg
pbhagrq nyy gung fbeebj sbe zber guna ure uhzna ybg, fhpu nf zvtug
orsnyy nal ynetr ubhfrubyq. Naq gung fur abj, va ure rkgerzr byq ntr,
unq nyy ure puvyqera tngurerq nobhg ure va gur fnzr gbja, va n pybfr
snzvyl-pvepyr, va na nssrpgvbangr snzvyl-yvsr: guvf fur pbafvqrerq n
terng unccvarff; fur gunaxrq Tbq sbe vg. Fur unq ab zber eryvtvba bs gur
puhepu-tbvat xvaq guna jnf uryq gb or pbeerpg va ure pvepyr, juvpu jnf
irel qvssrerag sebz gur begubqbk Pnyivavfgvp pvepyr bs n srj byq Unthr
snzvyvrf; ohg fur jnf tengrshy gb Tbq va ure urneg. Fur gunaxrq Tbq sbe
ure unccvarff, sbe ure unccl byq ntr. Nyy jnf jryy, abj gung fur unq
Pbafgnapr onpx nyfb, onpx jvgu gur bguref ng gur Unthr. Arkg gb
Ohvgrambet, gur Unthr unq nyjnlf orra gb ure gur vqrny cynpr bs
erfvqrapr. Gur Pbheg jnf gurer; naq ure uhfonaq unq gnhtug ure gb ybir
fcyraqbhe. Gurer jnf na ngzbfcurer bs bssvpvny rzvarapr va gurve pvepyr
va juvpu fur gbbx cyrnfher nf va na ryrzrag gung unq orpbzr angheny gb
ure naq va juvpu Ina Antury naq Oregun nyfb unq nggnvarq gurve
qvfgvapgvba naq gurve uvtu cbfvgvba. Xnery unq erghearq gb gur Unthr,
nsgre ohetbznfgrevat ryfrjurer; naq va uvz fur unq ure fba onpx ntnva,
nygubhtu, va ure frperg urneg, fur qvq abg yvxr Pngrnh. Treevg, jub unq
orra n fhonygrea ng Qriragre naq Irayb, jnf abj n pncgnva ng gur Unthr.
Naq gur bgure puvyqera unq arire yrsg gur Unthr; fur unq nyjnlf orra
noyr gb xrrc gurz ebhaq ure.

Fur jnf unccl naq fur jnf abg hagunaxshy. Fur jnf rira gunaxshy gung
Bggb jnf ergheavat--nygubhtu gur ernfba, uvf jvsr'f vyyarff, jnf n fnq
bar--orpnhfr fur jbhyq frr ure terng-tenaqpuvyqera. Gurl jrer ure svefg;
fur sryg n arj wbl orpnhfr bs gurz, na haxabja rzbgvba. Fur unq sryg
fbzrguvat yvxr vg jura Bggb uvzfrys jnf obea, ure svefg tenaqpuvyq; ohg
abj gung srryvat jnf nyzbfg zber vagrafr, creuncf orpnhfr vg jnf n
sbhegu trarengvba, n pbagvahngvba bs gur snzvyl, rira gubhtu gurl jrer
Ina Anturyf naq abg Ina Ybjrf. Fur jnf n jbzna: fur qvq abg pner fb zhpu
nobhg gur anzr. Oregun jnf ure qnhtugre, Bggb ure tenaqfba, uvf puvyqera
ure tenaqpuvyqera. Fur genprq gurz onpx va guvf jnl gb urefrys naq gur
fbhaq bs gur anzr znggrerq yrff gb ure. Gurl jrer ure puvyqera, ure
tenaqpuvyqera, ure terng-tenaqpuvyqera; naq fur ybirq gurz nyy, jvgu bar
terng ybir, jvgu n pynaavfu ybir. Gung fur yvirq nybar va ure ovt ubhfr
jnf orpnhfr fur jnf byq naq pbhyq orne ohfgyr bayl jura vg jnf rkcrpgrq,
jura fur pbhyq cercner sbe vg. Gur Fhaqnl riravatf jrer ohfgyvat, ohg
gurl qvq abg gver ure. Ohg gb unir Cnhy be Qbevar yvivat jvgu ure, gb or
sbe rire urnevat gurz tbvat va naq bhg jbhyq unir jbexrq ba ure areirf.
Fur jnaqrerq qnvyl guebhtu nyy gur ebbzf bs gur ovt ubhfr gb frr vs
rirelguvat jnf gvql naq va vgf cynpr. Qbevar jnf fybirayl; naq Cnhy jnf
nalguvat ohg rnfl gb trg ba jvgu; naq Reafg, jvgu uvf pbyyrpgvba bs
phevbfvgvrf, fur jbhyq arire or noyr gb unir jvgu ure, orpnhfr fur jnf
nsenvq bs nyy gur zvpeborf gung unat nobhg gubfr byq guvatf. Ohg
arireguryrff fur ybirq gurz nyy naq fur jnf tynq gung gurl yvirq ng gur
Unthr naq gung fur fnj gurz erthyneyl. Fur jnf yvxr gung naq ab
bgurejvfr.

Naq fur abj pnzr rirel qnl gb Oregun'f, jnvgvat sbe Bggb naq uvf
puvyqera, hagvy Pbafgnapr terj wrnybhf naq ercebnpurq ure, fnlvat gung
fur arire pnzr gb ure arj ubhfr arne gur Jbbqf.




PUNCGRE KI


Gur Ina Anturyf tnir na riravat-cnegl ng gur Bhqr Qbryra Ubgry, gjb qnlf
fhofrdhrag gb gur fvtavat bs gur zneevntr-pbagenpg orgjrra Rzvyvr naq
Ina Enira: n qvaare, sbe eryngvbaf naq vagvzngr sevraqf, bs arneyl n
uhaqerq pbiref. Nsgre gung, gur lbhat crbcyr jrer gb qb fbzr
gurngevpnyf; naq, nsgre gung, gurer jnf n qnapr. Qvaare jnf bire; naq
Nqbycuvar nfxrq Hapyr Ehliranre:

"Jrer lbh ng gurve qvaare-cnegl gjb avtugf ntb?"

"Jung qvaare-cnegl?"

"Gur qnl orsber lrfgreqnl, nsgre gur pbagenpg. Gurl tnir n qvaare ng
gurve ubhfr. Nobhg fvkgl crbcyr. Bayl gurve fzneg sevraqf naq gurve
Pbheg frg. Jr jrer abg nfxrq. Znzzn jrag. Ohg abar bs gur oebguref naq
fvfgref."

"V qvq abg rira xabj gurer jnf n qvaare. Jr pnyyrq va gur nsgreabba gb
pbatenghyngr gur oevqr naq oevqrtebbz."

"Jryy, gung riravat gurl tnir gurve tenaq nssnve. Gb-avtug vf bayl n
fznyy cnegl sbe hf naq gur ent-gnt bs gurve npdhnvagnapr. Gur bgure
avtug, Oregun jber n ybj-arpxrq qerff naq n genva. Gb-avtug, fur unf n
uvtu sebpx."

Hapyr ynhturq:

"Lrf," ur fnvq, "gurfr cnegvrf ng ubgryf ner nyjnlf fpengpu nssnvef. Gur
qvaare jnf bayl fb-fb."

"Erthyne ubgry-sbbq."

"U'z. Gur punzcntar jnf tbbq," fnvq Hapyr, jub unq qehax uvf svyy.

"Ubj onqyl Ina Antury fcbxr! Qbrf ur fcrnx nf onqyl nf gung jura ur
vagebqhprf uvf Vaqvna ohqtrg? Naq jung n svther Ina Enira'f zbgure phgf!
Fur ybbxf yvxr V qba'g xabj jung!"

"Fgvyy, gurl'er fzneg crbcyr."

"Lrf, bs pbhefr gurl'er fzneg, be Oregun jbhyq arire unir frvmrq hcba
uvz sbe ure qnhtugre! Ur'f n snfg perngher, gung shgher arcurj bs zvar.
Naq ubj Rzvyvr unatf ba gb uvz! Vs Sybbegwr uhat ba gb Qvwxreubs yvxr
gung, V fubhyq tvir ure n tbbq gnyxvat-gb jura jr tbg ubzr. Rzvyvr
orunirf whfg yvxr n fgerrg-tvey."

Hapyr jnf va n tbbq uhzbhe, orpnhfr ur unq cyragl gb qevax; ur jnf
chssvat n ovg naq jbhyq unir yvxrq gb haqb n ohggba bs uvf jnvfgpbng:
gung qerff-jnvfgpbng bs uvf jnf trggvat engure gvtug sbe uvz.

"Ubj cerggl Sybbegwr vf ybbxvat, Nqbycuvar. Gung juvgr fhvgf ure."

Fur ynhturq unccvyl; fur sryg synggrerq:

"Lrf, qbrfa'g vg? Vg znxrf Rzvyvr ybbx fb cnyr."

Znzzn ina Ybjr cnffrq ba Bggb ina Antury'f nez:

"Vf Senaprf orggre, zl obl?"

"Lrf, Tenaal, fur'f cerggl jryy gb-qnl. Ohg fur trgf gverq fb fbba."

Ur jnf gnyy naq guva, jvgu n fpbjy nobir uvf uneq Ina Ybjr rlrf, uvf
tenaqsngure'f rlrf. Uvf gjb lrnef va Wnin unq znqr uvz fb ovggre gung vg
jnf cnvashy sbe uvf tenaqzbgure naq uvf cneragf gb yvfgra gb uvz.

"Jung n cvgl, Bggb, gung lbh unq gb yrnir Vaqvn!"

"Bu, onu, Tenaal, jung n pbhagel! Vg'f nyy irel jryy sbe lbh gb gnyx:
lbh xabj Vaqvn nf gur jvsr bs n erfvqrag naq nf gur jvsr bs gur
tbireabe-trareny. Ohg sbe lbhat crbcyr, fgnegvat yvsr...."

"Cncn jbhyq unir urycrq lbh, lbh xabj...."

"N ybg bs uryc Cncn pbhyq unir tvira!... N ornfgyl pbhagel; n qvegl,
jergpurq pbhagel!"

"Ohg, Bggb, V gubhtug vg qryvtugshy."

"Ab qbhog, va lbhe cnynpr ng Ohvgrambet. Gung tbrf jvgubhg fnlvat. Ohg
jrer lbh rire pyrex gb gur zntvfgengrf ng Enaxnf-Orgbrat?"

"Ab."

"Ab, bs pbhefr abg. Naq gung jvgu n jvsr jub gbccyrf bire yvxr n
avarcva, gjvpr n jrrx, jvgu gur urng, syng ba gur sybbe!"

"Bggb!"

"Bu, pbzr, Tenaqznzzn! Vg'f gur zbfg pbasbhaqrq, ornfgyl, svygul pbhagel
V rire jnf va. Jr unq zhpu orggre fryy gubfr pbybavrf gb Ratynaq; fur'yy
bayl gnxr gurz sebz hf, bar qnl, vs jr qba'g."

"Bggb, ernyyl V'z abg hfrq gb guvf ynathntr!"

"Bu, lrf, Tenaal, V xabj nyy gung bssvpvny obzonfg nobhg Vaqvn! Ohg jr
pna'g nyy or tbireabe-trareny be pbybavny zvavfgre. Vs V rire orpbzr
gung, V funyy ortva gb jbefuvc Vaqvn ng bapr."

"Lbh'er hcfrg orpnhfr Senaprf vf vyy."

"Vyy? Vyy? Vg gnxrf n jbzna gb or vyy. Fur'f abg rira gung. Fur'f n
errq. Vs lbh oybj hcba ure, fur oernxf."

"Fur jnf n qryvpngr yvggyr guvat nf n tvey, Bggb."

"Jryy, ohg ybbx urer, Tenaal: V pna'g ghea ure vagb n ebohfg yvggyr
guvat, pna V?"

"Sbe funzr, Bggb! Qba'g or fb ovggre. Lbh'ir tbg gjb qneyvat yvggyr
puvyqera."

"Lrf, puvyqera; V jvfu V unqa'g. V'z fbeel sbe gur cbbe yvggyr
qrivyf.... Vf gur fubj ortvaavat abj? Gnoyrnhk-ivinagf, neenatrq ol qrne
byq Ybhvfr.... N cynl jvgubhg jbeqf ol Senaf naq Uraev.... Fgnyr guvatf,
gurfr jrqqvat-cnegvrf, nyjnlf. V gubhtug bhef vafhssrenoyr."

"Zl qrne Bggb, lbh'er va na vagbyrenoyr uhzbhe."

"V'z nyjnlf yvxr gung abj, Tenaal."

"Gura V fgebatyl nqivfr lbh gb rkrepvfr n yvggyr frys-pbageby, be lbh
jvyy arire unir nal unccvarff va yvsr, va lbhe bja be lbhe jvsr'f be
lbhe snzvyl'f."

"Gur snzvyl qbrfa'g nssrpg zl unccvarff."

"Jung qb lbh zrna, Bggb?"

"Jul, V qba'g yvir naq zbir naq unir zl orvat va zl snzvyl, Tenaal!"

"Bu, ernyyl, zl obl, lbh'er gbb ubeevq! Gnxr zr onpx gb zl frng. V frr
lbhe zbgure orpxbavat gb zr: fur jnagf zr gb fvg orgjrra ure naq Nhag
Ehliranre. Gur cresbeznapr vf ortvaavat...."

"Lr-r-rf," Pngrnh jnf juvavat gb Ina Fnrgmrzn, Ina qre Jrypxr naq Xnery.
"Na riravat-cnegl bs fvk-gl crb-cyr. Naq gur Ehf-fvna _Zvavfgre_ jnf
gurer, naq gur Zvf-gerff bs gur _Eborf_."

"Jryy, nsgre nyy, vs gurl unir fb znal npdhnvagnaprf," fnvq Xnery, haqre
uvf oerngu, ol jnl bs rkphfr.

"Lr-r-rf, ohg, Xn-ery, abar bs gur snz-vyl. Ina qre Jry-pxr, jrer _lbh_
vaivgrq, ol punapr?"

"Ab."

"Bu, abg lbh rv-gure? Jryy, V fubhyq unir _gubhtug_ gung fur jbhyq unir
nfxrq Pba-fgnapr...."

"Jul?" nfxrq Ina qre Jrypxr, pbyqyl.

"Jr-ryy, orpnhfr fur hfrq gb tb gb _Pbheg_, va gur _byq_ qnlf. Naq lbh
_gbb_, qvqa'g lbh, Ina qre Jrypxr?"

"Lrf, V gbb," fnvq Ina qre Jrypxr, qevyl.

"Ina qre Jrypxr," fnvq Xnery. "Qvq lbh trg gung pneq bs zvar?"

"Jung pneq?"

"Jul, jura lbh jrer rkcrpgrq va gbja, V pnyyrq naq yrsg n pneq ba lbh."

"Fb qvq V, lbh xabj, Ina qre Jrypxr," vagreehcgrq Ina Fnrgmrzn.

"Bu, lrf," fnvq Ina qre Jrypxr. "Vg jnf irel pvivy bs lbh sryybjf. Jryy,
V'yy yrnir n pneq ba lbh bar bs gurfr qnlf."

"Bu, V qvqa'g zragvba vg sbe gung!" fnvq Ina Fnrgmrzn.

"V qvqa'g zragvba vg ba gung nppbhag!" rpubrq Xnery, fjryyvat jvgu
travnyvgl. "Bayl V fubhyq unir gubhtug vg n ober vs vg unq orra
zvfynvq."

"Lr-rf," juvzcrerq Pngrnh. "Orpnhfr gura vg jbhyq unir ybbxrq nf vs jr
jrera'g sevraq-yl.... Ubj erq gur _oevqr_ ybbxf, Fnrg-mr-zn! Gung juvgr
znxrf Rz-vyvr ybbx fb _irel_ erq."

"Lryybj, engure," fnvq Ina Fnrgmrzn.

"Lr-rf," qebarq Pngrnh. "Abj lbhe Sybbegwr, Fnrg-mr-zn, ybbxf fb _fjrrg_
va juvgr. Naq jung n _avpr_ sryybj Qvw-xreubs vf! Fhpu n gubebhtu _zna_.
Ohg ubj cnyr Ore-gun ybbxf!"

"Terra, engure," fnvq Ina qre Jrypxr, irel frevbhfyl.

Pngrnh ybbxrq hc, jvgu ure bjy'f rlrf:

"Terra?" fur ercrngrq, pnhgvbhfyl. "Qb lbh er-nyyl guvax Ore-gun ybbxf
_terra_, Ina qre Jry-pxr? Lrf, fur vf gverq, ab qbhog."

"Gb-zbeebj," gubhtug Ina qre Jrypxr, "nyy gur Unthr jvyy xabj gung V
gubhtug Oregun ybbxrq terra...."

N gnoyrnh jnf qvfpbirerq va gur qvfgnapr. Gur vqrn jnf Cnhy'f naq ur
rkcynvarq vg gb Pbafgnapr:

"Lbh frr, vg ercerfragf Yhkhel. Gur terng jurry pehfuvat qbja hcba
Znevrgwr naq Pnebyvragwr vf Vaqhfgel; naq Sybbegwr vf Yhkhel, fgnaqvat
va n qnapvat nggvghqr ba Vaqhfgel naq fpnggrevat tbyq naq ebcrf bs
crneyf ng gjbcrapr n ebcr. Vg'f abg dhvgr pyrne, creuncf, Yhkhel
fgnaqvat hcba Vaqhfgel naq pehfuvat Znevnaar naq Pnebyvragwr. Sybbegwr
vf svqtrgvat naq tvttyvat. Bu, V zhfg gryy lbh, Nqbycuvar jnf qryvtugrq
jura fur urneq gung Sybbegwr, ure Sybbegwr, jnf gb or Yhkhel naq gb
pehfu Oregun'f Znevnaar!"

Pbafgnapr, fheebhaqrq ol nyy ure snzvyl, jnf va n tragyr, unccl zbbq:

"Bu, Cnhy, vg'f n irel avpr, zbgureyl srryvat ba Nqbycuvar'f cneg, gb
yvxr gb frr ure puvyq unccl orsber nabgure...."

Cnhy fcyhggrerq jvgu ynhtugre:

"Fb lbh guvax gung Sybbegwr vf unccl nf Yhkhel, ba gur gbc bs Znevnaar
naq gung Znevnaar fhssref onqyl haqrearngu! Pbaavr, ubj fragvzragny lbh
ner gb-avtug naq jung fvyyl guvatf lbh fnl!... Ohg lbh'er ybbxvat irel
avpr. Pbzr, yrg'f tb naq fvg qbja urer. Lbhe unve vf gheavat terl, ohg V
unir na vqrn gung lbh yrnir vg hagbhpurq sbe fbzr pbdhrggvfu ernfba,
orpnhfr vg tbrf fb jryy jvgu lbhe lbhat srngherf. Vg'f n irel cerggl
funqr bs terl. Vg'f abg byq unve. Ohg lbh'er lbhat fgvyy, lbh xabj. Naq
lbh'er ybbxvat avpr, irel avpr...."

"V oryvrir lbh'er znxvat sha bs zr...."

"V ybir tbbq-ybbxvat crbcyr; naq bar frrf fb srj bs gurz. Whfg tynapr
ebhaq gur ebbz: nyy htyl crbcyr; bar jnyxf pebbxrq, nabgure unf n fgbbc,
guvf bar'f ohfg fgvpxf bhg sbe zvyrf, gung bar unf n sng fgbznpu. V

sbetvir zr: fur vf lbhe fvfgre-va-ynj; naq vg vf _irel_ trarebhf, _zbfg_
trarebhf bs lbh...."

Gjb nhagf bs Nqryvar'f fgbccrq gur snve-unverq yvggyr zbgure:

"Nqryvragwr!"

"Lrf, Nhagvr?"

"Gung arj fvfgre bs lbhef: qb lbh yvxr ure?"

"Vf fur avpr?"

"Lrf, Nhagvr, ernyyl irel avpr."

"Ohg fur'f orra na vzcebcre jbzna."

"Bu, Nhagvr!"

"Lrf, lrf, lrf, zl tvey, jr xabj nyy nobhg vg; lbh or pnershy."

"Naq qba'g orpbzr unaq-va-tybir gbb dhvpxyl."

"Lbh'er fb gubhtugyrff, Nqryvragwr."

"Naq Treevg vf fb tbbq-angherq."

"Gnxr pner, obgu bs lbh!"

"N jbzna yvxr gung pna qb uvz unez va uvf pnerre."

"Bu, pbzr, Nhagvr! Vs gur Ina Anturyf erprvir gurz!"

"Lrf, ohg gur Ina Anturyf qvfnccebir bs gurz fgebatyl."

"Fgvyy, fur'f gurve fvfgre."

"Rirelobql'f gnyxvat nobhg gurz. Crbcyr fnl...."

"Jung?"

"Gung Pbafgnapr vf abg ... jryy, gung fur'f abg ure sngure'f puvyq!"

"Ohg Nhagvr, gung'f n sevtugshy guvat gb fnl!"

"Orpnhfr gur Ina Ybjrf jrer nyjnlf fb erfcrpgnoyr, fur pna'g...."

"Ab, fur pna'g or n qnhtugre bs...."

"Bs byq Ina Ybjr'f."

"V fnl, Nhagvr, guvf vf fpheevybhf!"

"Nqryvragwr!"

"Nhagvr, V jba'g yvfgra gb nabgure jbeq!"

Pbhfvaf bs gur Ina Fnrgmrznf', gnyxvat jvgu gur VWxfgenf, eryngvbaf bs
Pngrnh'f:

"Cbbe qrne Nqbycuvar!"

"Fur'f shevbhf!"

"Jung ng?"

"Bu, nyy fbegf bs guvatf! Svefg, orpnhfr gur Ina Anturyf tnir n cnegl ng
juvpu gur jubyr snzvyl jrer vtaberq."

"Bu, jryy, gung pregnvayl jnf engure...."

"Gura, orpnhfr Nqbycuvar unf ab ebbz va ure ubhfr gb tvir n cnegl ng
juvpu fur jbhyq vtaber gur snzvyl va ure ghea."

"Naq orpnhfr bs gur frng juvpu fur jnf tvira ng qvaare guvf riravat."

"Naq orpnhfr bs Rzvyvrgwr'f gjb jvgarffrf: ure Hapyr Ina Antury, gur
Dhrra'f Pbzzvffnel va Birevwffry, naq Xnery ina Ybjr, jurernf fur fnlf
gung Ina Fnrgmrzn vf byqre guna Xnery naq gurersber...."

"Naq nyfb orpnhfr bs Rzvyvrgwr'f sebpx, orpnhfr gung syvzfl juvgr guvat
pnzr sebz Oehffryf naq pbfg guerr uhaqerq senapf."

"Jung n urnc Ina Antury zhfg or fcraqvat ba gur jrqqvat!"

"Ab, vg'f Oregun: vg'f gur Ina Ybjrf jub nyjnlf guebj zbarl nobhg."

"Rknpgyl, gung'f jung V fnl: Nqbycuvar qbrf gur fnzr guvat, whfg nf
gubhtu fur pbhyq nssbeq vg."

"Gung'f orpnhfr nyy bs gubfr Ina Ybjrf ner rngra hc jvgu cevqr naq
pbaprvg."

"Lrf, fvapr gur sngure orpnzr tbireabe-trareny, gurl unir nyjnlf npgrq
yvxr zrtnybznavnpf."

"Gur byq ynql vf n erthyne crnpbpx."

"Naq Oregun, jvgu ure fzneg npdhnvagnaprf!"

"Naq gura gung Zef. ina qre Jrypxr: fur'f tbg n avpr cnfg gb ybbx onpx
hcba! Naq fur orunirf nf gubhtu fur jrer gur Dhrra!"

"Gurl'er dhvgr na beqvanel snzvyl, gur Ina Ybjrf."

"Lrf, gurl'er abobqvrf: gur tenaqsngure jnf n tebpre."

"Ab!"

"Lrf, V nffher lbh!"

"Naq gung znq Reafg, jub'f nyjnlf fghqlvat gur snzvyl-cncref gb qvfpbire
vs gurl ner abg bs aboyr qrfprag!"

"Bu, ur'f znq, vs lbh yvxr!"

"Va snpg, gurl'er nyy n yvggyr ovg znq."

"Lrf, gurer'f n fgenva bs vg va nyy bs gurz."

"N fgenva? Fbzrguvat zber guna n fgenva _V_ pnyy vg. Naq vg'f pbagvahrq
va gur Ina Anturyf."

"Nqbycuvar'f gur orfg bs gur ybg."

"Fur'f n zrtnybznavnp, gubhtu, sbe nyy gung."

"V fnl, guvf Zef. ina qre Jrypxr: jung unf fur pbzr urer sbe?"

"Jryy, fur guvaxf gur jubyr guvat unf oybja bire. Vg jnf svsgrra lrnef
ntb, lbh frr. Naq fur'f zneevrq gb Ina qre Jrypxr."

"Abg nppbeqvat gb Qhgpu ynj."

"Ab, ohg fur pna trg zneevrq ntnva."

"Lrf, ohg gurl ner abg, gurl ner _abg_ zneevrq nppbeqvat gb Qhgpu ynj."

"Jryy, va gung pnfr, _V_ qba'g ybbx hcba gurz nf zneevrq ng nyy!"

"Abg nppbeqvat gb Qhgpu...."

"Ab, ohg...."

"Lrf...."

"Ab...."

"Lrf...."

Gur cnegl raqrq naq gur thrfgf qrcnegrq.




PUNCGRE KIV


Arkg qnl, Rzvyvr naq Znevnaar ina Antury jrer uneq ng jbex va gurve
obhqbve. Gurl funerq n fvggvat-ebbz orgjrra gurz; Ybhvfr, gur ryqrfg
fvfgre, unq bar gb urefrys. Rzvyvr jnf gnxvat qbja jngre-pbybhef sebz
gur jnyy:

"Gur ebbz jnf fb oevtug naq purreshy!" fur fnvq, fbsgyl, naq chg gur
qenjvatf gbtrgure.

Znevnaar fhqqrayl ohefg vagb fbof. Gur ebbz jnf nyy gbcfl-gheil, orpnhfr
Rzvyvr jnf pbyyrpgvat ure orybatvatf, naq gur jnyy-cncre abj fubjrq va
serfu, hasnqrq erpgnathyne cngpurf.

"Jung ba rnegu qb lbh jnag gb zneel gung ubeevq zna sbe!" pevrq
Znevnaar, fboovat. "Jr jrer fb unccl, gur gjb bs hf; jr jrer nyjnlf
gbtrgure. Jvgu lbh zneevrq, V funyy unir ab bar; naq V ungr gur vqrn bs
neenatvat zl ebbz nyy bire ntnva."

Rzvyvr frrzrq gb or fgnevat oynaxyl vagb n oynax shgher:

"Bu, pbzr, Znevnaar: V funyy fgvyy or ng gur Unthr!"

"Ab, V'ir ybfg lbh!" fboorq Znevnaar, cnffvbangryl. "Jung qvq lbh frr va
gung zna, jung _qvq_ lbh frr va uvz?" Fur rzoenprq ure fvfgre ivbyragyl
naq vafvfgrq. "Gryy zr, gryy zr: jung qvq lbh frr va gung zna?"

"Va Rqhneq? V ybir uvz."

"Bu?" fnvq Znevnaar. "Vf gung nyy vg zrnaf, ybivat n zna? Vf gung ybir?"

N znvq ragrerq:

"Serhyr, gurer'f n obk pbzr sebz Oehffryf, jvgu lbhe qerffrf. Zriebhj
jnagf gb xabj vs vg pna or oebhtug hc ng bapr, fb nf abg gb znxr n
yvggre qbjafgnvef."

"Lrf, gurl pna oevat vg hc."

Birejebhtug, Znevnaar unq fhax vagb n punve naq pybfrq ure rlrf. Fur jnf
va n fgngr bs areibhf rkpvgrzrag, juvyr Rzvyvr, jvgu fgenatr pnyzarff,
jnf pbyyrpgvat obkrf, cbegenvgf, beanzragf.

"Rzvyvr," fnvq Znevnaar, erfvtarqyl, "jung n zrff lbh'er znxvat!"

"Arire zvaq, V'z gnxvat vg nyy njnl."

"Lrf, gung'f whfg vg: rirelguvat'f tbvat njnl, rirelguvat'f tbvat njnl!"

"Znevnaar, qb pbageby lbhefrys."

Gjb znvqf pnzr qenttvat nybat n cnpxvat-pnfr.

"Jurer funyy jr chg vg, serhyr?"

"Yrnir vg gurer, va gur cnffntr."

Oregun pnzr hcfgnvef:

"Hacnpx vg ng bapr, Rzvyvr, be gur guvatf jvyy pernfr."

"Qb lbh guvax vg'f zl jrqqvat-qerff?"

"V rkcrpg fb."

"Gura vg pna tb ba gur orq."

"Ab, vg unq orggre or uhat va gur jneqebor."

Gur freinagf bcrarq gur cnpxvat-pnfr naq cebqhprq pneqobneq obkrf. N
guveq znvq ragrerq:

"N ovyy sebz Ina qre Ynna'f, zriebhj."

"Znevnaar, urer'f zl xrl-onfxrg; whfg cnl vg, jvyy lbh? Vg'f fvkgl-fvk
thvyqref."

Gur gjb Yrvqra oblf pnzr hcfgnvef:

"Wbyyl ornfgyl, V pnyy vg," fnvq Senaf. "Lbh arire svaq nal bar va gur
qenjvat-ebbz, jura lbh pbzr ubzr. Rvgure vg'f n cnegl, be ryfr
rirelguvat'f hcfvqr qbja."

"Oyrff zl fbhy, tveyf," fnvq Uraev, "ybbx ng gur fgngr lbhe ebbz'f va!"

"V fnl, funyy V uryc lbh hacnpx?"

"Zriebhj, V pna'g haqrefgnaq jung gur lbhat zriebhj'f _onobr_[10]
fnlf...."

"_Znh ncn_,[11] Nyvzn?"

"_Awbawn zbrqn_[12] nfxf vs _awbawn orfne_[13] jbhyq zvaq pbzvat
hcfgnvef," fnvq gur _onobr_, va Znynl.

"Lrf, V'yy pbzr ng bapr."

"Jung ner lbh nyy qbvat urer?" nfxrq Znevrgwr, ng gur qbbe. "Znzzn, unf
Rzvyvr'f qerff pbzr? Znl V frr?"

"Vs lbh cyrnfr, zriebhj, gur byq zriebhj naq Zef. ina qre Jrypxr ner
qbjafgnvef.... Funyy V nfx gurz gb jnvg va gur qenjvat-ebbz?"

"Tenaal!" fubhgrq Senaf bire gur onyhfgref.

"Unys n zbzrag!" fnvq Uraev, ehfuvat qbja gur fgnvef. "V'yy srgpu Tenaal
naq Nhagvr."

Znevnaar ortna fboovat ntnva:

"Zl qrne puvyq, jung'f gur znggre abj?" rkpynvzrq Oregun.

"V'z tbvat znq!" pevrq Znevnaar.

Rzvyvr xvffrq ure.

Byq Zef. ina Ybjr pnzr fybjyl hc gur fgnvef, tnyynagyl rfpbegrq ol ure
tenaqfba, naq jnf zrg ba gur ynaqvat ol ure bgure tenaqfba.

"Tenaal, Rzvyvr'f jrqqvat-qerff unf pbzr naq fur'f tbvat gb gel vg ba!"
pevrq Znevrgwr, rkpvgrqyl.

"Nz V va gur jnl?" nfxrq Pbafgnapr.

"Ab, bs pbhefr abg, Pbafgnapr," fnvq Oregun.

"Pbzr va."

Nyy gur qbbef bs gur obhqbve naq orqebbz jrer bcra. Ybhvfr pnzr va--fur
hfhnyyl xrcg bhg bs gur jnl ng ohfl gvzrf--naq, gbtrgure jvgu Oregun naq
gur ynql'f znvq, fubbx bhg gur juvgr qerff, juvpu fgenvtugjnl svyyrq gur
jubyr ebbz jvgu n fabjl juvgrarff....

"Jung vf vg, _onobr_?" nfxrq Zef. ina Ybjr. "_Awbawn zbrqn_ nfxf vs
_awbawn orfne_ jbhyq pbzr hcfgnvef," ercrngrq gur _onobr_. "Ohg creuncf
vs gur _xnaqwrat awbawn orfne_[14] pbhyq pbzr...." fur nqqrq, cvyvat ba
gur gvgyrf bhg bs erfcrpg sbe gur byq ynql, jub unq bapr orra gur
_awbawn orfne Obtbe_.[15]

"Gura V'yy tb hc," fnvq gur byq ynql. "Pbafgnapr, jvyy lbh pbzr gbb?..."

Irel fybjyl, n yvggyr gverq nsgre gur fgnvef, gur byq ynql pyvzorq hc,
jvgu ure unaq ba gur onyhfgre-envy. Pbafgnapr sbyybjrq ure. Ba gur gbc
sybbe, gurer jnf n fhqqra qenhtug; qbbef fynzzrq.

"_Onobr_.... Vf gurer n jvaqbj bcra?"

Gur _onobr_ ena nobhg fghcvqyl, hasnzvyvne nf lrg jvgu Qhgpu qbbef naq
jvaqbjf.

Va n fvggvat-ebbz, gurl sbhaq Senaprf, Bggb'f jvsr, jvgu gur gjb
puvyqera.

"Ohg, Senaprf, lbh'ir tbg n jvaqbj bcra!"

"Bu, Tenaqznzzn, V jnf fhssbpngvat!"

"_Onobr_, fuhg gur jvaqbj ng bapr! Senaprf, ubj pbhyq lbh!"

"V pna'g, _xnaqwrat_!" fvturq gur _onobr_, cerffvat jvgu gur fgeratgu bs
n tang ba gur onef bs gur fbyvq Qhgpu jvaqbj.

Pbafgnapr urycrq ure, chfurq qbja gur jvaqbj.

"Guvf vf Nhag Pbafgnapr, jub unf pbzr gb znxr lbhe npdhnvagnapr,
Senaprf. Ohg Senaprf, lbh'er fgvyy va lbhe _fnebat_ naq _xnonnv_!"[16]

"Vfa'g gung nyybjrq, Tenaal? Ubj q'lr qb, Nhag?"

"Puvyq, ubj Vaqvna lbh'ir orpbzr va gurfr srj lrnef!" pevrq gur byq
ynql, natevre guna Pbafgnapr erzrzorerq rire frrvat ure. "Ubj vf vg
cbffvoyr, ubj vf vg cbffvoyr! Unir lbh sbetbggra Ubyynaq? Va Znepu, jvgu
gur jvaqbj bcra, va n grnevat qenhtug, jvgu obgu gur puvyqera, lbh va
_fnebat_ naq _xnonnv_ naq Uhvt va n yvggyr fuveg! Qb lbh jnag gb xvyy
lbhefrys naq gur puvyqera? _Onobr_, chg n _onnqwr_ ba _fvawb_![17]
Senaprf, Senaprf, V fcrag lrnef naq lrnef va Vaqvn, ohg rira va Vaqvn V
jnf arneyl nyjnlf qerffrq; naq, jura V pnzr onpx gb Ubyynaq, V unq abg
sbetbggra Ubyynaq va gur jnl va juvpu lbh, n cheryl Qhgpu tvey, unir
sbetbggra vg va gurfr srj lrnef!"

Gur byq jbzna unq gnxra gur puvyq ba ure bja ync naq jnf qerffvat vg
zber jnezyl.

"Tenaqznzzn, ubj lbh'er tehzoyvat.... Vg'q or orggre vs lbh gbyq pbbx gb
znxr Bggryvragwr'f _obrobre_[18] cebcreyl: gur puvyq pna'g rng gung
fgnepu gurl tvir ure. Naq fur gbyq _onobr_ gung fur unq ab gvzr gb pbbx
vg qvssreragyl. Gur jubyr ubhfr unf tbar znq orpnhfr Rzvyvr vf trggvat
zneevrq. Jr ernyyl pna'g fgnl urer, ba gur gbc sybbe ng Cncn naq
Znzzn'f."

"Senaprf, qerff lbhefrys svefg, be V funyy trg ernyyl natel."

"_Nyynu_, Tenaqznzzn!" pevrq Senaprf, veevgnoyl; ohg, jura Pbafgnapr
tnir ure gur fnzr nqivpr, fur syhat n jenccre bire ure _fnebat_ naq
_xnonnv_ naq erznvarq yvxr gung, jvgu ure oner srrg va fyvccref.

"Ab jbaqre lbh'er nyjnlf vyy!" tehzoyrq Tenaqznzzn, fgvyy ohflvat
urefrys jvgu gur puvyq.

"Bu, Nhag Pbafgnapr, V jbaqre vs lbh jbhyq eha qbja gb gur xvgpura naq
gryy pbbx gung Bggryvragwr pna'g unir ure _obrobre_ znqr yvxr gung?"

"Zl qrne Senaprf," ynhturq Pbafgnapr, "gur pbbx unf arire frra zr, abe V
ure: naq, vs V jrag gb ure xvgpura naq gnyxrq nobhg gur _obrobre_, fur
jbhyq bayl ghea zr bhg."

"Jung n pbhagel gb yvir va, Ubyynaq!" pevrq Senaprf. "Zl puvyq vf
fgneivat sbe sbbq!"

"V'yy tb qbja gb Znzzn, vs lbh yvxr...."

"Lrf, qb, jbhyq lbh?"

Pbafgnapr jrag qbjafgnvef. Va gur obhqbve, Rzvyvr, va ure jrqqvat-qerff,
jnf fgnaqvat va sebag bs n ybat tynff. Gur urnil juvgr fngva pehfurq
ure, ybbxrq uneq naq pehry hcba ure, abj gung ure unve jnf abg qbar naq
fur gverq naq cnyr.

"Gur obqvpr qbrfa'g svg. Vg jvyy fvzcyl unir gb tb onpx gb Oehffryf,"
fnvq Oregun.

"Vg'f fvpxravat!" fnvq Rzvyvr; naq gur jbeq fbhaqrq nyzbfg yvxr n phefr
orgjrra ure yvcf.

"Znevnaar, jvyy lbh jevgr gur yrggre? V'yy cva gur qerff hc. Be ab, V
unq orggre jevgr zlfrys. Pbafgnapr, qb ybbx!"

"Gurer'f n pernfr urer," fnvq Pbafgnapr, "ohg vg'f abg irel onq. Qnera'g
lbh unir vg nygrerq urer?"

"Hcba zl jbeq, V'z cnlvat...." Oregun ortna, ohg fur purpxrq urefrys naq
qvq abg fnl ubj zhpu. "Naq gb unir vg svg onqyl vagb gur onetnva!"

"Oregun, Senaprf nfxrq zr gb pbzr naq frr lbh."

"Jung nobhg?"

"Gurer'f fbzr gebhoyr nobhg Bggryvragwr'f _obrobre_."

"V'yy tb hc," fnvq Oregun, jbea-bhg gubhtu fur jnf.

Gur znvq, ubyqvat hc Rzvyvr'f genva, sbyybjrq ure vagb gur orqebbz;
Znevnaar naq Pbafgnapr erznvarq oruvaq nybar. Pbafgnapr fnj gung
Znevnaar jnf pelvat.

"Jung vf vg, qrne?"

"Bu, Nhagvr!"

"Jung vf vg?"

"Vf yvsr jbegu nyy guvf obgure naq shff? Trggvat zneevrq, zbivat lbhe
guvatf, qnapvat, tvivat qvaaref naq cnegvrf, beqrevat qerffrf gung qba'g
svg naq pbfg uhaqerqf, orvat vyy, univat onovrf, rngvat _obrobre_:
Nhagvr, vf vg ernyyl nyy jbegu juvyr?"

"Jul, Znevnaar, V zvtug or yvfgravat gb Cnhy!"

"Bu, ab, V'z abg fb rybdhrag nf Cnhy! Ohg V'z fhssbpngvat jvgu vg nyy,
V'z fgvsyvat naq V'z greevoyl, greevoyl, greevoyl haunccl!"

"Znevnaar!"

Gur lbhat tvey fhqqrayl ohefg vagb areibhf fbof naq guerj urefrys vagb
Pbafgnapr' nezf. Nebhaq ure, gur ebbz jnf bar fprar bs pbashfvba; gur
qbbef jrer nyy bcra.

"Znevnaar, yrg zr fuhg gur qbbef."

"Ab, Nhagvr, qba'g zvaq nobhg gung, ohg fgnl jvgu zr, qb! Vg'f zber guna
V pna fgnaq, zber guna V pna fgnaq! V'z fb gverq bs guvf ehfu, bs guvf
haarprffnel rkpvgrzrag, bs gur cnegl lrfgreqnl, bs gubfr
gnoyrnhk-ivinagf, bs Sybbegwr'f wrnybhfl, bs Nhag Nqbycuvar'f
fcvgrshyarff, V nz gverq, gverq, gverq bs rirelguvat. V pna'g fgnaq vg,
Nhagvr. V'z fb sbaq bs Rzvyvr, jr'ir nyjnlf orra gbtrgure, vg jnf fb
avpr, fb wbyyl; naq abj, nyy ng bapr, fur'f trggvat zneevrq gb gung
ungrshy zna; naq fur'f gnxvat njnl ure fxrgpurf; naq vg'f nyy bire; naq
abj rirelguvat'f tbar, rirelguvat'f tbar! Naq Uraev gbb vf fb hcfrg
nobhg vg: ur qbgrf ba Rzvyvr, whfg nf V qb, naq ur pna'g haqrefgnaq
rvgure jung fur'f qbvat vg sbe. Fur'f irel unccl urer; Cncn naq Znzzn
naq nyy gur erfg ner sbaq bs ure; jr unq fhpu n avpr yvsr, rira vs vg
jnf n ovg bireqbar naq V qba'g pner sbe gung rireynfgvat tbvat bhg; ohg
abj vg'f nyy bire, nyy bire! V fng pelvat jvgu Uraev lrfgreqnl; naq ng
gur cnegl jr unq gb or tnl; naq rirel bar gubhtug gung ur jnf tnl, gur
tnl haqretenqhngr; naq gur cbbe obl jnf zvfrenoyr; naq lrfgreqnl V unq
gb nccrne va gung gnoyrnh; naq Sybbegwr jnf fb ubeevq naq fcvgrshy; naq
Uraev naq Senaf unq n qvnybthr gb qb; naq gur cbbe obl pbhyqa'g fcrnx
uvf jbeqf; naq V nfx lbh, Nhagvr, jul nyy guvf haunccvarff, jura jr jrer
fb unccl gbtrgure?"

Fur pyrapurq ure svfgf naq, guebhtu ure fbof, fhqqrayl ortna gb ynhtu
nybhq:

"Bu, Nhagvr!... Un, un!... Bu, Nhagvr!... Qba'g zvaq jung V fnl! V nz
znq, V nz znq, ohg vg'f gurl jub ner qevivat zr znq: Znzzn, gur oblf,
gur freinagf, gur _onobr_, Senaprf naq gur puvyqera! Vg'f bar terng
zreel-tb-ebhaq! Un, un!... Qvq lbh rire frr fhpu na rireynfgvat ehfu nf
jr unir va guvf ubhfr?"

Fur jnf abj fboovat naq ynhtuvat gbtrgure; naq fhqqrayl fur erzrzorerq
gung fur unq yrg urefrys tb gbb zhpu jvgu n fgenatr nhag naq gung Znzzn
qvq abg yvxr gurfr fcbagnarbhf pbasvqraprf gb fgenatref; naq, orpnhfr
fur jnagrq gb erpbire urefrys, fur fhqqrayl orpnzr engure qvtavsvrq naq
nfxrq:

"Qvq lbh rawbl lbhefrys snveyl lrfgreqnl, Nhag Pbafgnapr?"

"Lrf, Znevnaar, V gubhtug vg irel avpr gb or onpx nzbat lbh nyy."

"Qba'g lbh yvxr Oehffryf orggre guna gur Unthr?"

PUNCGRE KVK


Va gur fnzr areibhf zbbq va juvpu fur unq orra nyy qnl, Pbafgnapr
uheevrq, nsgre qvaare, gb gur Ormhvqraubhg, gnxvat gur genz nybat gur
Fpuriravatfpur Jrt naq nabgure gb gur Cyrva. Jura fur enat ng gur Ina
Anturyf', fur gubhtug vg fgenatr gung gurer jnf ab yvtug va gur unyy, nf
fur xarj, sebz Nqqvr, gung gurl jrer ng ubzr gung riravat. Gur ohgyre,
jub bcrarq gur qbbe, fnvq gung ur qvq abg xabj jurgure zriebhj pbhyq frr
ure, nf zriebhj jnf abg srryvat jryy.

Fur jnvgrq va gur qenjvat-ebbz, jurer gur ohgyre uheevrqyl ghearq ba gur
yvtug orsber tbvat gb fnl gung fur jnf gurer. Nyy ebhaq gur ovt ebbz
jrer gur snqrq naq jvgurerq sybjre-onfxrgf naq obhdhrgf bs Rzvyvr'f
jrqqvat, gur senvy sybjref fueviryyrq naq oebja naq qrpnlrq, juvyr gur
oebnq juvgr evoobaf fgvyy uhat va fvyirel sbyqf nebhaq gurz. Gur ebbz
unq rivqragyl abg orra gbhpurq fvapr gur jrqqvat-oernxsnfg: gur qhfg ynl
guvpx ba gur sheavgher; naq gur punvef fgvyy fgbbq nf gubhtu gur ebbz
unq whfg orra yrsg ol n zhygvghqr bs thrfgf.... Pbafgnapr jnvgrq fbzr
gvzr; gura fur urneq sbbgfgrcf. Znevnaar pnzr va, ybbxvat cnyr naq
hagvql:

"Jr ner fb fbeel, Nhagvr, gb unir xrcg lbh jnvgvat. Znzzn vf irel gverq
naq unf na njshy urnqnpur naq vf ylvat qbja va ure ebbz."

"Gura V jba'g qvfgheo ure."

"Ohg Znzzn nfxrq vs lbh jbhyq pbzr hcfgnvef."

Fur sbyybjrq Pbafgnapr gb Oregun'f orqebbz. Pbafgnapr jnf nfgbavfurq ng
gur nyzbfg qrnguyl fgvyyarff va gung terng ubhfr, juvpu, ba gur guerr be
sbhe bppnfvbaf gung fur unq ragrerq vg, fur unq arire frra bgure guna
shyy bs zbirzrag, yvsr, nyy fbegf bs yvggyr vagrerfgf juvpu gbtrgure
znqr hc n ohfgyvat rkvfgrapr. Gurer jnf ab qenhtug ba gur gbc sybbe,
jurer Senaprf unq ure ncnegzragf; gurer jrer ab qbbef fynzzvat; fur fnj
ab znvqf, ab _onobr_, ab puvyqera: rirelguvat jnf dhvrg, qrnqyl dhvrg.
Naq, jura fur ragrerq Oregun'f ebbz, vg ybbxrq gb ure, va gur fhoqhrq
yvtug, yvxr n fvpx-ebbz.

"V unir pbzr gb frr ubj lbh ner."

Oregun chg bhg ure unaq, fvyragyl. Gura fur fnvq:

"Gung vf avpr bs lbh. V nz irel gverq naq V unir n urnq-npur."

"V funyy abg fgnl ybat."

"Lrf, qb fgnl. V qba'g zvaq lbh."

Oregun naq Pbafgnapr jrer abj nybar. Naq vg fgehpx Pbafgnapr gung n
qvfpbafbyngr fnqarff qvfgbegrq Oregun'f srngherf naq gung fur ybbxrq
irel byq, abj gung ure unve, jvgu vgf terl cngpurf, jnf qbja.

"Nyy guvf ehfu unf orra gbb zhpu sbe lbh."

"Bu, V qba'g xabj," fnvq Oregun, inthryl. "Gurer'f nyjnlf cyragl bs ehfu
urer."

"Fgvyy, vg'f whfg nf jryy gung lbh'er gnxvat n erfg."

"Lrf."

Gurl jrer fvyrag naq gurer jnf ab fbhaq fnir gur gvpxvat bs gur pybpx.
Gura Pbafgnapr fgbbcrq naq xvffrq Oregun ba gur sberurnq:

"V jnagrq onqyl gb frr lbh guvf riravat," fur fnvq. "Nqqvr jnf bhg jvgu
Uraev naq ur gbyq zr gung Uraev jnf fb qrcerffrq. Naq fb V pnzr ebhaq."

"Uraev?" fnvq Oregun, inthryl. "V qba'g guvax fb; ur frrzrq nyy evtug."

"Ohg Nqqvr fnvq...."

"Jung?"

"Gung ur jnf fb qrcerffrq."

"Ernyyl? V qvqa'g abgvpr vg."

"Lrf, vg'f jebat. Naq zl jubyr yvsr vf jebat, rirelguvat unf tbar jebat

"Ab, ab. Jr bayl raqher rnpu bgure, sbe Nqqvr'f fnxr."

Ubyynaq; naq guvf vf gur svefg gvzr gung jr unir unq n punapr bs gnyxvat

guvf vf abg sebz urnegyrffarff, ohg orpnhfr bar unf ab gvzr."

"Lrf, Oregun, V xabj; naq V nz abg ercebnpuvat lbh; naq lbh'ir orra irel
ohfl jvgu gur jrqqvat...."

"Naq, jura vg'f abg n jrqqvat, vg'f fbzrguvat ryfr. Vg vf nyjnlf yvxr
gung, Pbafgnapr. Naq fbzrgvzrf V nfx zlfrys, jul: jul qb jr qb vg? Jul

ernfba sbe vg nyy: bhe puvyqera'f unccvarff yvrf va gung qverpgvba. Jr
qb rirelguvat sbe bhe puvyqera, gung'f jung vg pbzrf gb. Ina Antury'f

puvyqera unccl. Va erghea sbe nyy bhe gebhoyr naq jbeel, sbe nyy guvf

Senaprf vyy; Ybhvfr fnq orpnhfr bs Bggb, jubz fur vf fb sbaq bs; Rzvyvr
zneevrq abj--ohg ubj zneevrq, cbbe guvat, naq jul?--naq Znevnaar nyy
areirf naq abg xabjvat jung fur jnagf; naq Uraev gbb fb zrynapubyl: gura
V fnl gb zlfrys, 'Jul unir jr nyy gurfr puvyqera, sbe jubz jr yvir naq
guvax naq pbagevir? Naq jbhyqa'g vg or orggre abg gb unir gurz? Naq
vfa'g vg orggre gb unir nf yvggyr nf cbffvoyr va bar'f yvsr naq gb znxr
gung yvsr nf fznyy naq fvzcyr naq dhvrg nf cbffvoyr, bapr jr unir gb
yvir? Bu, Pbafgnapr, nyy guvf nvzyrffarff naq hfryrffarff nzvq juvpu

fbzrjurer naq ybbx bhg bire gur frn? Jbzra yvxr bhefryirf zneel nf lbhat
tveyf, xabjvat abguvat naq univat bayl n inthr cerfragvzrag bs bhe
yvirf, gung gurl jvyy or yvxr gur yvirf bs bhe zbguref orsber hf; naq

ivfvgf, qerffrf, qvaaref, guvatf juvpu jr gubhtug jrer arprffnel, nyy

abguvat! Naq gura, jura jr guvax gung jr unir yvirq sbe bhe puvyqera naq

abguvat, abguvat; naq abg bar bs gurz vf unccl....' Lbh frr, Pbafgnapr,
V unir gnyxrq gb lbh abj; ohg jung'f gur tbbq bs vg? Jul fnl nyy gung V
unir fnvq? Lbh'yy tb njnl cerfragyl naq guvax, 'Jung n svg bs qrcerffvba
Oregun unq!' Naq gung vf nyy vg jnf: n svg bs qrcerffvba. Sbe, jura V

"V nz irel tynq gubhtu, Oregun, gung lbh unir yrg lbhefrys tb. V qvq abg
xabj lbh gubhtug yvxr gung; V zlfrys unir fbzrgvzrf gubhtug fb, rira

abg arrq gb tb ba yvivat!'"

"Naq creuncf gurer ner uhaqerqf jub guvax yvxr gung, va bhe pynff."

"Vfa'g vg gur fnzr va rirel pynff?"

"Creuncf yvsr vf ubcryrff sbe rirelobql. Naq lrg, jura V nz erfgrq,
gb-zbeebj be gur qnl nsgre, naq jura zl urnq-npur vf tbar, V funyy fgneg
nyy guvf jbex bire ntnva."

ntnva, jrer yvxr gjb fvfgref. Gura Oregun jrag ba:

"Jura V yvr urer yvxr guvf, jvgu zl urnq-npurf, V nyjnlf guvax bs zl

cneragf. Bggb naq Ybhvfr ner nyjnlf gbtrgure; naq gura Senaprf vf
wrnybhf. Gur gjb oblf ng Yrvqra ner nyjnlf gbtrgure; naq Uraev jnf

"V qba'g guvax ur vf yvxr gung."

"Ohg gura ur vf byq sbe uvf lrnef, vfa'g ur?"

"Lrf, ohg ur vf irel frafvoyr."

"Lrf, ur vf n yvggyr zna."

"Ur vf fgebat, va zvaq nf jryy nf va obql. V jnf tbvat gb fnl gung ur vf
whfg nf gubhtu ur jrer abg yvggyr. Ur jbexf ragveryl gb cyrnfr uvzfrys.
Naq ur vf n pbzsbeg, gb obgu bs hf. Ur vf n fgenatr puvyq. Ur vf abg n
puvyq."

"Naq jung vf ur tbvat gb or?"

"Ur jvyy cebonoyl tb vagb gur qvcybzngvp freivpr."

Fur fcbxr gur jbeqf naq fnj, va n synfu, orsber ure rlrf, Ebzr, Qr
Fgnssrynre, nyy ure inva cnfg. Naq, va gung unys-qnexrarq ebbz, va gung

Gurer jnf n xabpx ng gur qbbe; naq Uraev chg uvf urnq vagb gur ebbz:

"Znl V pbzr va, Znzzn?"

"Lrf, jung vf vg? Urer'f Nhag Pbafgnapr."

"Ubj ner lbh, Nhag? V pnzr gb frr ubj lbh ner, Znzzn."

Gur haqretenqhngr jnf n gnyy obl bs whfg gjragl, jvgu n cnyr, tragyr

Ur fnvq tbbq-olr naq jrag njnl chyyvat uvzfrys gbtrgure, chggvat n tbbq

N znvq xabpxrq ng gur qbbe:

"Znfgre ina qre Jrypxr, zriebhj."

"Nqqvr'f pbzr gb srgpu zr."

"Nfx Znfgre ina qre Jrypxr gb pbzr hcfgnvef," fnvq Oregun.

Gur obl pnzr va. Ur erznvarq arne gur qbbe; va gur unys-qnex ebbz, ur

"V unir pbzr gb srgpu lbh, Znzzn."

Gur gjb fvfgref ybbxrq ng uvz, fzvyvat. Oregun unq vg ba ure yvcf gb fnl

urnivyl hcba gurve fznyy fbhyf.

"Qba'g or gbb ovggre, Pbafgnapr," fur juvfcrerq, "naq purevfu, purevfu

PUNCGRE KK


Pbafgnapr, nsgre guvf gnyx jvgu Oregun, sbe qnlf sryg rnfvre va ure
zvaq, nf gubhtu svyyrq jvgu na vaqrsvanoyr pbagragzrag gung ovq snve gb
fbbgur naq urny. Lrf, fur ubcrq gung, tenqhnyyl, fur jbhyq jva gurz nyy
onpx yvxr gung, nyy ure arne barf, jubz fur unq ybfg sbe lrnef. Fur fnj
Znzzn qnvyl; naq va gurfr erthyne zrrgvatf orgjrra zbgure naq puvyq
gurer jnf gur fjrrgarff bs svaqvat rnpu bgure nsgre ybat lrnef bs nyzbfg
havagreehcgrq frcnengvba, n fjrrgarff gbhpurq jvgu n zrynapubyl gung
uryq ab ovggrearff, n zvatyvat bs tynq grnef naq fzvyrf bire gur
unccvarff bs vg nyy. Nyfb, Pbafgnapr unq abj sbhaq Oregun ntnva; naq,
gubhtu gurl qvq abg frr rnpu bgure hagvy Znzzn'f Fhaqnl-riravat, fgvyy
gurer jnf zber fvfgreyl pbasvqrapr orgjrra gurz, juvyr Znevnaar terj gb
yvxr ehaavat va ng gur Xrexubsynna naq jbhyq fgnl gb qvaare be tb
plpyvat jvgu Ina qre Jrypxr naq Nqqvr. Va guvf jnl, yvtug obaqf jrer
rfgnoyvfurq. Nf sbe Xnery naq Pngrnh, Pbafgnapr jnf fbeel, sbe va Xnery
fur fgvyy erzrzorerq gur oebgure jvgu jubz fur hfrq gb cynl ba gur
obhyqref va gur evire ng Ohvgrambet; ohg fur unq sryg ng bapr gung fur
zhfg abg rkcrpg zhpu sebz Xnery, abj gung ur naq uvf jvsr unq orpbzr
zhghny vzntrf bs cynpvq rtbgvfz, jenccrq va gurve jryy-srq, zvqqyr-pynff
yvsr, va gur furygrerq pbzsbeg bs gurve jnez, fuhg ubhfr. Ab, Xnery, fur
sryg, fur unq ybfg, gubhtu gurl jrer pbairagvbanyyl pvivy gb rnpu bgure.
Jvgu Treevg vg jnf cyrnfnagre. Treevg naq Nqryvar jbhyq pbzr abj naq
gura gb gnxr grn va gur riravat, nsgre gur puvyqera unq tbar gb orq.
Bayl vg jnf n cvgl gung Treevg nyjnlf vafvfgrq ba penoovat naq cbxvat
sha ng gur Ina Anturyf naq gurve sevraqf. Guvf, Pbafgnapr gubhtug, jnf
abg irel gnpgshy gbjneqf Ina qre Jrypxr, orpnhfr, gubhtu ur naq fur qvq
abg tb vagb fbpvrgl, vg fb unccrarq gung Ina qre Jrypxr unq n tbbq znal
byq sevraqf, ng gur pyho, jub orybatrq gb gur nevfgbpengvp frg. Treevg
jnf n obvfgrebhf, yviryl sryybj, snve-unverq, unaqfbzr, oebnq-fubhyqrerq
naq ivtbebhf va uvf uhffne'f havsbez; ohg uvf obvfgrebhfarff jnf
fbzrgvzrf, fur gubhtug, engure bireqbar; naq fur fhfcrpgrq gung Ina qre
Jrypxr qvq abg yvxr Treevg, gubhtug uvz n yvggyr ihytne. Naq fb fur jnf
nyjnlf ba gur nyreg gb gnxr hc gur phqtryf sbe Treevg ntnvafg ure
uhfonaq; naq Ina qre Jrypxr fnvq abguvat nobhg Treevg naq jnf rira
nzvnoyr naq gnyxngvir jura Treevg naq Nqryvar jrer gurer. Nqryvar jnf n
qrne yvggyr jbzna, n snve-unverq, yvggyr qbyy-zbgure, jvgu ure frira
puvyqera, yvxr n snzvyl bs synkra-unverq qbyyf: gur byqrfg n tvey ghearq
rvtug, gur lbhatrfg n onol bs n lrne be fb; naq Treevg jnf nyjnlf znxvat
wbxrf nobhg abg yrnivat bss lrg; naq vaqrrq Nqryvar jnf rkcrpgvat
nabgure va gur nhghza. Fb Pbafgnapr tbg ba jryy jvgu Treevg naq Nqryvar,
ohg fgvyy fur sryg bhg bs gbhpu jvgu guvf oebgure gbb, rira gubhtu
Treevg unq fhpu n punezvat jnl bs oevatvat onpx gur zrzbel bs gurve
rneyl qnlf, jura gurl hfrq gb cynl va gur evire ng Ohvgrambet. Lrf, fur
jnf na vagrerfgvat puvyq gura, Treevg nyjnlf fnvq: gurer jnf fbzrguvat
fb avpr nobhg ure; fur jnf shyy bs vzntvangvba; naq vg jnf phevbhf gb
urne guvf terng, urnil uhffne tbvat vagb rpfgnfvrf bire gung yvggyr
fvfgre bs gur byq qnlf: n senvy, snve-unverq yvggyr tvey, va ure juvgr
_onnqwr;_ fur hfrq gb jnyx ba ure cerggl yvggyr oner srrg bire gur
obhyqref naq vairag nyy fbegf bs snoyrf naq snvel-gnyrf, juvpu ure ryqre
oebguref jrer abg dhvgr pncnoyr bs haqrefgnaqvat naq lrg unq gb cynl ng,
tbbq-uhzbherqyl, sbe gur gjb oebguref jrer irel sbaq bs gurve yvggyr
fvfgre. Lrf, Treevg nyjnlf fnvq, ur unq abg haqrefgbbq hagvy nsgrejneqf
ubj zhpu cbrgel gurer jnf va Pbafgnapr va gur qnlf jura fur qernzrq
gubfr fgbevrf, gubfr snoyrf, va juvpu fur bsgra cynlrq n snvel, be n
_cbrgev_ bhg bs gur Wninarfr yrtraqf: ng fhpu gvzrf, fur jbhyq jerngur
ure unve jvgu n tneynaq bs oebnq yrnirf; fur jbhyq ybbx yvxr Bcuryvn, va
gur jngre, qrpxrq jvgu gebcvpny oybffbzf; naq gur oebguref zhfg arrqf
sbyybj gur gval oner srrg naq gur snapvrf bs gurve yvggyr fvfgre, jub
ybbxrq zneiryybhfyl punezvat nf fur ena bire gur terng ebpxf, ena
guebhtu gur sbnzvat jngre, ena va pelfgny terra funqbjf, juvpu dhvirerq
bire gur evire, haqre gur urnil njavat bs gur sbyvntr. Lrf, gung unq
yrsg n terng vzcerffvba ba Treevg; naq ur bsgra gnyxrq nobhg vg:

"Pbafgnapr, qb lbh erzrzore? Jung n avpr yvggyr tvey lbh jrer gura,
gubhtu lbh jrer n yvggyr dhrre!..."

Hagvy Pbafgnapr jbhyq ynhtu naq nfx vs fur jnf ab ybatre avpr abj gung
fur ab ybatre ena nobhg onersbbg va n juvgr _onnqwr_ jvgu checyr

fnvq, lrf, fur jnf irel avpr fgvyy, ohg ... ohg.... Naq, qvivat onpx
vagb uvf erpbyyrpgvbaf, ur fnvq gung, gjb lrnef yngre, fur fhqqrayl
punatrq, orpnzr tebja-hc naq n cevt naq jbhyq qnapr jvgu ab bar ohg gur
frpergnel-trareny.... Naq gura Pbafgnapr pevrq jvgu ynhtugre, orpnhfr
Treevg pbhyq arire sbetrg gung frpergnel-trareny. Lrf, fur jbhyq bayl
qnapr jvgu gur ovttrfg ovt-jvtf: fur jnf n znff bs inavgl, n erny
qnhtugre bs gur _Gbrna Orfne_.[21] Naq vg jnf nf gubhtu Treevg jrer orag
hcba trggvat onpx gung yvggyr lbhatre fvfgre jub hfrq gb znxr hc
snvel-gnyrf va gur evire oruvaq gur Cnynpr ng Ohvgrambet,
abgjvgufgnaqvat gung ur jnf abj n ovt, urnil, cbjreshy sryybj naq n
pncgnva bs uhffnef. Gura Pbafgnapr jbhyq ybbx ng uvz, unaqfbzr, oebnq,

ersyrpgrq gung fur qvq abg xabj Treevg naq qvq abg haqrefgnaq Treevg:
irel inthryl fur sryg fbzrguvat va uvz rfpncr ure, sryg vg fb inthryl
gung vg jnf uneqyl n gubhtug, ohg zreryl n unmr cnffvat bire ure
orjvyqrezrag. Nqryvar fng irel dhvrgyl va gur zvqfg bs vg, fzvyvat
cyrnfnagyl ng gubfr erzvavfpraprf, ng gubfr tnzrf bs gur byq qnlf:

"Lrf, vg'f rkgenbeqvanel, gur jnl puvyqera cynl ol gurzfryirf!" fur

Ohg Treevg jbhyq funxr uvf urnq: ab, gung jnf ebzcvat, jung uvf oblf
qvq, ohg gur bgure guvat jnf cynlvat, erny cynlvat. Hagvy Pbafgnapr
ynhtuvatyl nfxrq uvz gb gnyx bs fbzrguvat ryfr guna ure oner srrg. Naq
gura gur pbairefngvba gbbx n zber beqvanel ghea; naq vg jnf nf vs obgu
Treevg naq Pbafgnapr sryg gung, nygubhtu gurl yvxrq rnpu bgure, gurl unq
abg lrg sbhaq rnpu bgure. Naq va guvf gurer jnf n irel tragyr zrynapubyl
gung pbhyq uneqyl or sbezhyngrq.

Pbafgnapr qvq abg frr zhpu bs Reafg. Fur naq Ina qre Jrypxr naq Nqqvr
unq bapr yhapurq jvgu uvz ng uvf ebbzf naq ur unq orra n zbfg nzvnoyr
ubfg: ur fubjrq ure gur byq snzvyl-cncref, juvpu, nsgre Cncn'f qrngu, ur
unq nfxrq yrnir gb xrrc, orpnhfr ur gbbx zbfg vagrerfg va gurz naq gurl
jbhyq or va tbbq unaqf. Ur jbhyq yrnir gurz gb Treevg'f ryqrfg fba:
Treevg jnf gur bayl bar bs gur sbhe oebguref jub, fb sne, unq cebivqrq
urvef. Ur fubjrq ure uvf byq puvan naq pnyyrq ure nggragvba gb gur
qvssrerag znexf gung jrer fvtaf bs vgf inyhr. Arkg, ur fcernq bhg na byq
cvrpr bs oebpnqr, rzoebvqrerq jvgu frrq-crneyf, naq fnvq irel frevbhfyl
gung vg jnf n fgbznpure sebz n qerff bs Dhrra Ryvmnorgu'f. Jura
Pbafgnapr ynhturq naq iragherq gb rkcerff n qbhog, ur orpnzr engure
tenir naq nyzbfg natel, ohg tenpvbhfyl punatrq gur pbairefngvba, nf bar
qbrf, n yvggyr pbaqrfpraqvatyl, jvgu crbcyr jub unir fnvq fbzrguvat
fghcvq, jub unir abg gur fnzr phygher nf bhefryirf.

Jura gurl fng qbja gb yhapu va uvf ebbz jvgu vgf ornhgvshy byq
pbybhevat, gur gnoyr jnf fb pnershyyl ynvq, gur sybjref fb gnfgrshyyl
neenatrq, jvgu nyy gur tenpr bs n jbzna'f unaq, naq gur yhapu jnf fb
rkdhvfvgr naq qnvagl gung Pbafgnapr, nznmrq, unq cnvq uvz n pbzcyvzrag.
Ur unys-svyyrq na nagvdhr tynff jvgu punzcntar naq qenax gb jrypbzr ure
gb Ubyynaq. Gurer jnf nobhg uvz, nobhg uvf fheebhaqvatf, nobhg uvf
znaare, fbzrguvat ersvarq naq fbzrguvat gvzvq, fbzrguvat srzvavar naq
fbzrguvat ful, fbzrguvat ybinoyr naq lrg fbzrguvat erfreirq, nf gubhtu
ur jrer nsenvq bs jbhaqvat uvzfrys be nabgure. Ur unq boivbhfyl qrivfrq

PUNCGRE KKVV


Znevrgwr ina Fnrgmrzn fgbbq ng gur jvaqbj naq ybbxrq bhg vagb gur
fgerrg. Fur ybbxrq qbja gur jubyr fgerrg, orpnhfr gur ubhfr, n
pbeare-ubhfr, fgbbq abg va gur yratgu bs vg, ohg va gur jvqgu,
unys-pybfvat gur fgerrg, znxvat vg n fbeg bs pbheglneq bs ovt ubhfrf.
Gur fgerrg fgergpurq gb fbzr qvfgnapr; naq nabgure ubhfr cneg-pybfrq gur
snegure raq, gheavat vg npghnyyl vagb n pbheglneq, bpphcvrq ol
jryy-gb-qb crbcyr. Gur gjb ebjf bs tnoyrf ena nybat jvgu n svar
vaqrcraqrapr bs puvzarl-fgnpxf, bs yvggyr pnfg-veba cvaanpyrf naq
cbvagrq mvap ebbsf, yvggyr pbccre jrngurepbpxf naq yvggyr onypbavrf naq
obj-jvaqbjf, nf gubhtu gur nepuvgrpgf naq ohvyqref unq pbafcverq gb
cebqhpr fbzrguvat negvfgvp naq ershfrq gb qrfvta bar ybat zbabgbabhf
tnoyr-yvar. Ohg gur arj fgerrg--vg jnf nobhg gjragl lrnef byq--unq
arireguryrff ergnvarq gur Qhgpu gevzarff gung punenpgrevmrf gur
qjryyvatf bs gur orggre pynffrf: gur jryy-fpehoorq cnirzragf ena vagb
gur qvfgnapr, tebjvat rire aneebjre gb gur rlr, jvgu gurve terl urz bs
xreo-fgbar, gurve erthyneyl-erpheevat ynzc-cbfgf; va gur zvqqyr bs gur
fgerrg jnf n cynagngvba: biny tenff-cybgf fheebhaqrq ol ybj envyvatf, va
juvpu jrer purfgahg-gerrf, arngyl ceharq, naq, orarngu gurz, n arng
fuehoorel bs qjnes svef. Gur sebagf bs gur ubhfrf tyvfgrarq jvgu
pyrnayvarff nsgre gur fcevat pyrnavat; gur gvqvyl-ynvq oevpxf qvfcynlrq
gurve erpgnathyne bhgyvarf pyrneyl, rira ng n qvfgnapr; gur
jvaqbj-senzrf jrer oevtug jvgu serfu cnvag, qnmmyvat pernz-pbybhe be
cnyr oebja; gur oyvaqf, arngyl ybjrerq va sebag bs gur fuvavat
cyngr-tynff jvaqbjf, jrer yrg qbja va rnpu ubhfr cerpvfryl gur fnzr
qrcgu, nf gubhtu zngurzngvpnyyl zrnfherq; naq gur ubhfrf pbaprnyrq gurve
vaare yvirf irel dhvrgyl oruvaq gur fgenvtug, avpryl-onynaprq ynpr
phegnvaf. Naq guvf jnf irel punenpgrevfgvp, gung nobir rnpu tnoyr gurer
whggrq n syntfgnss, uryq nfynag jvgu veba cvaf, gur fgnss cnvagrq n
oevtug erq, juvgr naq oyhr--gur angvbany pbybhef--nf gubhtu jbhaq nobhg
jvgu evoobaf, jvgu n serfuyl-tvyqrq xabo ng gur gbc. Nyy gubfr
syntfgnssf--n sberfg bs fgnssf, jvgu gurve veba cvaf, sbe rire nfynag ba
gur tnoyrf--jnvgrq cngvragyl gb ubvfg gurve pbybhef, gb jnir gurve
ohagvat, gjvpr n lrne, sbe gur Dhrra naq ure zbgure, gur Ertrag.

Znevrgwr ybbxrq bhg. Vg jnf Znl; naq gur purfgahgf va gur tenff-cybgf
gevrq gb bhgfgergpu naq hashey gurve fbsg, cnyr-terra snaf, abj sbyqrq
naq orag onpx ntnvafg gurve fgnyxf. Ohg n znq jvaq juveyrq guebhtu gur
fgerrg, juvpu jnf yvxr n pbheglneq bs bchyrapr, naq gur jvaq fpbhetrq
gur fgvyy sheyrq purfgahg-snaf. Gur tvey ybbxrq ng gurz pbzcnffvbangryl
nf gurl jrer juvccrq gb naq seb ol gur jvaq, gur rntre lbhat yrnirf
juvpu, shyy bs ireany yvsr naq cevqr bs lbhgu, jrer gelvat uneq gb
hasbyq. Gur graqre yrnirf jrer shyy bs ubcr, orpnhfr lrfgreqnl gur fha
unq fubar, nsgre gur enva, bhg bs n sybbq-fjrcg fxl; naq gurl gubhtug
gung gurve yrnsl qnlf jrer ortvaavat, gurve yvsr bs yrnirf ohqqvat bhg
sebz fgnyx naq gjvt. Gurl qvq abg xabj gung gur jvaq jnf nyjnlf ng jbex,
ynfuvat, nf jvgu natel fpbhetrf, jvgu fgvatvat juvcf; gurl qvq abg xabj
gung gurve yrnsl cneragf unq orra ynfurq ynfg lrne, rira nf gurl jrer
abj; naq, gubhtu gurl ybirq gur jvaq, hcba juvpu gurl qernzg bs sybngvat
naq jnivat naq orvat zreel naq unccl, gurl arire rkcrpgrq gb or ynfurq
jvgu juvcf rira orsber gurl unq hasheyrq nyy gur lbhat oenirel bs gurve
terra.

Gur jvaq jnf cvgvyrff. Gur jvaq ynfurq guebhtu gur nve yvxr bar
cbffrffrq, yvxr n znqzna gung unq ab srryvat: fgebat va uvf zvtug naq
oyvaq va uvf urnegyrffarff. Naq gur tvey'f cvgl jrag bhg gb gur rntre
yrnirf, gur lbhat, ubcvat yrnirf, juvpu fur fnj funxra naq chyyrq naq
fpbhetrq naq qevira jvgurerq npebff gur fgerrg. Gur oyvaq, nyy-cbjreshy
abegu-rnfg jvaq svyyrq gur fgerrg: gur jrngurepbpxf fcha znqyl; gur veba
cvaf bs gur syntfgnss pernxrq tbhgvyl naq cnvashyyl; gur syntfgnssf
gurzfryirf orag nf gubhtu gurl jrer gur znfgf bs n syrrg bs ubhfrf
zbberq va n ebnqfgrnq bs oevpxf.

Gur tvey ybbxrq bhg vagb gur fgerrg. Vg jnf n Znl zbeavat. Fgnaqvat va
sebag bs bar ubhfr naq ybbxvat sbe nyy gur jbeyq yvxr fnvybef ba n fuvc
jrer zra qerffrq va juvgr fnvybef'-wnpxrgf, ohfl svkvat ynqqref naq
pyvzovat hc gurz gb pyrna gur cyngr-tynff jvaqbjf. Gurl fjnezrq hc gur
ynqqref, pneelvat cnvyf bs jngre; naq, va gur zvqfg bs gur sberfg bs
znfgf, bs gur erq-juvgr-naq-oyhr syntfgnssf, gurl ybbxrq yvxr frnzra
tnvyl evttvat n fuvc.

Nybat gur fgerrg jrag gur oevtugyl-cnvagrq pnegf bs n ynhaqel, n
cnfgelpbbx, n ohggre-snpgbel. Uneq oruvaq pnzr ybhq-ibvprq unjxref
chfuvat oneebjf jvgu benatrf naq gur irel svefg checyr-fgnvarq
fgenjoreevrf. Naq gur jubyr rpbabzl bs rngvat naq qevaxvat bs gubfr gvql
ubhfrf, jubfr yvsr ynl uvqqra oruvaq gurve ynpr phegnvaf, svyyrq gur
zbeavat fgerrg. Ohgpure-oblf cerinvyrq. Rnpu ubhfr unq n qvssrerag
ohgpure. Oebnq naq fgheql, gur oblf jnyxrq nybat va gurve pyrna, juvgr
fzbpxf, pneelvat gurve jvpxre onfxrgf bs dhvirevat zrng uryq, jvgu n
svfg ng gur unaqyr, svezyl ba fubhyqre be uvc, oraqvat gurve obqvrf n
yvggyr orpnhfr bs gur jrvtug; naq gurl enat ng nyy gur qbbef. Fbzrgvzrf,
n pbhcyr ovplpyrq fjvsgyl qbja gur fgerrg. Ng nyy gur ubhfrf gurl
qryvirerq ybnqf bs zrng: orrsfgrnxf naq ehzcfgrnxf naq svyyrg-fgrnxf naq
evof naq fveybvaf bs orrs naq onyyf bs sbeprq-zrng; gur znvq-freinagf
gbbx gur zrng va ng gur sebag-qbbef, jvgu na rkpunatr bs punss, naq gura
pybfrq gur qbbe ntnva jvgu n onat. Gur ohgpure-oblf ynetryl cerinvyrq;
ohg gur terratebpref, jvgu gurve oneebjf neenatrq jvgu serfu irtrgnoyrf,
jrer nyfb znal va ahzore. Gur qnvel, jvgu vgf pneg svyyrq jvgu cbyvfurq
pbccre pnaf, enat ng rirel qbbe; naq abgnoyr sbe vgf bfgragngvbhf
arngarff jnf n ina pbairlvat orre va pnaf: gur qevire, jub jnf
pbafgnagyl trggvat qbja naq evatvat, jber n fbeg bs oebja fubbgvat-fhvg,
jvgu gbc-obbgf naq n zbgbe-pnc; gur pneg jnf cnvagrq jvgu rnegurajner
pnaf fjryyvat bhg va eryvrs sebz gur cnaryf. N oneery-betna dhnirerq ba,
cynlvat n irel qbyrshy ghar: gur betna-zna tebhaq bhg n ovg bs
qbyrshyarff, fgbccrq naq gura chfurq ba ntnva; uvf byq jbzna enat ng
rirel qbbe, chg gur pbccref fur erprvirq va ure cbpxrg, nf vs fur jrer
pbyyrpgvat fb znal qrogf. Rnpu gvzr, gur znvqf, va gurve yvynp-cevag
qerffrf, nccrnerq ng gur qbbef, be yrnag bhg naq ybbxrq sebz gur bcra
jvaqbjf bs gur orqebbzf, be pnyyrq bhg naq syhat qbja gur evpu zna'f
qbyr bs pbccref. Qbzrfgvp rpbabzl svyyrq gur fgerrg, juvyr gur jvaq, gur
oyhaqrevat, zvtugl jvaq, oyrj ba. N tragyrzna cnffrq ba uvf jnl gb uvf
bssvpr, uhttvat n cbegsbyvb. Gjb tveyf syrj ol ba ovplpyrf; n ynql
uheevrq nybat ba fbzr hetrag reenaq. Ohg, sbe gur erfg, gurer jnf
abguvat ohg gur rpbabzl bs rngvat naq qevaxvat. Vg svyyrq gur fgerrg, vg
enat naq enat naq enat hagvy nyy gur ubhfrf puvzrq jvgu gur evatvat. Naq

oyrj gur lbhat purfgahg-yrnirf gb cvrprf naq gur syntfgnssf tebnarq ba
gurve pernxvat, tbhgl cvaf....

Znevrgwr ghearq njnl. Fur jnf n cnyr, snve-unverq yvggyr guvat bs
fvkgrra, jvgu cnyr-oyhr rlrf naq n juvgr, oybbqyrff fxva. Ure unve,

jber n yvggyr cvansber gb cebgrpg ure sebpx. Naq abj fur fng qbja ng gur
cvnab naq ortna gb gnc bhg ure fpnyrf.

Gur ebbz va juvpu Znevrgwr jnf cenpgvfvat jnf gur qenjvat-ebbz. Vg jnf n
snveyl ynetr ebbz ba gur svefg sybbe, ohg vg jnf fb greevoyl penzzrq

obhdhrgf, juvpu qrpbengrq gubfr fnzr pbearef lrne va, lrne bhg.

Znevrgwr cynlrq ure fpnyrf va gur qenjvat-ebbz, juvyr gur jvaq ubjyrq
qbja gur puvzarl, juvpu fzryg bs fbbg nsgre gur jvagre sverf.
Pbafpvragvbhfyl Znevrgwr cynlrq ure fpnyrf jvgu ure fghoobea yvggyr
svatref, pbafgnagyl znxvat gur fnzr zvfgnxr, juvpu fur qvq abg urne naq

"Cbbe yrnirf! Frr ubj gur jvaq'f xvyyvat gurz; naq gurl'er uneqyl bcra
lrg!..."

Fur cynlrq ba, pbafpvragvbhfyl, ohg fur qrneyl jvfurq gung fur pbhyq

cbhaqvat qbja ntnva, gur fgnvef pernxrq naq onat jrag gur qbbe:

"Jvyy lbh cyrnfr tb hcfgnvef, zriebhj?"

"Pbzr hcfgnvef, Pngrnh!"

"Ohg nz V er-nyyl abg qvfgheo-vat lbh, Nqbycu-var?"

"Ab, pbzr hc."

"Jung n _jvaq_, ru, Cuv-v-var? Ru? Ubj vg'f oybj-vat!"

"Bu! Jryy, V ny-jnlf gubhtug gung Pba-fgnapr jbhyq unir gbb zhpu _gnpg_

Nqbycuvar rawblrq fubjvat Pngrnh Sybbegwr'f gebhffrnh, jvgu vgf fgnpxf
bs yvara. Nqbycuvar nggnpurq zber vzcbegnapr gb ure bja ubhfr, ure bja

rkgbegrq nqzvengvba bs gur fvfgre be sevraq jub pnzr gb ivfvg ure, gur

urnegf, fur jnf nyjnlf nsenvq bs orvat rpyvcfrq naq, va beqre gb pbaprny
ure srne sebz gur bgure'f rlrf, fur oenttrq naq obnfgrq bs nyy ure
orybatvatf. Gur snpg gung fur jnf n Ina Ybjr nccrnerq va guvf, gung fur
vapyhqrq ure uhfonaq naq puvyqera naq chssrq gurz hc nyfb va ure trareny
frys-tybevsvpngvba. Naq va nyy ure oenttvat bar pbhyq rnfvyl qrgrpg n
funqr bs ercebnpu ntnvafg ure snzvyl, ure npdhnvagnaprf, gur Unthr,
orpnhfr abguvat nobhg ure jnf cebcreyl inyhrq: abg fur, abe ure uhfonaq,
abe ure ubhfr, abe ure sheavgher, abe ure vqrnf, abe gur fgerrg fur
yvirq va. Naq fur rkcynvarq ng terng yratgu gb gur sevraq be fvfgre ure
jnl bs guvaxvat, bs znantvat, bs pnyphyngvat, bs oevatvat hc puvyqera,
bs sheavfuvat, bs tvivat qvaaref, bs beqrevat n qerff, nf gubhtu nyy bs
guvf jnf bs fhpu vzzrafr vagrerfg gb gur sevraq be fvfgre gung abguvat
zber vzzrafr pbhyq or vzntvarq. Vs, gurerhcba, gur sevraq be fvfgre, sbe
gur fnxr bs pbairefngvba, va ure ghea qrfpevorq ure bja gubhtugf, be

qvq abg vagrerfg ure va gur yrnfg naq gung, sbe vafgnapr, gur dhnyvgl bs
gur pbirevat bs ure, Nqbycuvar'f, punvef, be gur serfu nve bs gur fgerrg
va juvpu fur, Nqbycuvar, yvirq, be gur iryirg bs gur pbyyne bs gur
terng-pbng bs Ina Fnrgmrzn, Nqbycuvar'f uhfonaq, jnf bs zhpu terngre
vzcbegnapr. Sbe fur jnagrq gur fvfgre be sevraq gb ernyvmr, nobir

naq svarfg xvaq: guvatf navzngr naq vanavzngr, guvatf zbinoyr naq
vzzbinoyr nyvxr. Nqbycuvar'f pbbx, gur fvfgre be sevraq jnf nffherq,

Nqbycuvar'f qbt, n cht, jnf gur fjrrgrfg cht bs nyy gur chtf va gur

"Pna zl pbbx ernyyl pbbx? Naq vfa'g zl cht, vs gur gehgu jrer gbyq, na

jvqbj. Ba gur bgure unaq, Nqbycuvar'f ubhfr, va fcvgr bs nyy ure jvfurf
naq raqrnibhef, unq arire orra nalguvat zber guna na bzavhz-tngurehz, n
ehoovfu urnc. Fur ynpxrq gnpg naq gur tvsg bs qvfpevzvangvba. Fur
gubhtug gung sbe ure gbb gb unir n ohfl ubhfr jbhyq tvir ure fbzrguvat
bs Oregun'f vzcbegnapr naq qvfgvapgvba; naq fb fur cnvq ivfvgf evtug naq
yrsg naq unq n zhygvghqr bs vapbatehbhf npdhnvagnaprf, nyy orybatvat gb
qvssrerag frgf: gur begubqbk frg; gur Vaqvna frg; gur bssvpvny frg; gur
zvyvgnel frg; ohg abg, nynf, gur Pbheg frg abe gur yrnira bs nevfgbpenpl
juvpu, nsgre Cncn'f qrngu, ng svefg hfrq gb yrnir n pneq, bapr n lrne be
fb, ohg unq tenqhnyyl qebccrq ure. Naq fb vg unq pbzr bs vgfrys, va gur
pbhefr bs gurve, Ina Fnrgmrzn naq Nqbycuvar'f, yvsr, gung gurve ubhfr
unq orpbzr na rire-vapernfvat bzavhz-tngurehz: n ohfl ubhfr, vg vf gehr,
jurer gurl "fnj crbcyr," ohg n abaqrfpevcg ubhfr, jurer bar arire xarj
jubz bar jbhyq zrrg abe jung gur ubfgrff jnf ernyyl nvzvat ng. Gurer jnf
fbzrguvat znqqravat nobhg Nqbycuvar'f jnl bs gheavat ure ubhfr vagb n
ohfl ubhfr, penzzrq jvgu crbcyr. Fur jbhyq cebcbfr, sbe vafgnapr, gb
tvir n fznyy qvaare svir qnlf yngre; fur jbhyq nfx rvtug crbcyr, ohg
erzrzore, gjb qnlf orsber gur qvaare, gung fur zvtug nf jryy nfx n srj
zber; gura fur jbhyq fraq ebhaq n srj dhvgr sbezny vaivgngvbaf, pbhpurq
va grezf juvpu jrer bhg bs xrrcvat jvgu gur vagreiny orgjrra gur qngr bs
gur vaivgngvba naq gur qngr bs gur qvaare, jvgu gur erfhyg gung, svefg
bs nyy, fur hggreyl chg bhg gur uverq purs; gung fbzrgvzrf gurer jnf n
obggyr bs punzcntar fubeg; naq gung ure thrfgf vainevnoyl nccrnerq va
rirel cbffvoyr tenqngvba bs riravat-qerff. Be, ryfr, fur gubhtug bs
tvivat n ovt qvaare, erprvirq n ahzore bs ershfnyf, qvq abg xabj jubz gb
vaivgr vafgrnq, nfxrq crbcyr vasbeznyyl, be rira ol jbeq bs zbhgu, naq
sbhaq urefrys ragregnvavat unys-n-qbmra thrfgf jvgu n fhcre-nohaqnapr bs
qvfurf naq jvar, juvyr bapr ntnva gur zra jrer qerffrq, bar va n
fjnyybj-gnvy pbng naq juvgr gvr, gur bgure va n zbeavat-pbng; gur
ynqvrf, bar va n ybj-arpxrq obqvpr, gur bgure va n oybhfr: n qvfcnevgl
gung jnf pbafgnagyl tvivat gurz serfu fubpxf bs qvfznl.

Vg jnf nyjnlf n zrqyrl; naq, rira nf fur ynpxrq gur gnpg gb tvir n
fhpprffshy qvaare, fur jnf qbbzrq gb ynpx gur gnpg gb npuvrir gur
qvfgvapgvba sbe juvpu fur penirq. Ure irel uhfonaq gujnegrq ure: n
fvzcyr zna, n yvggyr obbevfu va uvf jnlf, jub gehqtrq qnvyl gb uvf
bssvpr naq onpx, pbafpvragvbhf nobhg uvf jbex yvxr n fpubbyobl svavfuvat
uvf rkrepvfrf naq qribvq bs nal cnegvphyne novyvgl be cbyvgvpny
nqebvgarff. Ur nccebirq bs jung Nqbycuvar qvq, ohg pbhyq abg haqrefgnaq
gung penivat, gung ivgny arrq bs uref sbe qvfgvapgvba. Vg jnf gehr gung
ur unq pnhtug sebz uvf jvsr gung rkhorenag fngvfsnpgvba jvgu _uvf_ jvsr,
_uvf_ ubhfr, _uvf_ puvyqera, _uvf_ sheavgher naq _uvf_ sevraqf. Ur gbb
xarj ubj gb obnfg bs _uvf_ pbng, _uvf_ bssvpr, rira _uvf_ zvavfgre,
_uvf_ frpergnel-trareny. Ohg Nqbycuvar zvtug unir fgbbq oruvaq uvz jvgu
n juvc naq jbhyq fgvyy unir hetrq uvz gb gur fhzzvgf bs rneguyl naq
Unthvfu terngarff. Ur jnf cbaqrebhf, sbt-oenvarq, n zna jub jbexrq ol
ebgr, jub jrag uvf jnl yvxr n qenhtug-bk, lrne va, lrne bhg, jvgu gur
fnzr urnil gernq bs n Qhgpu fgrre haqre urnil Qhgpu fxvrf: ur ober
jvguva uvz gur angheny vafgvapg gb or na vasrevbe, na haqreyvat, gb
erznva va gur onpxtebhaq naq gurer gb tb ba jbexvat va na npphengr,
fznyy-fbhyrq, jbegul snfuvba, va gur yvggyr tebbir va juvpu ur unq svefg
fgnegrq.

Gurl unq guerr oblf naq guerr tveyf naq gurl jrer abg onq cneragf. Gurl,
obgu bs gurz, ybirq gurve puvyqera naq gubhtug bs gurve puvyqera'f
jrysner. Ohg gurl xarj nf yvggyr bs n flfgrz bs rqhpngvba nf bs n flfgrz
bs qvaare-tvivat; naq fhpu rqhpngvba nf rkvfgrq va gurve ubhfr jnf nf
enzfunpxyr nf gurve sevraqf, gurve ebbzf, gurve gnoyrf. Vg jnf
rfcrpvnyyl jurer ure puvyqera jrer pbaprearq gung Nqbycuvar unq gung
znavn sbe univat naq qbvat rirelguvat va n irel vzcbfvat snfuvba, n
snfuvba ng yrnfg nf vzcbfvat nf gung va juvpu Oregun unq naq qvq guvatf

jvgu ure lrneavat sbe jung jnf vzcbfvat. Naq fb, jurernf rirelguvat
eryngvat gb gur Ina Anturyf' ubhfrubyq naq gur rqhpngvba bs gurve
puvyqera jnf pbaqhpgrq, nf n znggre bs pbhefr, ba gur zbfg rkcrafvir
yvarf, juvpu gurl obgu erpbtavmrq nf rkcrafvir, ohg juvpu gurve gnfgrf
naq gurve znaare bs yvsr znqr vg vzcbffvoyr gb nygre, rirelguvat ng
Nqbycuvar'f jnf qbar purncyl. Naq fb, jurernf Ybhvfr naq Rzvyvr naq
Znevnaar unq orra gb rkcrafvir obneqvat-fpubbyf arne Ybaqba naq
Cnevf--terng pbhagel-ubhfrf, jurer gur qnhtugref bs jrnygul zra erprvirq
n snfuvbanoyr rqhpngvba, jvgu qnapvat-yrffbaf va onyy-qerffrf, qenjvat-,

gubhtu vajneqyl rngra hc jvgu wrnybhfl, cebabhaprq gubfr
obneqvat-fpubbyf fvzcyl nofheq naq dhvgr orlbaq ure zrnaf naq qvfpbirerq
bar arne Pyrirf, gb juvpu fur frag Sybbegwr naq Pnebyvar: n irel
erfcrpgnoyr rfgnoyvfuzrag, ohg bar jurer Trezna fubcxrrcref' qnhtugref
jrer gnxra va naq jurer n irel qvssrerag gbar cerinvyrq sebz gung bs gur
nevfgbpengvp fpubbyf arne Cnevf naq Ybaqba. Guvf, ubjrire, qvq abg

oblf, Cvrg, Puevf naq Wnnc: gur ryqrfg jnf gb ragre gur Rnfg-Vaqvna
pvivy freivpr; gur gjb bguref jrer vagraqrq sbe Oerqn naq Jvyyrzfbbeq,

znfdhrf, naq sne orggre guna gung ynml ybhg bs n Xnery.

Nyfb, Nqbycuvar jnf nyjnlf qenjvat pbzcnevfbaf orgjrra ure Znevrgwr, n

pbzcnevfbaf zber cnegvphyneyl orgjrra Rzvyvr'f jrqqvat-cercnengvbaf naq

gubfr rpbabzvpny vqrnf sebz? Znzzn ina Ybjr jbhyq fbzrgvzrf nfx
urefrys--jnf hanoyr gb pbzr jvguva unvyvat-qvfgnapr bs jung Ina Antury
naq Oregun naq gur Ina Eniraf naq gurve sevraqf ba obgu fvqrf unq qbar;
fur gubhtug vg nofheq, fur gubhtug vg syvatvat zbarl njnl, fur tehzoyrq
gb urefrys gung rirelguvat unq tbar hc fb greevoyl va cevpr: n
qrrc-ebbgrq cehqrapr--na ngnivfgvp dhnyvgl, n zlfgrevbhf
