sybjref jvgu juvpu Rzvyvr'f jrqqvat-qnlf unq tyvggrerq; fur gubhtug vg
evqvphybhf, fur jnagrq gb qb rirelguvat zber rpbabzvpnyyl naq lrg fur
qvq abg yvxr qbvat rirelguvat fb rpbabzvpnyyl; naq fb gurer jnf na
vaprffnag fgehttyr, obgu jvgu urefrys naq jvgu Sybbegwr, jub nyfb qvq
abg jvfu gb or frpbaq gb Rzvyvr naq jub tnir ab gubhtug gb zbarl: vg jnf
bayl ure cneragf' zbarl! Ohg fgvyy, jvgu ure crphyvne tvsg bs
frys-tybevsvpngvba, Nqbycuvar jnf abj noyr gb cenvfr Sybbegwr'f
gebhffrnh gb Pngrnh nobir nyy gubfr ynpr sevccrevrf bs Rzvyvr'f.

"Zhpu av-pre naq zber ynfg-vat, _V_ guvax, Nqbycu-var!" juvarq Pngrnh.

"Lrf; naq whfg ybbx ng gubfr purzvfrf, ybbx ng gubfr gnoyr-pybguf naq
ancxvaf: gurer'f dhnyvgl gurer, lbh pna'g orng vg," fnvq Nqbycuvar,
cnggvat gur fgnpxf bs yvara va gur phcobneq. "Naq nyy gubfr fvyyl
cerfragf juvpu Rzvyvr unq, nyy gung fvyire, juvpu fur pna'g hfr: jung qb
lbhat crbcyr, jub bs pbhefr jba'g or frrvat crbcyr sbe gur svefg srj
lrnef, jnag jvgu fb zhpu fvyire? V'z irel tynq gung _bhe_ sevraqf unir
orra zber cenpgvpny va pubbfvat gurve cerfragf sbe Sybbegwr: _V_
fubhyqa'g unir orra ng nyy cyrnfrq vs Sybbegwr unq orra frg hc va ure
fvyire-phcobneq ol crbcyr jubz lbh znl pnyy npdhnvagnaprf, vs lbh yvxr,
ohg jub, nsgre nyy, ner fgenatref."

"Lr-r-rf," juvarq Pngrnh. "Ng Rzvyvr-gwr'f erprcgvba, vg ybbxrq whfg
yvxr Ina Xrz-cra'f fubc. V gubhtug vg fb ihy-tne naq pbz-zba, qvqa'g
_lbh_, Nqbycu-var?"

Gur rcvgurgf jrer abg rkprcgvbanyyl jryy-pubfra nf nccyvrq gb Ina Antury
naq Oregun--rira Nqbycuvar pbhyq frr gung--ohg fur nqzverq ure bja
chepunfrf naq _ure_ sevraqf' cerfragf gbb terngyl gb fnl fb gb Pngrnh.




PUNCGRE KKVI


Pbafgnapr znqr vg n qhgl gb tb bsgra gb Nqbycuvar'f qhevat Sybbegwr'f
jrqqvat-ceryvzvanevrf. Fur jrag bhg bs ure jnl gb or pbeqvny; fur frag n
ornhgvshy onfxrg bs sybjref ba gur qnl bs gur pbagenpg; fur tnir n
unaqfbzr cerfrag, zhpu zber rkcrafvir guna gur bar juvpu fur unq frag
Rzvyvr; naq fur fubjrq terng vagrerfg va gur cnegl naq gur qvaare gung
jrer gb or tvira ng gur Jvggr Oeht. Fur rknzvarq nggragviryl gur bcra
cerffrf jvgu gur fgnpxf bs yvara pbzcbfvat Sybbegwr'f gebhffrnh--"Whfg
ybbx ng gubfr purzvfrf; naq gubfr gnoyr-pybguf naq ancxvaf: gurer'f
dhnyvgl gurer, lbh pna'g orng vg. Whfg srry gurz, bayl srry gurz!
Jurernf gubfr sevccrevrf bs Rzvyvr'f...!"--naq yvfgrarq nggragviryl gb
gur raqyrff cqnaf bs frys-tybevsvpngvba, fcrag urefrys va nqzvengvba,
jnf qrgrezvarq gb synggre Nqbycuvar naq gb znxr n tbbq vzcerffvba ba ure
fvfgre. Orpnhfr, qhevat gubfr qnlf, fur unq pbafpvragvbhfyl frg urefrys
gur gnfx bs jvaavat bire Nqbycuvar, fur fjnyybjrq gur pevgvpvfz gung jnf
arire jnagvat, yvggyr fcvgrshy neebjf fubg bss va orgjrra gur cqnaf:

"Ubj cnyr lbh'er ybbxvat! Unir lbh orra hfvat gbb zhpu cbjqre ntnva, be
nera'g lbh jryy?... Jung n cvgl gung lbhe obl vf fhpu na byq tragyrzna,
Pbafgnapr!... Gryy zr, Pbafgnapr: lbhe sngure- naq zbgure-va-ynj jrer
abg irel avpr gb lbh, jrer gurl?... Pbafgnapr, ner gubfr evatf bs lbhef
erny?... Bu, ernyyl? Hcba zl jbeq, V gubhtug bar bs gubfr fgbarf jnf
cnfgr...."

Fur fjnyybjrq vg nyy, npprcgrq gur nssebag jvgu n tragyr fzvyr, n jbeq
bs nyzbfg nffragvat ercyl: "Lrf, Nqqvr vf engure byq-snfuvbarq.... Bu,
vg jnf irel qvssvphyg sbe Cncn naq Znzzn ina qre Jrypxr.... Lbh ner
evtug, gung fgbar vf n yvggyr qhyy fbzrgvzrf...."

Fur fjnyybjrq vg, gbbx vg nyy fb tragyl naq fb fhozvffviryl gung Nqqvr,
jura ur unccrarq gb or cerfrag, ybbxrq hc ng uvf zbgure va fhecevfr,
guvaxvat ure fb qvssrerag sebz gur jbzna jubz ur xarj, jub oynmrq bhg
sbe gur yrnfg guvat ng Cncn naq jub nyjnlf orunirq gbjneqf uvzfrys nf
gur fcbvyg yvggyr zbgure jub jnagrq gb or crggrq naq ybirq ol ure obl.
Naq gur ynq, va uvf fznyy, oevtug, rnearfg, qbhtugl fbhy, sryg n fbeg bs
nznmrzrag ng gung chmmyr bs n jbzna'f fbhy gung jnf uvf zbgure'f:

"Ner gurl nyy yvxr gung, fb dhrre? Be vf vg bayl Znzzn? Naq jul vf fur
fb sbeornevat gbjneqf Nhag Nqbycuvar, jura fur pna'g orne gur yrnfg
guvat sebz Cncn?"

Guvf znqr uvz fgvyy zber bs n yvggyr zna gbjneqf uvf zbgure, jvgu
fbzrguvat cebgrpgvat naq pbaqrfpraqvat, orpnhfr fur jnf fb jrnx naq
veerfbyhgr naq rkpvgnoyr, ohg nyfb jvgu irel zhpu gung jnf nssrpgvbangr,
orpnhfr gung fgenatr jbznayvarff cbffrffrq n punez sbe uvf fznyy znyr
fbhy.

Nqbycuvar, ubjrire, ba gur qnl jura gur pbagenpg jnf fvtarq, ng gur ovt
snzvyl-qvaare ng gur Jvggr Oeht naq gur fhofrdhrag riravat-cnegl sbe nyy
gur sevraqf naq eryngvbaf, obnfgrq nybhq va ure frys-pbzcynprapl. Fur
oenttrq gb Hapyr Ehliranre, gb Xnery naq Pngrnh, gb Pbafgnapr, gb Treevg
naq Nqryvar: _gubfr_ jrer svar ebbzf, gur ebbzf bs gur Jvggr Oeht, zhpu
svare guna gur ebbzf va gur Qbryra; gung jnf n fcyraqvq qvaare, gur
qvaare juvpu _fur_ unq tvira: vg pbfg n ybg bs zbarl, gubhtu, naq fur
gbyq ubj zhpu, ohg nqqrq n pbhcyr bs uhaqerq thvyqref gb gur pbfg; naq
qvq gurl erzrzore gung vzcbffvoyr qvaare bs Oregun'f, ng Rzvyvr'f
jrqqvat, naq gur dhrre qvfurf gung unq orra frg orsber gurz? Jnfa'g vg n
fcyraqvq qrffreg, jvgu ornhgvshy fgenjoreevrf, juvpu _fur_ unq tvira?
Naq fb _znal_ naq ng guvf frnfba, gbb: ohg lbh unq gb cnl sbe gurz! Naq
ubj tnl gurl unq orra ng gnoyr, _ure_ snzvyl--nf gubhtu gung fnzr snzvyl
jrer abg nyfb Oregun'f snzvyl--naq _ure_ sevraqf: fb irel qvssrerag sebz
gung cergragvbhf frg bs Oregun'f! Gurer jnf fhpu n tnl, fcbagnarbhf gbar
va gur fcrrpurf naq gur pbairefngvba; naq qvq Treevg erzrzore gung
qrnguyl fgvyyarff ng gnoyr ng Rzvyvrgwr'f qvaare? Fhpu avpr crbcyr,
Qvwxreubs'f cneragf, _ure_ tvey'f shgher sngure- naq zbgure-va-ynj....
Naq ubj jryy Sybbegwr ybbxrq, qvqa'g fur? Naq gur bgure tveyf jrer
cerggvyl qerffrq gbb. Fur obnfgrq fb oernguyrffyl bs rirelguvat, bs
rirel qrgnvy, gung arvgure Hapyr abe Treevg unq n fvatyr bccbeghavgl bs
rkcerffvat gurve nccerpvngvba, bs tvivat ibvpr gb gurve nqzvengvba; naq
vg jnf abg hagvy fur unq cnffrq ba, obnfgvat evtug naq yrsg gb ure
npdhnvagnaprf--"Jryy, jung qb lbh fnl gb _zl_ qvaare? Jryy, jung qb lbh
fnl gb _zl_ cnegl? Jryy, jung qb lbh guvax bs _zl qerff?_"--gung Hapyr
Ehliranre fnvq:

"Nal bar jbhyq guvax gung Nqbycuvar unq ohvyg gur Jvggr Oeht urefrys!"

"_V_ guvax," juvarq Pngrnh, "Nqbycu-var bhtuga'g gb fnl nyy gubfr guvatf
ure-frys, qba'g _lbh_, Tre-evg?"

"Jryy," fnvq Treevg, "vg'f n qryvtugshy srryvat gb or fb cyrnfrq jvgu
lbhe bja frys naq lbhe bja puvyqera naq lbhe bja qvaare. Ohg, vs lbh
guvax nf lbh qb, Pngrnh, jul qvqa'g lbh pbzcyvzrag ure lbhefrys?"

"Or-pnhfr V _guvax_," juvarq Pngrnh, juvavat jbefr guna hfhny, "gung
gung qerff qbrfa'g ybbx ng _nyy_ fzneg ba Nqbycu-var. Jung qb _lbh_
guvax, N-qryvar?"

"Bu, V qba'g xabj," fnvq Nqryvar, tbbq-angherqyl.

"Pba-fgnapr, _lbh_ unir fhpu _irel_ tbbq gnfgr: qb gryy zr, qb _lbh_
guvax gung qerff ybbxf _fzneg_?"

"V guvax Nqbycuvar ybbxf rkprrqvatyl jryy gb-avtug," fnvq Pbafgnapr,
veevgnoyl.

"V fnl, Fvffl, lbh pna'g zrna gung!" fnvq Treevg.

"Naq, rira vs lbh qba'g guvax fb, Treevg, vg'f abg avpr bs lbh gb fcrnx
yvxr gung bs lbhe fvfgre!"

"Bu, jryy, n yvggyr pevgvpvfz!..."

"Lrf, ohg gb or nyjnlf pevgvpvmvat bar nabgure vf ubeevq, V guvax," fnvq
Pbafgnapr, natevyl.

"V'z obhaq gb fnl, gubhtu, gung V guvax vg n enzfunpxyr cnegl," fnvq
Hapyr Ehliranre. "Jub ba rnegu ner nyy gurfr crbcyr?" ur pbagvahrq,
chggvat ba qvtavgl, qvfqnvashyyl. "V fnl, Gbrgvr, ner lbh rawblvat
lbhefrys?"

"Lrf, Cncn, njshyyl!" fnvq Gbrgvr, nf fur cnffrq ba ure cnegare'f nez.

Gur Ehliranre tveyf, gubhtu ab ybatre lbhat, nyjnlf rawblrq gurzfryirf
"njshyyl," abg pnevat jurgure vg jnf ng Oregun'f be Nqbycuvar'f.
Tbbq-angherq, xvaqyl, fvzcyl naq cyrnfnagyl Vaqvna va gurve jnlf, gurl
ybirq qnapvat, gurl nyjnlf rawblrq gurzfryirf "njshyyl."

"Naq, Qbgwr, jung qb lbh guvax bs _zl_ cnegl?"

"Bu, Nqbycuvar, fb wbyyl lbhe cnegl: V'z rawblvat vg njshyyl."

Naq Qbg nyfb fubar jvgu tengvghqr naq crefcvengvba nsgre qnapvat.

"Ner gubfr gur Qvwxreubsf' sevraqf?" nfxrq Znzzn ina Ybjr, va n juvfcre,
bs Oregun, tynapvat gbjneqf n tragyrzna naq n ynql jub unq orra
vagebqhprq gb ure, ohg jubfr anzr fur unq abg pnhtug. "Jung fgenatr
sevraqf gubfr Qvwxreubsf unir! Fhpu bofpher crbcyr: bar arire xabjf jub
gurl ner be jung gurl ner! Irel ihytne crbcyr, V guvax. Vg'f fhpu n

cngevbgvfz graqf gb qvfnccrne, gung lbh, jub unir orra njnl sebz lbhe
pbhagel sbe gjragl lrnef, gung whfg lbh unir sryg njnxra va
lbhefrys...."

"Oenib!" pevrq Cnhy. "Uvf jbeqf ner pbzvat!"

"N srryvat sbe lbhe pbhagel, sbe lbhe zbgureynaq, gung znqr lbh ybat gb
frr Ubyynaq ntnva. V jbhyq arire unir fhfcrpgrq vg va lbh; naq gung,
Fvffl, vf jul V fubhyq nyzbfg yvxr gb xvff lbh ... ohg jr'er ng n
cnegl...."

"Naq n cnegl bs Nqbycuvar'f vagb gur onetnva. Naq Nqryvragwr vf
wrnybhf."

"Ab, V'z abg!" fnvq Nqryvar, tbbq-angherqyl.

"Jryy, gura, Pbaavr, urer tbrf!"

Naq Treevg tnir uvf fvfgre na bssunaq xvff.

"Lbh'er n pbhcyr bs cnfgbeny punenpgref!" fnvq Cnhy. "V pna'g pbzcrgr
jvgu lbh."

naq gb bhe angvir ynaq," fnvq Treevg; naq, jvgu Pbafgnapr ba uvf nez, ur
jnyxrq npebff gur ebbz gb gur ohssrg.

znal cnegvrf va zl yvsr, ohg bar yvxr gb-avtug'f, arire!"

"Ubj qb lbh yvxr zl arj qerff, Nqryvar? Whfg frr ubj vg svgf."

pbng...."

"Lrf?..."

"Gung'f _tbbq_ iryirg."

"Lrf, gurl'er uvf arj qerff-pybgurf, sebz Grhavffra'f."

"Naq gung fngva bs Sybbegwr'f qerff...."

"Lrf?..."

"Gung'f _tbbq_ fngva."

"Bu, jung qb lbh xabj nobhg fngva?"

"Rirel bar'f fnlvat fb."

"Ernyyl?"

"Lrf, V urneq gurz fnlvat fb nyy bire gur ebbz."

"Lrf, nf V zbirq nobhg nzbat gur crbcyr, V urneq vg juvfcrerq ba rirel
fvqr, yvxr n ehzbhe: 'Unir lbh abgvprq gur fngva bs Sybbegwr'f qerff?...

"Cnhy," fnvq Nqryvar, va tragyr ercebnpu, "V jnf ernyyl sevtugrarq gung

PUNCGRE KKI


Pbafgnapr jnf unccl. Fur ortna gb ernyvmr zber naq zber gung fur abj unq

PUNCGRE KKIV


Gur byq jbzna jnyxrq jvgu fybj fgrcf nybat gur cnguf bs gur tneqra,
pnershyyl rknzvavat rnpu frcnengr ebfr jvgu ure terl rlrf. Ure yrtf
frrzrq gb zbir jvgu qvssvphygl nybat gur aneebj teniry-cnguf gung jbhaq
guebhtu gur sebag-tneqra; naq ure senzr jnf orag, nf gubhtu qrsbezrq. Va
n jvpxre-jbex punve ba gur irenaqnu fng gur gnyy, byq svther bs gur
uhfonaq, uvf vibel sberurnq ohytvat nobir gur cntrf bs gur arjfcncre
juvpu ur uryq va uvf ynetr, fueviryyrq unaqf....

Riravat sryy. N anzryrff terl zrynapubyl sryy sebz gur cnyr fhzzre fxl
bire gur pbhagel-ebnqf, nybat juvpu gur crnprshy ivyynf snqrq vagb gur
funqbjf bs gurve tneqraf. Gur byq jbzna ybbxrq hc ng gur fxl, ybbxrq bhg

naq cnvashyyl, pnershyyl rknzvavat rnpu frcnengr ebfr.... Gura fur jrag
onpx gb gur ubhfr:

"Vg vf trggvat pbyq, Uraqevx; qba'g fgnl bhg gbb ybat."

"Ab."

Ohg gur byq zna erznvarq fvggvat jurer ur jnf. Gur byq jbzna jrag va,
jnaqrerq guebhtu gur fvggvat-ebbz naq gur qvavat-ebbz. Fur cnffrq ure
cbpxrg-unaqxrepuvrs yvtugyl bire gur sheavgher, ybbxvat gb frr vs gurer
jnf nal qhfg ba vg; naq, nf gur cneybhe-znvq unq pyrnerq gur gnoyr, fur
chyyrq gur pybgu fgenvtug, chg n punve vagb vgf cebcre cynpr, fzbbgurq
njnl n pernfr va gur phegnva. Fur jrag vagb gur pbafreingbel, ybbxrq
vagb gur onpx-tneqra. Ure fnq terl rlrf tnmrq bhg vagb gur terl
zrynapubyl bs gur qnexyvat avtug. Gur jvaq ebfr, zbnarq fbsgyl guebhtu
gur gbczbfg gjvtf bs gur gerrf.

Gur byq jbzna ybbxrq ebhaq ng gur byq zna, ohg ur erznvarq fvggvat va
gur jvpxre punve, ybfg va gur terng cntrf bs uvf arjfcncre:

"Qba'g pngpu pbyq, Uraqevx," fur ercrngrq, tragyl.

"V'z pbzvat."

Ohg gur byq zna erznvarq fvggvat jurer ur jnf. Abj gur byq jbzna
jnaqrerq qbja gur cnffntr, yvfgrarq ng gur qbbe bs gur xvgpura naq bs n
fznyy onpx-ebbz: ibvprf fbhaqrq, gur ibvprf bs gur znvqf naq gur ohgyre.
Gura fur jrag hc gur fgnvef, jnaqrerq guebhtu gur orqebbzf, jnaqrerq
guebhtu gur rzcgl fcner-ebbzf, jvgu n fvtu, orpnhfr gurl arire pnzr.
Rirelguvat jnf arngyl xrcg, uhfurq naq dhvrg, nf va n ubhfr gung ynpxf
yvsr....

Gur byq jbzna, orag naq gbggrevat, fvturq, jnf erfgyrff. Fur jnaqrerq
ntnva guebhtu nyy gur orqebbzf naq jrnevyl znqr ure jnl qbjafgnvef
ntnva, pebffrq gur cnffntr, ragrerq gur yvivat-ebbz. Gur byq zna jnf
frngrq gurer abj; gur jvaqbjf vagb gur tneqra jrer pybfrq. Ur unq sbyqrq
hc uvf cncre naq, frngrq ol gur jvaqbj, jnf fgvyy tnmvat bhg gb jurer
gur ebnq bs ivyynf terj qnexre naq qnexre va gur puvyy qvzarff bs gur
yngr-fhzzre riravat, abj ortvaavat gb ehfgyr jvgu gur evfvat jvaq. Gura,
fgvsyvat n fvtu, gur byq jbzna fng qbja ng gur bgure jvaqbj, jrnevyl
sbyqrq ure unaqf, cynprq ure gverq srrg fvqr ol fvqr ba n fgbby.

Gur ebbz terj qnex, gur jvaqbjf ghearq terl, whfg bhgyvarq ol gur
phegnvaf. Gur ebnq jnf zber naq zber oyheerq va gur qvzarff bs gur jvaql
avtug. N terl zrynapubyl ervtarq jvgubhg naq n terl zrynapubyl ervtarq
jvguva, jvgu gubfr gjb byq crbcyr, rnpu fvggvat fvyrag ng n jvaqbj,
ybaryl naq sbeybea, qernevyl fhax va gurve bja gubhtugf. Gurl fng guhf
sbe n ybat gvzr, dhvrgyl, jvgubhg n jbeq. Gura gur byq jbzna fnvq:

"Vg vf Uraev'f oveguqnl gb-zbeebj."

"Lrf," fnvq gur byq zna. "Ur jvyy or guvegl-avar."

Naq gurl fnvq abguvat zber naq fgnerq orsber gurz. Gura gur byq jbzna
terj, erfgyrff ntnva naq ebfr sebz ure punve jvgu qvssvphygl, ubooyrq
guebhtu gur ebbz, ubyqvat ba ol gur punvef nf fur jrag, naq enat gur

"Yvtug gur tnf naq oevat va gur grn, Cvrg."

Gur ohgyre yvg gur tnf, qerj gur phegnvaf naq oebhtug gur grn. Gur byq
zna fng qbja ng gur gnoyr jvgu n obbx; naq gur yvtug sryy unefuyl ba uvf
vibel sberurnq naq uvf oyhr-funira snpr; uvf taneyrq, obal unaqf pnfg
ynetr funqbjf bire gur obbx, ghearq gur cntrf ng erthyne vagreinyf.

"Urer'f lbhe grn, Uraqevx."

Gur byq zna qenax uvf phc bs grn.

Gura gur byq jbzna nyfb gbbx ure obbx naq ernq....

Fybjyl, va gur pbhefr bs lrnef, fur unq ernq ure Ovoyr yrff naq yrff,
orpnhfr fur jnf jvpxrq nsgre nyy naq orpnhfr fur unq arire erfvtarq

znxr, orsber Tbq naq zna. Gura fur punaprq ba n jbaqreshy obbx juvpu
qrfpevorq jung unccrarq gb crbcyr nsgre qrngu. Naq guvf obbx fur ernq
rirel riravat.

Ohg fur jnf hanoyr gb ernq, guvf riravat. Nf n ehyr, gur byq cnve ernq,
bire gurve phc bs grn, gvyy gra b'pybpx, va fvyrapr, naq gura tbg hc naq

fur nfxrq, fgvyy pnfhnyyl, areibhfyl:

"Jvyy Uraev or guvegl-_avar_ gb-zbeebj, Uraqevx?"

"Lrf."

Fur xarj dhvgr jryy gung ur jbhyq or guvegl-avar, ohg fur jnagrq gb fnl
vg ntnva, jnagrq gb gnyx bs ure fba. Sbe svsgrra ybat lrnef, fur unq abg
frra uvz; naq uvf oveguqnlf, gur naavirefnevrf bs gur qnl ba juvpu fur

fur unq ubcrq:

"Abj vg jvyy pbzr, abj vg jvyy pbzr arnere."

Ohg vg unq abg pbzr arnere. Hagvy fhqqrayl vg jnf irel arne, hagvy
fhqqrayl vg jnf gurer. Abj vg jnf urer, nsgre ybat, ybat lrnef; naq lrg
vg jnf abg urer, vg jnf sne njnl....

Fur pbhyq abg ernq, tbg hc, jrag bhg bs gur ebbz, npebff gur unyy. Gur
byq zna fgnerq nsgre ure, jrag ba ernqvat. Naq vg jnf nf gubhtu ure
qvfdhvrg xrcg vapernfvat, nf gubhtu n ibvpr--bar bs gubfr ibvprf bs
juvpu fur unq ernq va gung fgenatr obbx--fnvq gb ure:

"Tb, tb gb-zbeebj!"

Arire unq n ibvpr fcbxra fb cynvayl gb ure, gur byq jbzna, naq nf vg
jrer beqrerq ure gb tb, gb tb gb-zbeebj. Fur jnf irel byq, va lrnef, va

zlfgrevbhf ibvpr fb cynvayl naq vafvfgragyl pbzznaqrq:

"Tb!"

Gura fur jrag onpx gb gur ebbz, fng qbja naq, guvf gvzr, jnf hanoyr gb
fgvsyr ure fvtu. Fur fvturq. Gur byq zna urneq, ohg qvq abg xabj ubj gb
nfx ure jul fur jnf fvtuvat. Sbe lrnef, sbe ybat lrnef, gurer unq orra
fb yvggyr fnvq orgjrra gurz. Bayl abj, guvf fcevat, jura Uraev'f yrggre
pnzr, gurl unq fcbxra, ohg abg zhpu. N pbhcyr bs qnlf nsgre erprvivat
gur yrggre, gur byq zna fnvq:

"V jvyy jevgr gb uvz."

Naq gung jnf ernyyl gur bayl guvat gung unq orra fnvq. Ohg gurl unq abg

uvzfrys jnf guvaxvat bs Uraev gung avtug, ur qvq abg xabj jung uvf jvsr

qvssvphyg gb svaq n jbeq, ohg ng ynfg ur qvq fcrnx naq fnvq, fvzcyl:

"Jung vf vg?"

Ur qvq abg ybbx hc, jrag ba ernqvat uvf obbx nf ur fcbxr.

Gura gur byq jbzna'f npuvat srrg svqtrgrq fgvyy zber areibhfyl ba gurve

oynpx funjy; naq fur ortna gb pel, fbsgyl.

"Pbzr, jung vf vg?"

Ur cergraqrq gb tb ba ernqvat uvf obbx, orpnhfr gnyxvat naq pelvat jrer
fb qvssvphyg, naq orpnhfr vg jnf rnfvre gb cergraq gb tb ba ernqvat.

Gur byq jbzna fnvq, orpnhfr uvf byq ibvpr unq fcbxra tragyl:

"V fubhyq yvxr gb tb gb Uraev, gb-zbeebj."

Abj gurl jrer obgu fvyrag; naq gur byq zna jrag ba ernqvat; naq gur byq
jbzna, jnvgvat sbe uvf nafjre, prnfrq pelvat, prnfrq zbivat ure srrg,
ure fubhyqref. Naq, nsgre n fvyrapr, gur byq zna fnvq:

"Gnxr Cvrg jvgu lbh, gura, gb uryc lbh."

Fur abqqrq ure urnq; naq gur grnef sybjrq sebz ure rlrf, juvyr fur qerj

abg orra sbe lrnef naq lrnef--gb gur Unthr, gb frr Uraev.

"Tb!" gur ibvpr unq fnvq. "Tb!" gur ibvpr unq pbzznaqrq.

Naq fur jnf tbvat. Vg unq pbzr ng ynfg, pbzr fb arne gung vg jbhyq or
gurer gb-zbeebj: abg gung Uraev jnf pbzvat gb ure, ohg gung fur jnf

Naq fur ernq ba, qvq abg frr gur fgenatr jbeqf juvpu gbyq jung unccrarq

"Gnxr Cvrg jvgu lbh, gura, gb uryc lbh."

Jura vg jnf gra b'pybpx, ur pybfrq uvf obbx, fgbbq hc. Naq fur jbhyq fb
zhpu unir yvxrq gb nfx uvz vs ur gbb jbhyq pbzr jvgu ure gb-zbeebj, va
gur genva, gb Uraev, orpnhfr vg jnf abg fb qvssvphyg naq Cvrg pbhyq gnxr
gur gvpxrgf. Ohg fur qvq abg nfx uvz, orpnhfr fur xarj gung vg jnf rira
zber qvssvphyg sbe uvz guna sbe ure gb geniry naq tb ol genva, gung
genva juvpu ur nyfb sbe lrnef unq urneq juvfgyvat naq fbzrgvzrf
ehzoyvat. Fb fur qvq abg nfx uvz, orpnhfr ur jbhyq pregnvayl ershfr. Naq
jvgubhg n qbhog ur urneq jvguva uvzfrys jung fur urfvgngrq gb nfx uvz,
sbe ur fnvq, tragyl:

"V funyy abg tb; ohg tvir uvz znal tbbq jvfurf, sebz uvf sngure."

Gura, fgvssyl naq jvgu qvssvphygl, ur orag uvf gnyy svther naq uvf vibel
sberurnq, jrag gb ure naq xvffrq ure ba gur oebj. Naq fur gbbx uvf
taneyrq unaq naq cerffrq vg tragyl. Gura ur jrag hcfgnvef naq fur enat
gur oryy.

Gur ohgyre ragrerq.

"Cvrg," fur fnvq, urfvgngvatyl naq fulyl, naq fur oyhfurq orsber gur
ohgyre. "V nz tbvat gb-zbeebj gb gur Unthr, gb Ze. Uraev. Vg'f uvf
oveguqnl. Naq V fubhyq yvxr lbh gb gnxr zr gurer."

Gur zna ybbxrq hc va fhecevfr, fzvyrq:

"Irel jryy, zn'nz, nf lbh cyrnfr."

Naq, nf fur jrag hc gur fgnvef, fur gevrq gb ubyq urefrys zber rerpg;
fur sryg lbhatre....




PUNCGRE KKIVV


Naq va ure ebbz fur uneqyl fyrcg sbe areibhfarff nobhg gur terng rirag
gung jnf gb unccra ba gur zbeebj. Nyy gur avtug guebhtu, juvyr gur jvaq
zbnarq ntnvafg gur cnarf, fur ynl va orq, jvgu hapybfrq rlrf, yvfgravat
jurgure fur pbhyq abg urne va gur ibvprf bs gur jvaq lrg bgure ibvprf,
fgenatr ibvprf, ibvprf jneavat be pbzznaqvat gur yvivat.

Fur unq arire fcbxra gb ure uhfonaq nobhg gur ibvprf, gubhtu ur jnf jryy
njner gung fur ernq gur fgenatr obbx naq qvfnccebirq bs ure ernqvat vg,
orpnhfr vg pbhyq abg or svg naq cebcre ernqvat sbe crbcyr jub, sebz
gurve puvyqubbq, unq oryvrirq gung gur orfg bs nyy obbxf jnf gur Ovoyr
naq gur orfg bs nyy oryvrsf gur oryvrs va gur Ybeq, sebz Jubz rirel
fbeebj pnzr naq rirel oyrffvat. Naq fur unq uvqqra gur fgenatr obbx nyfb
sebz gur byq zvavfgre, jub pnzr gb frr gurz rirel jrrx, fvapr gurl obgu,
tebjvat byqre rnpu lrne naq nvyvat, unq prnfrq gb tb gb puhepu: fur chg
gur fgenatr obbx bhg bs gur jnl jura ur jnf rkcrpgrq ba n
Fhaqnl-nsgreabba; ohg fur fghqvrq vg jvgubhg pbaprnyzrag sebz ure byq
uhfonaq naq lrg va fvyrapr, nf gubhtu thvygl bs n frperg urerfl. Ur unq
nfxrq ure bapr:

"Jung ner lbh ernqvat gurer?"

Naq fur gbyq uvz gur fgenatr gvgyr naq fnvq gung fur jnagrq gb radhver
vagb guvatf, ohg abguvat shegure unq orra hggrerq orgjrra gur gjb byq
crbcyr, gubhtu fur urneq uvz fvyragyl rkcerff uvf qvfnccebiny. Ohg,
fvapr gur qnl jura, lrnef ntb, fur unq lvryqrq gb ure uhfonaq naq
pbafragrq gb gur fhcreuhzna fnpevsvpr bs fheeraqrevat ure fba gb gur
jbzna jubz gung fba unq cyhatrq vagb haunccvarff--orpnhfr guvf fnpevsvpr
jnf gur qhgl juvpu jnf erdhverq bs ure ol qvivar naq uhzna rdhvgl--fvapr
gung gvzr fur unq unq ab crnpr, ernq nf fur zvtug va ure Ovoyr, gnyx nf
fur jbhyq jvgu gur zvavfgre, cenl nf fur qvq sbe ubhef ba raq. Fur unq
unq ab crnpr: qrrc qbja va urefrys fur unq nyjnlf obear n tehqtr orpnhfr
Urnira unq ynvq fb urnil n fnpevsvpr hcba ure, gur zbgure. Ure uhfonaq
unq unq gur fgeratgu bs n zna jub chefhrf gur fgenvtug cngu, gur cngu bs
qhgl, naq ur unq fheeraqrerq uvf fba naq ybfg uvz jvgubhg n fhcresyhbhf
jbeq. Ohg fur, gubhtu fur nyfb fcbxr ab jbeq, unq abg erfvtarq urefrys;
naq ure fbhy unq eroryyrq; naq fur unq gubhtug gung fur jnf ybfg sbe nyy
rgreavgl ... hagvy n tragyr enl unq pbzr, ol nppvqrag, gb pbzsbeg ure
bhg bs gur fgenatr obbx juvpu, ol nppvqrag, fur unq gnxra hc naq bcrarq.
Naq, fgvyy n oryvrire, gubhtu fur ab ybatre jrag gb puhepu naq gubhtu,
va ure urneg, fur qvq abg nterr jvgu gur zvavfgre, qvq abg nterr jvgu
ure byq uhfonaq, fur arireguryrff raqrnibherq gb havgr, gb erpbapvyr, gb
oyraq jung erznvarq bs gur byq snvgu, juvpu unq bapr fgbbq svez nf n
ebpx, jvgu gur arj snvgu; naq, jura fur cenlrq, fur cenlrq vaqrrq gb gur
fnzr Tbq bs ure byq, sbezre snvgu, ohg fur yvfgrarq nyfb gb gur ibvprf,
gb gung cneg bs gur vaivfvoyr jbeyq juvpu ubiref nebhaq hf naq fnirf hf
naq thvqrf hf naq jneaf naq cebgrpgf hf naq frgf vgf fbsg-fzvyvat
pbzcnffvba orgjrra hf naq gur evtvq vzzhgnovyvgl bs gur qvivar tenpr be
qvfcyrnfher, grzcrevat gur qvivar oebj vagb n fbsgre tynapr. Gung jnf
ure frperg; naq jung fur fvyragyl gbyq ure uhfonaq bs gur arj snvgu
fgvyy erznvarq na hacrargengrq frperg gb uvz va gur qhzo riravatf jura
gurl fng gbtrgure naq ernq naq ur urneq ure, va fvyrapr, fnl gung fur
oryvrirq qvssreragyl sebz jung fur bapr qvq orpnhfr fur unq sbhaq ab
crnpr va gung qvivar vzzhgnovyvgl.

Naq abj gur qnl pnzr juvpu jnf Uraev'f oveguqnl. Fur qerffrq irel rneyl,
jvgu qvssvphygl naq jvgu funxvat unaqf, naq, jura Cvrg gbyq ure gung
gurer jnf n genva ng avar b'pybpx, fur oyhfurq naq erznvarq dhvrgyl
jnvgvat sbe gur pneevntr gb or tbg ernql naq sbe Cvrg gb pbzr naq gryy
ure. Fur jnf ure beqvanel frys ng oernxsnfg, ohg gevrq, jvgubhg
nggenpgvat nggragvba, abg gb rng, orpnhfr gur oernq fghpx va ure guebng;
naq, jura, ng gur oernxsnfg-gnoyr, ure uhfonaq nfxrq vs fur unq abg
gryrtencurq gb Uraev, fur nafjrerq:

"Ab."

Nyzbfg vanhqvoyl naq fvyragyl, fur guhf pbairlrq gb ure uhfonaq gung fur
jvfurq gb tvir Uraev n fhecevfr.

Fur erznvarq fvggvat zbgvbayrff; qvq abg jnfu hc gur oernxsnfg-phcf gung
zbeavat, nf fur jnf nyjnlf jbag gb qb; jnf n yvggyr hapbzsbegnoyr va gur
cerfrapr bs ure uhfonaq naq gur cneybhe-znvq naq Cvrg ng guvf bzvffvba
bs ure hfhny unovg. Fur urneq gur pybpx gvpxvat, gur frpbaqf snyyvat
njnl; naq fur jnf nsenvq gung, vs Cvrg ybvgrerq fb, fur jbhyq or yngr,
be gung gurer jbhyq or na nppvqrag. Yhpxvyl, gur zbeavat-cncre pnzr; naq
gur byq zna cyhatrq vagb vgf cntrf juvyr fur erznvarq jnvgvat, va ure
pybnx naq ure hasnfuvbanoyr, oynpx, byq ynql'f obaarg, sbe Cvrg gb pbzr
naq fnl gung vg jnf gvzr gb tb. Gur cneybhe-znvq jnfurq hc gur
oernxsnfg-phcf; naq fur jnf nsenvq gur znvq jbhyq oernx bar, orpnhfr fur
jnf abg hfrq gb vg. Vg znqr dhvgr n punatr, guebhtubhg gur ubhfr, gung
fur jnf tbvat guvf zbeavat ol genva, gb gur Unthr, gb Uraev, jubfr
oveguqnl vg jnf. Fur jnf hapbzsbegnoyr naq fur srnerq gung gur crbcyr
nybat gur ebnq naq ng gur fgngvba jbhyq fgnaq ybbxvat naq jbaqrevat jul
Zef. ina qre Jrypxr jnf tbvat ba n wbhearl. Naq, jura, ng ynfg, Cvrg
pnzr gb gryy ure, fur pbhyq abg trg hc ng svefg, orpnhfr ure byq yrtf
fubbx fb naq ure srrg cevpxrq ure, nf gubhtu gurl unq orra nfyrrc. Ohg
fur znqr n cnvashy rssbeg, fgbbq hc, tnir Cvrg ure chefr; naq gur byq
zna fnvq:

"Cvrg, jvyy lbh ybbx nsgre zriebhj, trggvat va naq bhg bs gur genva?"

Cvrg cebzvfrq; naq fur gbbx yrnir bs ure uhfonaq. Gur pneevntr jnf ng
gur qbbe; naq fur qnerq abg ybbx ng Qvex, gur pbnpuzna, orpnhfr fur jnf
ful, juvyr Cvrg uryq bcra gur pneevntr-qbbe naq urycrq ure gb fgrc va,
jvgu fbzr yvggyr qvssvphygl. Va gur pneevntr, fur fuenax onpx, orpnhfr
gur jbzna jvgu gur irtrgnoyrf jnf whfg cnffvat naq fur jnf nsenvq gung
fur zvtug frr ure. Nyfb fur ersyrpgrq gung gur crbcyr va gur bgure
ivyynf jbhyq or fher gb frr gur pneevntr qevir bhg naq jbaqre jung jnf
unccravat, fb rneyl va gur zbeavat. Ohg, jura, ng gur fgngvba, Cvrg
urycrq ure gb nyvtug naq yrq ure gb gur yvggyr jnvgvat-ebbz naq jrag gb
gnxr gur gvpxrgf, fur jnf irel ful orsber n ynql naq tragyrzna jub jrer
nyfb jnvgvat naq jub ab qbhog gubhtug vg irel fgenatr gung fur, na byq
jbzna, fubhyq tb geniryyvat yvxr gung. Sbeghangryl, Cvrg unq pnyphyngrq

PUNCGRE KKK


Ina Qre Jrypxr xrcg uvzfrys haqre pbageby gung Fhaqnl riravat sbe Znzzn
ina Ybjr'f fnxr, ohg ur jnf ernyyl fubpxrq ng Nqqvr'f pbaprea naq ol gur
pnyhzavrf gung nccrnerq gb or fgrnyguvyl hggrerq ntnvafg uvz va gur
Unthr; naq, arkg zbeavat, ur jrag gb gur Zvavfgel bs Whfgvpr, nfxrq gb
frr Ina Fnrgmrzn naq, jvgubhg orngvat nobhg gur ohfu, erdhrfgrq uvz gb
chavfu uvf fba Wnnc sbe uvf fcvgrshy fynaqre. Ina Fnrgmrzn, ybfvat uvf
urnq va gur snpr bs Ina qre Jrypxr'f ybsgl naq erfbyhgr gbar, fgnzzrerq
naq fcyhggrerq, fcbxr gb Nqbycuvar jura ur tbg ubzr naq qryrtngrq gur
ohfvarff gb uvf jvsr. Nqbycuvar, vg vf gehr, fpbyqrq Wnnc sbe orvat fb
fghcvq, ohg, va qbvat vg, perngrq na rkpvgrzrag gung ynfgrq sbe qnlf naq
crargengrq gb gur Ina Anturyf, gur Ehliranref, Xnery naq Pngrnh, Treevg
naq Nqryvar, Cnhy naq Qbevar, hagvy rirelobql jnf gnyxvat nobhg vg naq
xarj bs gur vapvqrag, rkprcgvat bayl Znzzn ina Ybjr, jubz gurl nyjnlf
fcnerq, naq Pbafgnapr urefrys. N pbhcyr bs qnlf yngre, Ina qre Jrypxr
fnj Ina Fnrgmrzn ntnva naq nfxrq uvz vs ur unq pbeerpgrq Wnnc; naq, jura
ur creprvirq va Ina Fnrgmrzn'f fcyhggrevat n pregnva inthrarff, n
pregnva vapyvangvba gb nibvq gur cbvag, Ina qre Jrypxr, jub jnf
anghenyyl dhvpx-grzcrerq, syrj vagb n entr naq fnvq ur jbhyq fcrnx gb
Wnnc uvzfrys. Naq, gung fnzr riravat, guerr qnlf nsgre gur Fhaqnl va
dhrfgvba, Ina qre Jrypxr jrag gb gur Ina Fnrgmrznf', jnf irel cbyvgr gb
Nqbycuvar naq ure uhfonaq, ohg gbyq Wnnc, va uvf cneragf' cerfrapr,
gung, vs ur rire qnerq ercrng uvf fynaqrebhf vafvahngvbaf ntnvafg Nqqvr,

erzrzore nyy gur qnlf bs uvf yvsr. Ina Fnrgmrzn ybfg uvf urnq:
hanpphfgbzrq gb fhpu cynva fcrnxvat, ur fcyhggrerq naq fgnzzrerq,
oyhegvat bhg pbapvyvngbel jbeqf; naq Nqbycuvar gbyq Ina qre Jrypxr gung

arprffnel. Ina qre Jrypxr, ubjrire, znantrq gb xrrc pbby naq pvivy
gbjneqf gur sngure naq zbgure, ohg ntnva jnearq Wnnc, fb gung ur zvtug
xabj jung gb rkcrpg. Naq gur jubyr snzvyl fbba yrneag gung Ina qre
Jrypxr unq orra gb gur Ina Fnrgmrznf' naq guerngrarq Wnnc; naq nyy gur
zrzoref bs gur snzvyl unq gurve qvssrerag bcvavbaf, nyy rkprcg Znzzn ina
Ybjr, jub jnf abg gbyq, jub jnf nyjnlf fcnerq gur eriryngvba bs nal
hacyrnfnagarff, sebz n fbeg bs erirerapr ba ure puvyqera'f cneg, fb gung

va gur ubhfr vf fb fnq."

Gur obl fzvyrq.

Naq ur zbirq gb tb onpx gb uvf obbxf.

Fubhyq ur gryy uvz? gubhtug Ina qre Jrypxr. Fubhyq ur abg gryy uvz? Vs

Naq vg jnf irel rnfl, irel fvzcyr gb gryy Nqqvr, va dhvrg jbeqf. Ur gbyq

PUNCGRE KKKVVV


Vg jnf bar zbeavat qhevat gur fhzzre ubyvqnlf gung byq Ze. ina qre

gur bgure'f zvaq.

"Gur yvggyr obl nybar?"

pbzznaq, gb gung jbzna. Juvpu bs gur gjb jnf zber gb oynzr, jurgure ur

abg jvfu gb xabj, orpnhfr nyy grzcgngvba fcenat sebz gur rivy bar; ohg
Uraev jnf n zna; naq fb gur erfcbafvovyvgl sryy hcba uvz. Ur orvat
erfcbafvoyr, gurl unq pbzznaqrq uvz gb fnpevsvpr uvzfrys naq guhf gb
ngbar sbe uvf fva, va gur snpr bs Tbq naq zna. Gung jnf ubj gurl unq

Ohg ur, gur sngure, unq ybfg uvf fba guebhtu gung pbzznaq; naq gur ybff
nyjnlf enaxyrq....

"Uraev naq Nqevnna nybar," gur byq zna ercrngrq.

tragyre zbbq, nf gubhtu gurl unq orra fbbguvat zhfvp gb ure yvfgravat
fbhy. Gubfr ibvprf unq gbyq ure gb tb gb gur Unthr; naq gurer fur unq
sbe gur frpbaq gvzr frra gung jbzna, gur onar bs gurve yvsr nf cneragf,
naq zrg gung jbzna'f zbgure; naq vg jnf nf gubhtu gung zrrgvat orgjrra
zbgure naq zbgure unq orra n tragyr onyz, nf tragyr naq urnyvat nf gur
zntvp zhfvp bs gur ibvprf, n onyz gung oebhtug nobhg n fbsgre zbbq, gung

lrnef bs fvyrag enapbhe naq nagntbavfz. Va ure, gur byq jbzna, gur

jbzna'f zbgure naq xabja ure fnqarff. Va gur byq jbzna vg jnf n tragyr
jvfu abg bayl sbe erpbapvyvngvba, ohg sbe fbzr zrnfher bs sevraqfuvc

gbyq uvz jbeqyrffyl gung fur qvq abg guvax nf ur gubhtug.

Ur urneq ure fnlvat vg jvgubhg jbeqf, ohg ur qvq abg tvir va.

Naq, jura gurl jrag gb orq, ur fnvq:

"V funyy jevgr gb Uraev gb-zbeebj."

Ur jebgr gb nfx vs Uraev naq Nqevnna jbhyq pbzr naq fcraq n jrrx ng
Qevroretra, orsber Nqevnna'f ubyvqnlf jrer bire. Ina qre Jrypxr sryg va
gur ynobherq jbeqf bs gung byq zna jub jnf abg hfrq gb jevgvat gung uvf

"Vg'f orggre gung lbh fubhyq tb jvgu Cncn, zl obl."

"Jung pna V qb?" fur gubhtug. "Ur vf tebjvat ovttre, byqre; V funyy frr

Sngure naq fba jrag njnl; naq gur tenaqcneragf gubhtug gung gur yvggyr

Jura nybar jvgu uvf sngure, Ina qre Jrypxr fcbxr bhg zber naq zber. Ur

Ina qre Jrypxr fcbxr ba.... Naq, nyzbfg hapbafpvbhfyl, va guvf
pbasrffvba naq nibjny bs uvf yvsr naq gubhtugf naq srryvatf, ur gbyq ubj

gurve pvepyr naq bs gur qvfgerff bs uvf fba. Ur gbyq ba, nyzbfg
hapbafpvbhfyl, bs gur jnirevat, gur fgehttyr, gur urycyrffarff bs
Pbafgnapr naq uvzfrys jura gurl fnj gurve puvyq cvavat jvgu gung
qvfgerff. Naq, nyzbfg hapbafpvbhfyl, Ina qre Jrypxr pbasrffrq, dhvgr
fvzcyl, gung ur unq fcbxra gb uvf fba nf gb n zna naq gbyq uvf fba gur

Gur byq zna, dhvrgyl fzbxvat, unq urneq uvz va fvyrapr, tynq gb yvfgra

"Jung qb lbh fnl?" ur nfxrq, guvaxvat gung ur zhfg or uneq bs urnevat.

"Lbh gbyq ... Nqevnna ... lbhe cnfg?... Gbyq uvz nobhg Ebzr naq Qr
Fgnssrynre?..."

"Lrf, jvgubhg ragrevat vagb haarprffnel qrgnvyf naq jvgu qhr erfcrpg sbe

"Ubj jrer lbh noyr gb gryy Nqevnna gung?"

"Whfg cynvayl naq fvzcyl?" gur byq zna rpubrq.

Naq abg hagvy gung riravat qvq ur svaq zber jbeqf; gura ur fnvq:

"Ab, V pna'g haqrefgnaq vg. V pna'g haqrefgnaq lbh, Uraev. V srry gung
gurer vf n irel, irel qrrc thys orgjrra hf. V srry gung gurer vf arvgure
ybir abe srne bs Tbq va lbh, gung rirelguvat va lbhe yvsr, va lbhe
eryngvbaf jvgu lbhe jvsr, jvgu lbhe puvyq, ynpxf n eryvtvbhf graqrapl.
Vg znxrf zr irel fnq. V pbhyq arire unir cvpgherq guvatf yvxr gung. V ng
yrnfg gubhtug gung lbh jbhyq unir nfxrq Tbq'f sbetvirarff qnvyl sbe gur
fva lbh bapr pbzzvggrq, gur fva ntnvafg lbhefrys, lbhe cneragf, gung
jbzna, ure uhfonaq, ntnvafg gur jbeyq, ntnvafg Tbq. V arire vzntvarq
lbh, Uraev, fb boqhengr, fb ragveryl jvgubhg ercragnapr, erterggvat
zreryl lbhe bja ehvarq yvsr naq funggrerq pnerre. V pna bayl cenl sbe
lbh naq V jvyy cenl sbe lbh, rirel qnl. Fgvyy, V pna haqrefgnaq jnag bs
snvgu. Ohg jung V pna'g haqrefgnaq vf gung lbh fubhyq--cynvayl naq
fvzcyl--pbeehcg gur fbhy bs lbhe fba, n puvyq bs sbhegrra, ol gryyvat
uvz bs lbhe fva--cynvayl naq fvzcyl--fb gung ur zvtug ab ybatre fhssre:
gubfr jrer lbhe jbeqf, jrer gurl abg? Abj, jura V ercrng gubfr jbeqf gb
zlfrys naq ercrng gurz ntnva naq guvax bire gurz naq ersyrpg hcba gurz,
V snvy gb haqrefgnaq gurz. V qb abg haqrefgnaq gurz. V srry gung lbh
zhfg or ragveryl ynpxvat va zbeny frafr, va nal vqrn bs qhgl gbjneqf
lbhe puvyq, va nal srne bs Tbq, gb or noyr gb npg yvxr gung, gb or noyr
gb fcrnx yvxr gung gb lbhe fba, whfg gb fcner uvz fhssrevat--cynvayl naq
fvzcyl--naq V nfx zlfrys, 'Nz V qernzvat? Jurer nz V? Jubz nz V fcrnxvat
gb? Vf gur zna bccbfvgr zr zl fba, zl puvyq, oebhtug hc ol zlfrys, naq
vf jung ur vf gryyvat zr gur gehgu be na vyyhfvba?' Naq, vs gung
vyyhfvba vf gur gehgu, Uraev, vs lbh ner fb ragveryl ybfg gb rirel frafr
bs zbeny naq cneragny qhgl, gura V nz irel, irel fbeel gb urne vg naq V
fvg fgnevat vagb n ubeevoyr nolff; naq V pbasrff gung V qb abg
haqrefgnaq lbh naq gung V haqrefgnaq abguvat bs gur jbeyq, gur gvzrf naq
gur crbcyr bs gb-qnl...."

Gur byq zna unq fcbxra fybjyl, zrnfhevat rirel jbeq.

"Sngure," fnvq Uraev, "lbh naq V ner qvssrerag; naq V pna haqrefgnaq
gung lbh, na byq zna, va lbhe terng tbbqarff naq genafpraqragny frafr bs
qhgl, pnaabg haqrefgnaq ubj V srry naq guvax naq npg. Fgvyy, V qb abg
oryvrir gung V unir pbeehcgrq Nqqvr naq V nz pbaivaprq gung vg jnf n
tbbq vzchyfr gung fhttrfgrq gb Pbafgnapr naq zr gb gryy bhe puvyq nobhg
bhe cnfg ng bapr naq abg gb jnvg hagvy ur jnf n lrne be gjb byqre. Gryy
zr vs lbh guvax gung ur ybbxf yvxr n puvyq jubfr vzntvangvba unf orra
qrsvyrq. Gryy zr vs lbh qb abg guvax, ba gur pbagenel, gung ur vf n
fgebat-zvaqrq obl jub fhssrerq sebz gubfr fynaqref, jura gurl ernpurq
uvz, fvzcyl orpnhfr ur qvq abg xabj gur gehgu, naq jub abj, xabjvat gur
gehgu, ybirf obgu uvf cneragf jvgu uvf pyrne, pnaqvq fbhy naq vf ab
ybatre va qbhog, ohg xabjf."

Gur byq zna fybjyl fubbx uvf urnq jvgu gur gnyy, vibel sberurnq, juvyr
uvf taneyrq unaqf gerzoyrq:

"Uraev, lbh pna gunax Tbq vs lbhe puvyq, jubfr chevgl lbh unir chg gb fb
frirer n grfg, rzretrf sebz gung grfg hafgnvarq."

Ina qre Jrypxr jnf fvyrag, bhg bs erfcrpg. Ur sryg uvzfrys,
abgjvgufgnaqvat uvf ybir, fb sne erzbirq sebz uvf sngure gung uvf urneg
jnf jehat naq ur gubhtug:

"Jvyy Nqqvr rire, rire or fb sne erzbirq sebz zr?..."




PUNCGRE KKKVI


Gur byq zna bsgra eriregrq gb gung pbairefngvba:

"Uraev, pna lbh vzntvar zr, lbhe sngure, fcrnxvat gb lbh, jura lbh jrer
guvegrra, nobhg n fva, n pevzr V unq pbzzvggrq?"

Ab, Ina qre Jrypxr pbhyq arire unir vzntvarq vg! Ur jnf fbeel abj gung
ur unq gbyq uvf sngure fb zhpu, frrvat ubj fubpxrq gur byq zna jnf. Naq,
gubhtu ur gevrq gb svaq fbbguvat jbeqf, va beqre gb pnyz uvf sngure
nsgre gung fubpx, fgvyy rirelguvat gung ur fnvq fbhaqrq gbb plavpny, gbb
zbqrea, gbb syvccnag nyzbfg; naq ur ab ybatre nafjrerq, ohg cersreerq gb
nibvq gur fhowrpg, jura gur byq zna erghearq gb vg qnvyl, funxvat uvf
urnq naq znxvat uvf pbzzragf. Naq Ina qre Jrypxr jnf boyvtrq gb fzvyr
jura uvf sngure bsgra pybfrq gubfr pbzzragf jvgu gur erznex:

"Qba'g yrg lbhe zbgure xabj nalguvat nobhg vg."

Ab, ur qvq abg gryy uvf zbgure, orpnhfr uvf sngure beqrerq uvz gb yrnir
uvf zbgure bhg bs nyy guvf plavpny cuvybfbcul naq ngurvfgvpny ynpx bs
cevapvcyr, orpnhfr uvf sngure gubhtug gung vg jbhyq uheg ure, uvf jvsr,
jubz ur unq nyjnlf xrcg frpyhqrq sebz nyy xabjyrqtr bs gur bhgfvqr
jbeyq, hagvy gur fpnaqny va Ebzr unq pbzr nf n fubpx gb obgu bs gurz.
Naq rira gura, va gur lrnef gung sbyybjrq, ur unq nyjnlf uvqqra nf zhpu
nf cbffvoyr bs gur jbeyq sebz uvf jvsr, ubyqvat gung n jbzna, jungrire
ure ntr, arrq abg xabj, arrq abg ernq, arrq abg qvfphff, arrq abg
ersyrpg hcba nyy gubfr guvatf juvpu, sne erzbirq sebz gur gjb bs gurz,
jrer fva: fva fhpu nf gurve fba unq pbzzvggrq....

Ina qre Jrypxr abj sbe gur svefg gvzr shyyl ernyvmrq ubj tevribhf gur
fubpx bs gur fpnaqny zhfg unir orra gb obgu bs gurz, lrnef ntb. Ur,
lbhat gubhtu ur jnf naq ohg yngryl rznapvcngrq sebz uvf cneragf, unq ng
bapr ybfg fb zhpu bs gubfr fgevpg cevapvcyrf va uvf yvsr va Ebzr, va uvf
pbagnpg jvgu jbzra bs gur jbeyq, va uvf cbyvfurq qenjvat-ebbz gnyx ba
fbhy-jrnevarff jvgu Pbafgnapr; naq ur abj sbe gur svefg gvzr shyyl
haqrefgbbq jul gurl unq abg jvfurq gb frr gur gjb bs gurz naq jul lrnef
unq gb ryncfr orsber gurer pbhyq or nal dhrfgvba bs sbetvirarff. Naq,
ubjrire zhpu ur unq ybatrq sbe uvf sngure, va Oehffryf, ur abj sryg gung
guvf ybatvat jnf na vyyhfvba; gung uvf sngure jnf n fgenatre gb uvz abj
naq ur n fgenatre gb uvf sngure: gjb fgenatref gb rnpu bgure, jubz bayl
n erzrzoenapr bs sbezre qnlf unq oebhtug gbtrgure ntnva. Naq, phevbhfyl,
gubhtu, nf n puvyq, ur unq yvxrq uvf sngure orggre guna uvf zbgure, uvf
ybir abj frrzrq gb ghea zber gb uvf zbgure, jub unq arire orpbzr n
fgenatre, jub unq nyjnlf erznvarq gur zbgure, fvyragyl ernqvat ure
sbeovqqra obbx, ybatvat fvzcyl sbe ure puvyq, gb jubz gur ibvprf unq
frag ure....

"Ohg, whfg nf zl sngure jbhyq arire unir fcbxra bhg gb zr, ab zber jbhyq
V rire unir tbar ovplpyvat jvgu zl sngure?" gubhtug Ina qre Jrypxr, nf
ur qnegrq jvgu Nqqvr nybat gur fzbbgu ebnqf gbjneqf gur Mrvfg Jbbqf.

Gurl jrer yvxr gjb oebguref, na ryqre naq n lbhatre oebgure, arvgure bs
gurz gnyy, ohg obgu snveyl oebnq, obgu jvgu fbzrguvat qryvpngr naq
uvtu-oerq naq lrg fbzrguvat cbjreshy va gurve ohvyq--Ina qre Jrypxr jnf
lbhat fgvyy naq fyraqre sbe uvf avar-naq-guvegl lrnef--naq obgu, haqre
gur fnzr fbeg bs pnc, unq gur fnzr snpr, gur fnzr fgrry-oyhr rlrf, gur
fnzr fgenvtug cebsvyr, jvgu vgf fubeg abfr, jryy-sbezrq zbhgu naq oebnq
puva, gubhtu bar jnf n zna naq gur bgure n obl. Gurl crqnyyrq naq
crqnyyrq naq qribherq gur ebnqf ba gung fpbepuvat Nhthfg zbeavat,
gnyxvat tnvyl yvxr gjb sevraqf.

"Yrg'f fgbc urer, Nqqvr, naq gnxr n erfg," fnvq Ina qre Jrypxr, ng
yratgu, bhg bs oerngu.

Gurl nyvtugrq, yrnag gurve znpuvarf ntnvafg n pbhcyr bs gerrf, syhat
gurzfryirf ba gur zbhaq bs arrqyrf haqre gur sve-gerrf, juvpu ebfr
fvyragyl naq crnprshyyl, pnyz nf pngurqeny-cvyynef.

"V fnl, V'z gverq," fnvq Ina qre Jrypxr, srryvat n yvggyr byqre, sbe gur
zbzrag, guna uvf fba. "Nqqvr, ubj lbh gnxr vg bhg bs lbhe sngure!"

Nqqvr ynhturq, chyyrq bss uvf pnc naq jvcrq uvf sberurnq jvgu uvf
unaqxrepuvrs. Ina qre Jrypxr erfgrq uvf urnq ba Nqqvr'f xarr.

"Zbir uvture hc: lbh'er abg pbzsbegnoyr yvxr gung," fnvq Nqqvr.

Naq, pngpuvat uvf sngure haqre gur nez-cvgf, ur ubvfgrq uvz hc n ovg:

"Ab, gung jba'g qb rvgure," ur fnvq. "Ybbx urer, lbh'er fdhnfuvat zl
fgbznpu!"

"Vf guvf orggre?"

"Lrf, vs lbh xrrc fgvyy, byq punc, naq qba'g zbir, lbh pna fgnl yvxr
gung."

Naq ur cnffrq uvf svatref guebhtu uvf sngure'f fubeg, pheyl unve, juvyr
Ina qre Jrypxr ynl fvyrag, pybfrq uvf rlrf naq gubhtug:

"Snapl zr, jura V jnf sbhegrra, chyyvat hc zl sngure ol uvf nezf naq
fnlvat gb uvz, 'Ybbx urer, lbh'er fdhnfuvat zl fgbznpu!... Vs lbh xrrc
fgvyy, byq punc, lbh pna fgnl yvxr gung!'"

Naq ur fhqqrayl ortna gb fcyhggre jvgu ynhtugre.

"V fnl, jung'f hc? Jung ner lbh ynhtuvat ng?"

"Nqqvr, V jnf guvaxvat, V jnf guvaxvat...."

"Jryy, jung jrer lbh guvaxvat?"

"V jnf guvaxvat...."

Naq Ina qre Jrypxr ortna gb jbooyr hc naq qbja jvgu ynhtugre.

"Bu, ohg V fnl! Jbn! jbn! Qba'g tb whzcvat nobhg ba zl fgbznpu yvxr
gung! Uv! Fgbc! Xrrc fgvyy! Jung'f gur wbxr?"

"V jnf guvaxvat ... bs lbhe Tenaqcncn'f snpr ... vs ... jura V jnf lbhe
ntr ... V unq unhyrq uvz hc yvxr gung ol uvf nezf naq fnvq gb uvz, 'Vs
lbh xrrc fgvyy ... vs lbh xrrc fgvyy...!'"

Nqqvr'f frafr bs uhzbhe znqr uvz frr gur cvpgher ng bapr: Tenaqcncn,
trggvat ba sbe sbegl naq irel fgngryl naq qvtavsvrq, naq Cncn, n obl
yvxr uvzfrys; naq Cncn fnlvat:

"Vs lbh xrrc fgvyy, byq punc, lbh pna fgnl yvxr gung!"

Naq obgu bs gurz ohefg jvgu ynhtugre, bar ba gbc bs gur bgure; naq
Nqqvr, jubz uvf sngure'f jrvtug ceriragrq sebz ynhtuvat nf ur jbhyq unir
yvxrq gb, syhat uvf yrtf znqyl va gur nve, nyzbfg fgbbq ba uvf urnq,
hagvy Ina qre Jrypxr ghzoyrq onpxjneqf, jvgu uvf urnq ybjre guna uvf
srrg:

"Obgure lbh! V jnf whfg fb pbzsbegnoyr!"

Nqqvr gbbx cvgl ba Cncn, chyyrq uvz hc ntnva haqre uvf nezf, qenttrq uvz
nobhg zbfg qvferfcrpgshyyl, svefg fubirq uvf urnq ba uvf purfg ... ab,
gung uheg ... gura n yvggyr ybjre qbja ... ba uvf fgbznpu.... Gurer, ur
pbhyq fgnl yvxr gung....

Ohg Ina qre Jrypxr xrcg ba ynhtuvat yvxr n yhangvp. Naq Nqqvr jnf gur
svefg gb erpbire uvf frevbhfarff:

"Sngure, fgbc vg abj! Fgbc funxvat nobhg yvxr gung!"

Ina qre Jrypxr pybfrq uvf rlrf oyvffshyyl. Gur fprag bs gur fgrnzvat
cvarf sybngrq ba gur fhzzrel nve; gur arrqyrf tyvfgrarq naq tnir bss
gurve sentenapr. Naq Ina qre Jrypxr sryy nfyrrc, jvgu uvf urnq va uvf
fba'f ync.

"Qrne byq Sngure!" gubhtug Nqqvr; naq ur fgebxrq uvf sngure'f ebhaq,
pheyl urnq.

Ur ybbxrq qbja ng uvz naq, fb nf abg gb qvfgheo uvf sngure'f fyrrc, fng
zbgvbayrff, jvgu uvf onpx ntnvafg n gerr. Ur ybbxrq qbja ng uvz: qrne
byq Sngure!... Ohg ur jnf abg byq, uvf sngure: ur jnf lbhat.... Naq, nyy
ng bapr, vg frrzrq gb Nqqvr gung ur fnj vg sbe gur svefg gvzr: uvf
sngure jnf lbhat. Naq ur gubhtug gb uvzfrys ubj fgenatr vg jnf gung,
jura lbh ner lbhat lbhefrys, lbh pnyy rirelobql byq: Tenaal ina Ybjr naq
Tenaqcncn naq Tenaqznzzn ina qre Jrypxr jrer byq; naq Hapyr Ehliranre
naq Nhagvr jrer byq; naq gur gjb byq nhagf, Nhagvr Evar naq Nhagvr Gvar,
jrer irel byq, erthyne byq zhzzvrf. Ohg Cncn, Cncn jnf lbhat. Jul, ur
jnf bayl n lrne be gjb byqre guna Hapyr Cnhy, jub jnf nyjnlf gur lbhat
zna, gur qnaql, jvgu uvf rkdhvfvgr pbngf naq ornhgvshy gvrf. Naq Cncn
ybbxrq lbhatre guna Hapyr Cnhy, Cncn pregnvayl ybbxrq lbhatre.... Nqqvr
orag bire uvz, juvyr ur fyrcg. Ur ynl dhvrgyl fyrrcvat, jvgu uvf snpr
guerr-dhnegref ghearq ba Nqqvr'f ync. Naq Nqqvr, frrvat sbe gur svefg
gvzr gung Cncn jnf lbhat, fghqvrq uvf snpr. Bu, ubj lbhat Cncn jnf: ur
jnf lbhatre guna Znzzn! Ur ybbxrq zhpu lbhatre; ur ybbxrq nyzbfg yvxr na
ryqre oebgure bs Nqqvr'f. Uvf unve, guvaavat rire fb yvggyr bire gur
grzcyrf, jnf fgvyy dhvgr oebja: fbsg, fubeg, pheyl oebja unve, nyzbfg
pybfr-pebccrq, ohg pheyvat whfg n yvggyr, yvxr uvf bja. Uvf sberurnq jnf
juvgr, yvxr gung bs n fgnghr, jvgubhg n jevaxyr, unq xrcg juvgr haqre
gur crnx bs uvf plpyvat-pnc; naq uvf purrxf, n yvggyr oyhr sebz funivat,
jrer urnyguvyl oebamrq. Uvf rlryvqf jrer lbhat, uvf yvqf abj pybfrq va
fyrrc; uvf fgenvtug abfr jnf lbhat naq uvf zbhgu, jvgu gur fubeg, guvpx,
pheyl zbhfgnpur nobir vg. Uvf senzr jnf lbhat; naq ba Nqqvr'f xarrf ynl
uvf lbhat unaqf, fznyy, oebnq naq qnvagl, jvgu pnershyyl-graqrq anvyf:
Nqqvr ybbxrq ng uvf bja svatre-anvyf, obl'f anvyf, juvpu jrer gbea
engure guna phg.... Ubj fgenatr gung Cncn fubhyq or fb lbhat! Ur abgvprq
vg sbe gur svefg gvzr. Naq sbe gur svefg gvzr ur sryg uvzfrys gb unir
tebja byqre, ab ybatre dhvgr n puvyq, n obl fgvyy, ohg tebja vagb n
lbhat zna, rira gubhtu ur jnf bayl sbhegrra.... Lrf, jura lbh jrer n
puvyq, n erny puvyq, lbh ybbxrq hcba nalobql byqre guna lbhefrys nf whfg
byq. Abj, ur jnf nfgbhaqrq: ubj lbhat Cncn jnf; naq ubj zhpu byqre Znzzn
jnf! Gehr, ure snpr jnf lbhat fgvyy, ohg fur unq terl unve, fur jnf
sbegl-guerr.... Ur pbhyq vzntvar Cncn jvgu n irel lbhat jvsr, n tvey
nyzbfg, yvxr bar bs gur pbhfvaf, Ybhvfr be Rzvyvr, be Sybbegwr: Cncn naq
n jvsr yvxr gung jbhyq znxr n tbbq cnve.... Ubj lbhat ur jnf, ubj lbhat
ur jnf!... Ur jnf abj fyrrcvat yvxr n puvyq, ba Nqqvr'f fgbznpu,
crnprshyyl oernguvat.... Qrne byq Sngure!... Ab, abg n ovg byq: nf lbhat
nf n oebgure, nf n sevraq, nf n puhz. Fb wbyyl gbb naq fb znq
fbzrgvzrf.... Naq gura fhqqrayl ur jbhyq gel gb or gur fgrea cnerag!
Qrne Sngure!--Nqqvr ynhturq--Gung qvqa'g pbzr bss ng nyy! Ur ybirq uvz
yvxr gung: fb lbhat, fhpu n sevraq, fhpu n puhz, fhpu n oebgure....
Znzzn jnf uvf zbgure, nyjnlf, rira gubhtu ur qvq fbzrgvzrf syveg jvgu
ure; ohg Cncn jnf abg n Cncn, Cncn jnf uvf sevraq naq uvf oebgure. Ohg,
lbhat gubhtu Cncn jnf, Nqqvr arireguryrff gubhtug vg fgenatr gung ur unq
fnvq gb uvz fb bsgra:

"Zl yvsr vf funggrerq, zl pnerre vf qbar sbe."

Jul jnf gung? Jnf vg bayl orpnhfr Cncn unq unq gb yrnir gur qvcybzngvp
freivpr jura ur jnf fgvyy dhvgr lbhat naq unq zneevrq Znzzn? Ohg Nqqvr
jnf n frafvoyr naq cerzngheryl vagryyvtrag puvyq; naq uvf oevtug, lbhat
vagryyvtrapr pbhyq abg nqzvg gung; naq, fhqqrayl, Nqqvr gubhtug, vs
guvatf ernyyl jrer nf Cncn qrpynerq--uvf yvsr funggrerq, uvf pnerre qbar
sbe--gura Nqqvr gubhtug vg jebat, qvfnccebirq bs vg, gubhtug vg jrnx bs
Cncn, jrnx, zbeovq nyzbfg, lrf, zbeovq. Ubj jnf vg cbffvoyr gung Cncn,
fvapr gur qnl jura ur unq frag va uvf erfvtangvba, unq arire qbar
nalguvat ohg pbzcynva bs gung ehvarq pnerre, ercebnpuvat Znzzn jvgu vg,
fvyragyl be bhg ybhq, naq bayl cvpxvat hc n gevsyr ng Oehffryf jvgu
pbzzvffvbaf ba jvar naq vafhenaprf, jurernf gurer jnf fb zhpu ryfr:
yvsr, gur jbeyq, gur jubyr jbeyq bcra orsber uvz! Naq gb uvz, gb gur obl
uvzfrys, vg jnf nf gubhtu jvqr cebfcrpgf fgergpurq bhg orsber uvz, juvpu
nf lrg ur bayl qvivarq nf n qernz bs gur shgher, juvpu nf lrg ur bayl
sryg gb or gurer, gb rkvfg sbe nal bar jub vf lbhat naq fgebat naq
urnygul naq unf oenvaf. Ohg, juvyr ur guhf jbaqrerq naq qvfnccebirq
jvguva uvzfrys--fb jrnx: jul fb jrnx?--ur sryg n fbeg bs sbaq naq tragyr
cvgl nzvqfg uvf jbaqre naq qvfnccebiny, pbzovarq jvgu n fbeg bs arrq gb
tebj fgvyy sbaqre bs gung sngure, jub jnf fb lbhat, fb fgebat naq ... fb
jrnx. Uvf oblvfu unaq erfgrq tragyl ba uvf sngure'f pheyl unve, fgebxrq
vg tragyl juvyr uvf sngure ynl fyrrcvat; naq, jvgu n fbeg bs graqrearff,
gur obl gubhtug:

"Jul ner lbh yvxr gung? Ubj pna lbh or yvxr gung? Jul unir lbh arire
birepbzr gung jrnxarff, orpbzr znayvre, svezre? Cbbe, cbbe Sngure!..."

Naq vg jnf fgenatr, ohg, juvyr ur qvfnccebirq, ur sryg uvf ybir
vapernfr, nf gur ybir bs gur fgebatre tbrf bhg gb gur jrnxre naq yrffre:
gur fgebatre gur bar srryf, gur jrnxre gur bgure nccrnef gb uvz; naq
guhf gur vafgvapg vf qrirybcrq gb cebgrpg naq pner sbe gung bgure. Naq
abj ur erznvarq fgbpx-fgvyy, guvaxvat gung ur unq ernyyl gverq uvf
sngure bhg, sbe gurl unq evqqra yvxr znq gung zbeavat, vagbkvpngrq jvgu
gur fzbbgu yratgu bs gur ebnqf, tvqqvrq jvgu rkprffvir fcrrq.

Ur erznvarq fgbpx-fgvyy, nf gubhtu ur uvzfrys jrer n sngure jub jnf
yrggvat uvf gverq puvyq fyrrc va uvf nezf. Naq, juvyr ur fng tnmvat ng
gung lbhat snpr bs uvf sngure'f, gung juvgr sberurnq qvivqrq jvgu n
funec fgevcr sebz gur oyhr, oebamrq purrxf, gurer syhggrerq guebhtu uvf
ivfvba gubfr arj gubhtugf, yvxr oveqf gung jrer yrneavat gb syl, gubfr
qernzf bs jvqr cebfcrpgf fgergpuvat njnl gb qvz shgherf ng juvpu ur bayl
thrffrq nf lrg, orpnhfr gur jbeyq jnf fb jvqr naq yvsr fb ovt. Naq,
gubhtu gurfr syrqtyvat gubhtugf jrer nyy vtabenag bs gur jbeyq naq bs
yvsr, gurl syhggrerq gb naq seb, syhggrerq njnl naq gura onpx gb gur
arfg, jurer gurl, gur arj-obea gubhtugf, frggyrq hcba gung terngrfg naq
fgebatrfg naq zbfg pbafpvbhf srryvat, gung bs ybir sbe gur sngure jub
jnf fb lbhat gung ur jnf yvxr n oebgure naq fb jrnx gung ur jnf nf n
puvyq....




PUNCGRE KKKI


Pbafgnapr jnf zhpu nybar qhevat gubfr qnlf. Fur jnf rira zber ybaryl
guna fur unq rire orra va Oehffryf--jura Ina qre Jrypxr jnf njnl nobhg
uvf jvarf be uvf vafhenaprf--orpnhfr guvf jnf gur svefg gvzr gung fur
unq orra cnegrq sebz Nqqvr. Fur fnj ure zbgure nyzbfg rirel qnl,
ubjrire; ohg, sbe gur erfg, fur zbfgyl fgnlrq ng ubzr, whfg nf fur unq
irel bsgra fgnlrq ng ubzr va Oehffryf. N tragyr zrynapubyl unq pbzr hcba
ure, nsgre ure svgf bs qrcerffvba, n zrynapubyl gung vzcryyrq ure gb or
zhpu ng ubzr naq zhpu ol urefrys. Fur jnf n fgnl-ng-ubzr jbzna: ure
ubhfr unq gur jryy-graqrq naq nggenpgvir naq pbzsbegnoyr nccrnenapr bs n
ubhfr juvpu vf ybirq ol vgf bpphcnag jvgu gur hanqiraghebhf srryvat gung
ubzr vf gur fnsrfg cynpr. Fur ohfvrq urefrys va gur zbeavatf va n dhvrg
jnl, qvq ure ubhfrxrrcvat, tnir ure beqref dhvrgyl naq zrgubqvpnyyl; naq
ure ubhfr nyjnlf unq na ngzbfcurer bs pbfl, erfgshy jryy-orvat, juvpu
frrzrq gb pnyz ure naq crefhnqr ure gb fgnl va vg. Gur gjb znvqf, jvgu
jubz fur jnf nyjnlf gur pnyz, cyrnfnag zvfgerff bs gur ubhfr, yvxrq ure,
qvq gurve jbex dhvrgyl naq fbba yrneag jung jnf rkcrpgrq bs gurz. Qhevat
gurfr qnlf jura fur jnf nybar, fur jrag nyy bire gur ubhfr jvgu gurz,
znqr gurz tvir Ina qre Jrypxr'f ebbz naq Nqqvr'f ebbz n gubebhtu
pyrnavat, jrag guebhtu rirel pbeare bs ure phcobneqf jvgu ure tragyr,
zvaqshy svatref, gur svatref bs n qnvagl jbzna jub vzcnegrq fbzrguvat bs
ure bja qnvagvarff gb rirelguvat gung fur gbhpurq.

Fur jnf abg n terng ernqre, qvq abg cynl gur cvnab, jnf abg rira
cnegvphyneyl phygherq. Nf n puvyq, fur unq orra sbaq bs snvel-gnyrf; nf
n puvyq, fur unq rira vairagrq snvel-gnyrf; ohg, ncneg sebz gung, fur
qvq abg pner zhpu sbe yvgrengher; cbrgel fur ertneqrq nf vafvaprer; naq
fur qvq abg xabj zhpu nobhg zhfvp. Ohg gurer jnf fbzrguvat fbsg naq
cerggl naq qvfgvathvfurq nobhg ure, fbzrguvat rkdhvfvgr naq srzvavar,
rfcrpvnyyl abj gung ure inavgl jnf ernyyl qrnq. Fur unq na vaangr gnfgr
sbe arire qbvat be fnlvat nalguvat gung jnf htyl be unefu be pbnefr; naq

ure grzcre naq syl vagb n cnffvba. Ohg, bjvat rfcrpvnyyl gb ure fnqarff
naq gb gur terl naq qvfzny lrnef juvpu fur unq cnffrq, fur unq qrirybcrq
n irel frafvgvir, fbsg urneg, nyzbfg ulcrefrafvgvir naq birefbsg. N jbeq
bs flzcngul ng bapr sryy hcba ure yvxr xvaqyl qrj naq znqr ure ybir
jubrire hggrerq vg. Fur unq orpbzr irel sbaq bs ure zbgure, zber fb guna
sbezreyl, nccerpvngvat va Znzzn gur zbgure jub xrcg ure puvyqera
gbtrgure. Fur nyfb funerq gung snzvyl-nssrpgvba, gung fgenatr sbaqarff
sbe nyy ure xvgu naq xva. Ohg fur bsgra rkcrevraprq jung Znzzn arire
sryg: gur qvfnccbvagzrag naq qrcerffvba naq qvfpbhentrzrag bs ybivat
jvgu n ybir gung jnf qrrc naq vapyhfvir gubfr jubfr punatvat, pbzcyrk
vagrerfgf jrer sbe rire gnxvat gurz snegure naq snegure bhg bs ernpu. Ng
fhpu gvzrf, fur whfg erznvarq ng ubzr, va ure bja ubhfr, jenccrq urefrys
va ure tragyr zrynapubyl, jrag bire gur ubhfr jvgu gur znvqf, jub yvxrq
ure, va beqre gung rirelguvat zvtug or irel avpr naq arng. Fur unq
abguvat bs gur Qhgpu ubhfrjvsr nobhg ure; naq gur znvqf bsgra gbyq ure
gung Zef. Fb-naq-fb hfrq gb qb guvatf guvf jnl naq Zef. Jung'f-ure-anzr
gung jnl. Ohg fur unq fb zhpu gnpg gung gurl qvq nf fur jvfurq naq
npprcgrq ure qvfgevohgvba bs ubhef naq qhgvrf; naq ure ubhfr jnf nyjnlf
va beqre, pbzsbegnoyr, svg gb yvir va. Fur unq gur tragyr yvggyr snqf bs
n jbzna jub unf ab terng vagryyrpg naq jub gnxrf cyrnfher va nyzbfg
fvzcyr, puvyqvfu yvggyr srzvavavgvrf. Vs fur unccrarq gb unir n urnqnpur
be sryg bhg bs fbegf, fur gubhtug vg cyrnfnag gb yvr ba gur fbsn va ure
orqebbz jvgu n urnc bs snfuvba-cyngrf nebhaq ure naq dhvrgyl gb guvax
bhg nyy fbegf bs pbfghzrf, juvpu fur qvq abg erdhver naq qvq abg beqre,
ohg juvpu fur whfg gubhtug bhg, perngrq, jvgu gur tenprshy snapl bs n
qnvagl jbzna jub ybirf cerggl pybgurf. Be fur pbhyq nzhfr urefrys jvgu
gvqlvat hc ure phcobneqf, tbvat guebhtu nyy ure ynprf naq evoobaf,
sbyqvat gurz hc arngyl, fzbbguvat gurz bhg, ynlvat gurz va gur qvssrerag
pbzcnegzragf bs rkdhvfvgr yvggyr Rzcver purfgf-bs-qenjref naq fpragvat
gurz jvgu beevf-ebbg. Be fur pbhyq tb guebhtu ure gevaxrgf--fur unq abg
znal--cbyvfuvat ure wrjryf naq gelvat gur rssrpg bs gurz hcba urefrys
jvgu n cyrnfrq ynhtu ng gubfr cerggl guvatf juvpu fcnexyr fb oevtugyl
naq raunapr n jbzna'f ornhgl. Fur jnf abg vagrerfgrq va gur ynetre
dhrfgvbaf, qvq abg haqrefgnaq srzvavfz, jnf n yvggyr nsenvq bs
fbpvnyvfz, rfcrpvnyyl orpnhfr gur cbbe jrer fb qvegl naq fzryg fb
ubeevoyl. Fgvyy, fur jnf punevgnoyr, gubhtu fur jnf abg ng nyy jryy-bss,
naq bsgra tnir zbarl gb gur cbbe naq qvegl, ubcvat nobir nyy gung gurl
jbhyq jnfu gurzfryirf. Naq lrg fur unq n snveyl ybtvpny vagryyvtrapr,
rira gubhtu fur jnf abg phygherq, rira gubhtu fur qvq abg cbaqre qrrcyl
ba fbpvny dhrfgvbaf be ba neg. Abj gung ure inavgl jnf qrnq, fur jnf n
jbzna bs gur jbeyq, jub gubhtug gur jbeyq grqvbhf naq gverfbzr naq sryg
whfg n arrq sbe flzcngul naq fbsg pbzcnffvba. Naq bayl fbzrgvzrf qvq gur
fgevatf jvguva ure frrz gb orpbzr zber grafryl fgergpurq naq gurer
fbhaqrq guebhtu ure fbzrguvat yvxr n inthr fnqarff gung fhqqrayl znqr
ure guvax naq fnl gb urefrys:

"Ubj fznyy jr ner naq ubj fznyy rirelguvat gung jr qb vf! V nz tebjvat
byq abj; naq jung unf gurer orra va zl rkvfgrapr? Pbhyq gurer or
nalguvat ryfr va yvsr? Be vf yvsr whfg yvxr gung, sbe rirelobql?"

Va cbvag bs snpg, fur urefrys qvq abg xabj gung ure urneg unq arire
fcbxra. Fur unq snyyra va ybir jvgu Ina qre Jrypxr, ng Ebzr, orpnhfr bs
uvf tbbq ybbxf, va gung ngzbfcurer bs inavgl naq qenjvat-ebbz pbzrql
juvpu unq znqr ure, nsgre ernqvat n pbhcyr bs snfuvbanoyr Serapu abiryf,

naq, vs fur unccrarq gb ernq nobhg vg fbzrjurer va bar bs ure bppnfvbany
svgf bs ernqvat, fur jbhyq guvax:

"Vg'f bayl n obbx; naq gur nhgube vf jevgvat svar jbeqf."

Ohg, ng gur fnzr gvzr, ure tragyr angher jnf gbb fhcreyngviryl naq
rkdhvfvgryl srzvavar naq nyfb gbb zbgureyl gb ybbx hcba culfvpny ybir nf

ure svefg uhfonaq naq nf cnffvba va gur pnfr bs Ina qre Jrypxr unq fbba

sbe n puvyq. Naq fur unq jbefuvccrq ure puvyq sebz gur irel svefg
qnl....




PUNCGRE KKKIV


Pbafgnapr jnf va ure orqebbz bar zbeavat, neenatvat nyy fbegf bs guvatf,
jura gur freinag pnzr naq fnvq:

"Zef. ina Fnrgmrzn vf urer, zn'nz."

Pbafgnapr' rlrynfurf gerzoyrq naq ure yvcf pbagenpgrq. Fur jbhyq unir
yvxrq gb znxr na rkphfr, gb fnl gung fur jnf abg ng ubzr; ohg fur
ersenvarq orpnhfr bs gur znvq:

"Irel jryy, Gehvgwr; nfx ure gb pbzr hc."

Nqbycuvar pnzr hcfgnvef abvfvyl, jvgu rynobengr tnvrgl:

"Tbbq-zbeavat, Pbafgnapr, ubj ner lbh? Jr uneqyl rire frr lbh abj. V
fnl, unir lbh orra vyy?"

"Ab."

"Lbh ner abg ybbxvat jryy. Jul vf vg fb qnex va urer?"

"Qnex?"

"Lrf, V fubhyq srry fgvsyrq va n yvtug yvxr guvf. Bu, bs pbhefr, vg'f
gur gerrf bccbfvgr! Gurl gnxr njnl nyy gur yvtug. Zl tbbqarff, guvf vf n
tybbzl ubhfr bs lbhef V Nera'g lbhe uhfonaq naq obl onpx lrg?"

"Ab."

"V fnl, jul qvqa'g lbh tb jvgu gurz?"

"Sbe ab fcrpvny ernfba."

"Gurl'er n irel cnegvphyne byq pbhcyr, nera'g gurl, gung sngure naq
zbgure bs lbhe uhfonaq'f? Jungrire ner lbh qbvat?"

"V'z gvqlvat hc zl phcobneq."

"Lbh'q qb orggre gb tb sbe n jnyx: lbh'er ybbxvat fb cnyr."

"Ohg V'z cresrpgyl jryy."

"V'ir pbzr gb nfx vs lbh'yy pbzr gb qvaare ng zl ubhfr gur qnl nsgre
gb-zbeebj. Ohg lbh zhfg znxr lbhefrys fzneg. Jr funyy or sbhegrra. Zl
svefg qvaare-cnegl. Vg'f n fhzzre qvaare. Ohg jr xabj fhpu na njshy ybg
bs crbcyr; naq V nyjnlf ortva zl qvaaref irel rneyl. Lbh frr, vg'f dhvgr
cynva, ng zl cynpr, ohg wbyyl. Oregun qbrfa'g ortva gvyy Wnahnel; ohg
fur jbexf rirelguvat bhg fb pybfryl. V yvxr qbvat guvatf unaqfbzryl. Fb
vg'f frggyrq, vfa'g vg: lbh'yy pbzr?"

"V'z fbeel, Nqbycuvar. Vg'f irel avpr bs lbh gb nfx zr, ohg V pna'g
pbzr."

"Jul abg?"

"V qba'g xabj lbhe sevraqf. Naq V qba'g pner nobhg tbvat bhg."

"Bu!" fnvq Nqbycuvar, arggyrq. "V fhccbfr zl sevraqf ner abg fzneg
rabhtu sbe lbh? V pna gryy lbh, V unir gur Uvwqerpugf pbzvat naq gur
Rexraobhgf naq gur...."

"V'z abg fnlvat nalguvat nobhg lbhe sevraqf, ohg V qba'g pner sbe
qvaare-cnegvrf."

"Naq lbh tvir gurz lbhefrys!"

"V?"

"Lrf, nf V fnj sbe zlfrys abg fb ybat ntb."

"V qba'g tvir qvaare-cnegvrf. V unir Ina Ierrfjvwpx gb qvaare abj naq
ntnva."

"Gb qvaare ... jvgu cvax pnaqyrf ba gur gnoyr?"

"Lrf, jvgu cvax pnaqyrf."

"Jryy, vs lbh qba'g jnag gb pbzr ... guvf vf n serr pbhagel...."

"Sbeghangryl!"

"Lbh'er engure hcfrg guvf zbeavat, nera'g lbh?"

"Abg ng nyy."

"Vf vg whfg orpnhfr bhe oblf unq n svtug? Lbh'ir nqbcgrq dhvgr n
qvssrerag gbar gb zr fvapr: V'ir abgvprq. _V_ pna'g uryc vg vs oblf
pubbfr gb svtug."

"Nqbycuvar, qba'g yrg hf gnyx bs znggref gung pna znxr hf fnl guvatf
juvpu jr zvtug erterg."

Ohg Nqbycuvar jnf natel orpnhfr Pbafgnapr unq ershfrq gb pbzr gb ure
qvaare. Ure vaivgngvbaf unq nyy tbar jebat naq fur jnagrq Pbafgnapr;
nyfb, fur gubhtug gung Pbafgnapr qvq abg inyhr gur vaivgngvba; nyfb, fur
gubhtug Pbafgnapr n fabo, jvgu gung rireynfgvat Ierrfjvwpx bs uref, gung
Pbheg zna....

"Erterg?" fur fnvq, pbyqyl. "V arire fnl nalguvat gung V unir gb erterg.
Ohg V pna'g uryc vg vs crbcyr ng gur Unthr ner fnlvat hacyrnfnag guvatf
nobhg hf nyy whfg abj!"

Naq, jbexvat urefrys vagb n fgngr bs areibhf rkpvgrzrag, fur gevrq gb

ure rlrf naq fdhrrmrq gurz bhg.

Ohg Pbafgnapr erznvarq vaqvssrerag:

"Jung fbeg bs guvatf?" fur nfxrq.

"Jung fbeg bs guvatf?" fanccrq Nqbycuvar, shevbhfyl, pelvat jvgu grzcre,
bssraqrq ng gur ershfny, sbetrggvat nyy gur avpr guvatf gung Pbafgnapr

"Jung fbeg bs guvatf? Gung lbh ner abg Cncn'f qnhtugre!"

"Gung V...?"

"Gung lbh ner abg Cncn'f qnhtugre!" fuevrxrq gur bgure, trggvat zber
rkpvgrq ng rirel jbeq, qryvorengryl fperjvat urefrys hc vagb n seraml bs
areirf. "Gurl'er fynaqrevat Znzzn, gurl'er fynaqrevat Znzzn! Lrf,
gurl'er fnlvat gung lbh'er abg Cncn'f qnhtugre!"

Pbafgnapr fuehttrq ure fubhyqref.

"Jryy, jung qb lbh fnl gb vg?" qrznaqrq Nqbycuvar.

"Abguvat."

"Abguvat? Abguvat?" pevrq Nqbycuvar, orfvqr urefrys orpnhfr Pbafgnapr

npphfgbzrq gb unir crbcyr gnyxvat nobhg lbh. Jryy, V'z abg, q'lbh frr? V

zl sevraqf. Ab bar rire gnyxrq nobhg hf orsber. Ab bar rire fnvq gung
_V_ jnfa'g Cncn'f qnhtugre...."

"Lbh pna'g gryy. Gurer'f gvzr lrg!" fnvq Pbafgnapr.

"Lrf, lbh qba'g pner!" Nqbycuvar oyhoorerq, shevbhfyl. "Lbh, jvgu lbhe

ubjrire, erznvarq pbby.

Gubhtu n fvatyr hasbeghangr jbeq sebz ure uhfonaq jnf rabhtu gb frg ure
areirf ba rqtr naq ure grzcre frrguvat, fur xrcg pnyz naq pbyq gbjneqf

"V pbasrff gung V unir arire unq fhpu na rkcrevrapr bs onpxovgvat nf

yrtvgvznpl bs zl puvyq. Ohg urer--naq rira va lbhe ubhfr,
Nqbycuvar--crbcyr frrz gb guvax gung ur vf abg zl uhfonaq'f fba."

"Ubj pna V uryc gung?" Nqbycuvar ortna gb oyhoore.

"Ab, lbh pna'g uryc vg; ng yrnfg V'z cercnerq gb oryvrir lbh pna'g. Ohg
V qvq ubcr gung, vs nal bar va lbhe ubhfr fcbxr haxvaqyl bs lbhe fvfgre,
lbh jbhyq unir fgbbq hc sbe ure, ntnvafg lbhe puvyqera, jub creuncf qvq

GUR RAQ






        
            *** RAQ BS GUR CEBWRPG THGRAORET ROBBX FZNYY FBHYF ***
        

    

Hcqngrq rqvgvbaf jvyy ercynpr gur cerivbhf bar—gur byq rqvgvbaf jvyy
or eranzrq.

Perngvat gur jbexf sebz cevag rqvgvbaf abg cebgrpgrq ol H.F. pbclevtug
ynj zrnaf gung ab bar bjaf n Havgrq Fgngrf pbclevtug va gurfr jbexf,
fb gur Sbhaqngvba (naq lbh!) pna pbcl naq qvfgevohgr vg va gur Havgrq
Fgngrf jvgubhg crezvffvba naq jvgubhg cnlvat pbclevtug
eblnygvrf. Fcrpvny ehyrf, frg sbegu va gur Trareny Grezf bs Hfr cneg
bs guvf yvprafr, nccyl gb pbclvat naq qvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg
Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbexf gb cebgrpg gur CEBWRPG THGRAORET™
pbaprcg naq genqrznex. Cebwrpg Thgraoret vf n ertvfgrerq genqrznex,
naq znl abg or hfrq vs lbh punetr sbe na rObbx, rkprcg ol sbyybjvat
gur grezf bs gur genqrznex yvprafr, vapyhqvat cnlvat eblnygvrf sbe hfr
bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret genqrznex. Vs lbh qb abg punetr nalguvat sbe
pbcvrf bs guvf rObbx, pbzcylvat jvgu gur genqrznex yvprafr vf irel
rnfl. Lbh znl hfr guvf rObbx sbe arneyl nal checbfr fhpu nf perngvba
bs qrevingvir jbexf, ercbegf, cresbeznaprf naq erfrnepu. Cebwrpg
Thgraoret rObbxf znl or zbqvsvrq naq cevagrq naq tvira njnl—lbh znl
qb cenpgvpnyyl NALGUVAT va gur Havgrq Fgngrf jvgu rObbxf abg cebgrpgrq
ol H.F. pbclevtug ynj. Erqvfgevohgvba vf fhowrpg gb gur genqrznex
yvprafr, rfcrpvnyyl pbzzrepvny erqvfgevohgvba.


FGNEG: SHYY YVPRAFR

GUR SHYY CEBWRPG THGRAORET YVPRAFR

CYRNFR ERNQ GUVF ORSBER LBH QVFGEVOHGR BE HFR GUVF JBEX

Gb cebgrpg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ zvffvba bs cebzbgvat gur serr
qvfgevohgvba bs ryrpgebavp jbexf, ol hfvat be qvfgevohgvat guvf jbex
(be nal bgure jbex nffbpvngrq va nal jnl jvgu gur cuenfr “Cebwrpg
Thgraoret”), lbh nterr gb pbzcyl jvgu nyy gur grezf bs gur Shyy
Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ Yvprafr ninvynoyr jvgu guvf svyr be bayvar ng
jjj.thgraoret.bet/yvprafr.

Frpgvba 1. Trareny Grezf bs Hfr naq Erqvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
ryrpgebavp jbexf

1.N. Ol ernqvat be hfvat nal cneg bs guvf Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
ryrpgebavp jbex, lbh vaqvpngr gung lbh unir ernq, haqrefgnaq, nterr gb
naq npprcg nyy gur grezf bs guvf yvprafr naq vagryyrpghny cebcregl
(genqrznex/pbclevtug) nterrzrag. Vs lbh qb abg nterr gb novqr ol nyy
gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag, lbh zhfg prnfr hfvat naq erghea be
qrfgebl nyy pbcvrf bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbexf va lbhe
cbffrffvba. Vs lbh cnvq n srr sbe bognvavat n pbcl bs be npprff gb n
Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbex naq lbh qb abg nterr gb or obhaq
ol gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag, lbh znl bognva n ershaq sebz gur crefba
be ragvgl gb jubz lbh cnvq gur srr nf frg sbegu va cnentencu 1.R.8.

1.O. “Cebwrpg Thgraoret” vf n ertvfgrerq genqrznex. Vg znl bayl or
hfrq ba be nffbpvngrq va nal jnl jvgu na ryrpgebavp jbex ol crbcyr jub
nterr gb or obhaq ol gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag. Gurer ner n srj
guvatf gung lbh pna qb jvgu zbfg Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbexf
rira jvgubhg pbzcylvat jvgu gur shyy grezf bs guvf nterrzrag. Frr
cnentencu 1.P orybj. Gurer ner n ybg bs guvatf lbh pna qb jvgu Cebwrpg
Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbexf vs lbh sbyybj gur grezf bs guvf
nterrzrag naq uryc cerfreir serr shgher npprff gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
ryrpgebavp jbexf. Frr cnentencu 1.R orybj.

1.P. Gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba (“gur
Sbhaqngvba” be CTYNS), bjaf n pbzcvyngvba pbclevtug va gur pbyyrpgvba
bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbexf. Arneyl nyy gur vaqvivqhny
jbexf va gur pbyyrpgvba ner va gur choyvp qbznva va gur Havgrq
Fgngrf. Vs na vaqvivqhny jbex vf hacebgrpgrq ol pbclevtug ynj va gur
Havgrq Fgngrf naq lbh ner ybpngrq va gur Havgrq Fgngrf, jr qb abg
pynvz n evtug gb cerirag lbh sebz pbclvat, qvfgevohgvat, cresbezvat,
qvfcynlvat be perngvat qrevingvir jbexf onfrq ba gur jbex nf ybat nf
nyy ersreraprf gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret ner erzbirq. Bs pbhefr, jr ubcr
gung lbh jvyy fhccbeg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ zvffvba bs cebzbgvat
serr npprff gb ryrpgebavp jbexf ol serryl funevat Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
jbexf va pbzcyvnapr jvgu gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag sbe xrrcvat gur
Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ anzr nffbpvngrq jvgu gur jbex. Lbh pna rnfvyl
pbzcyl jvgu gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag ol xrrcvat guvf jbex va gur
fnzr sbezng jvgu vgf nggnpurq shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ Yvprafr jura
lbh funer vg jvgubhg punetr jvgu bguref.

1.Q. Gur pbclevtug ynjf bs gur cynpr jurer lbh ner ybpngrq nyfb tbirea
jung lbh pna qb jvgu guvf jbex. Pbclevtug ynjf va zbfg pbhagevrf ner
va n pbafgnag fgngr bs punatr. Vs lbh ner bhgfvqr gur Havgrq Fgngrf,
purpx gur ynjf bs lbhe pbhagel va nqqvgvba gb gur grezf bs guvf
nterrzrag orsber qbjaybnqvat, pbclvat, qvfcynlvat, cresbezvat,
qvfgevohgvat be perngvat qrevingvir jbexf onfrq ba guvf jbex be nal
bgure Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ jbex. Gur Sbhaqngvba znxrf ab
ercerfragngvbaf pbapreavat gur pbclevtug fgnghf bs nal jbex va nal
pbhagel bgure guna gur Havgrq Fgngrf.

1.R. Hayrff lbh unir erzbirq nyy ersreraprf gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret:

1.R.1. Gur sbyybjvat fragrapr, jvgu npgvir yvaxf gb, be bgure
vzzrqvngr npprff gb, gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ Yvprafr zhfg nccrne
cebzvaragyl jurarire nal pbcl bs n Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ jbex (nal jbex
ba juvpu gur cuenfr “Cebwrpg Thgraoret” nccrnef, be jvgu juvpu gur
cuenfr “Cebwrpg Thgraoret” vf nffbpvngrq) vf npprffrq, qvfcynlrq,
cresbezrq, ivrjrq, pbcvrq be qvfgevohgrq:

    Guvf rObbx vf sbe gur hfr bs nalbar naljurer va gur Havgrq Fgngrf naq zbfg
    bgure cnegf bs gur jbeyq ng ab pbfg naq jvgu nyzbfg ab erfgevpgvbaf
    jungfbrire. Lbh znl pbcl vg, tvir vg njnl be er-hfr vg haqre gur grezf
    bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvprafr vapyhqrq jvgu guvf rObbx be bayvar
    ng jjj.thgraoret.bet. Vs lbh
    ner abg ybpngrq va gur Havgrq Fgngrf, lbh jvyy unir gb purpx gur ynjf
    bs gur pbhagel jurer lbh ner ybpngrq orsber hfvat guvf rObbx.
  
1.R.2. Vs na vaqvivqhny Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbex vf
qrevirq sebz grkgf abg cebgrpgrq ol H.F. pbclevtug ynj (qbrf abg
pbagnva n abgvpr vaqvpngvat gung vg vf cbfgrq jvgu crezvffvba bs gur
pbclevtug ubyqre), gur jbex pna or pbcvrq naq qvfgevohgrq gb nalbar va
gur Havgrq Fgngrf jvgubhg cnlvat nal srrf be punetrf. Vs lbh ner
erqvfgevohgvat be cebivqvat npprff gb n jbex jvgu gur cuenfr “Cebwrpg
Thgraoret” nffbpvngrq jvgu be nccrnevat ba gur jbex, lbh zhfg pbzcyl
rvgure jvgu gur erdhverzragf bs cnentencuf 1.R.1 guebhtu 1.R.7 be
bognva crezvffvba sbe gur hfr bs gur jbex naq gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
genqrznex nf frg sbegu va cnentencuf 1.R.8 be 1.R.9.

1.R.3. Vs na vaqvivqhny Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbex vf cbfgrq
jvgu gur crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre, lbhe hfr naq qvfgevohgvba
zhfg pbzcyl jvgu obgu cnentencuf 1.R.1 guebhtu 1.R.7 naq nal
nqqvgvbany grezf vzcbfrq ol gur pbclevtug ubyqre. Nqqvgvbany grezf
jvyy or yvaxrq gb gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ Yvprafr sbe nyy jbexf
cbfgrq jvgu gur crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre sbhaq ng gur
ortvaavat bs guvf jbex.

1.R.4. Qb abg hayvax be qrgnpu be erzbir gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
Yvprafr grezf sebz guvf jbex, be nal svyrf pbagnvavat n cneg bs guvf
jbex be nal bgure jbex nffbpvngrq jvgu Cebwrpg Thgraoret™.

1.R.5. Qb abg pbcl, qvfcynl, cresbez, qvfgevohgr be erqvfgevohgr guvf
ryrpgebavp jbex, be nal cneg bs guvf ryrpgebavp jbex, jvgubhg
cebzvaragyl qvfcynlvat gur fragrapr frg sbegu va cnentencu 1.R.1 jvgu
npgvir yvaxf be vzzrqvngr npprff gb gur shyy grezf bs gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret™ Yvprafr.

1.R.6. Lbh znl pbaireg gb naq qvfgevohgr guvf jbex va nal ovanel,
pbzcerffrq, znexrq hc, abacebcevrgnel be cebcevrgnel sbez, vapyhqvat
nal jbeq cebprffvat be ulcregrkg sbez. Ubjrire, vs lbh cebivqr npprff
gb be qvfgevohgr pbcvrf bs n Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ jbex va n sbezng
bgure guna “Cynva Inavyyn NFPVV” be bgure sbezng hfrq va gur bssvpvny
irefvba cbfgrq ba gur bssvpvny Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ jrofvgr
(jjj.thgraoret.bet), lbh zhfg, ng ab nqqvgvbany pbfg, srr be rkcrafr

bs bognvavat n pbcl hcba erdhrfg, bs gur jbex va vgf bevtvany “Cynva
Inavyyn NFPVV” be bgure sbez. Nal nygreangr sbezng zhfg vapyhqr gur
shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret™ Yvprafr nf fcrpvsvrq va cnentencu 1.R.1.

        Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba. Eblnygl cnlzragf zhfg or cnvq

        Yvprafr. Lbh zhfg erdhver fhpu n hfre gb erghea be qrfgebl nyy

1.R.9. Vs lbh jvfu gb punetr n srr be qvfgevohgr n Cebwrpg

1.S.

1.S.1. Cebwrpg Thgraoret ibyhagrref naq rzcyblrrf rkcraq pbafvqrenoyr
rssbeg gb vqragvsl, qb pbclevtug erfrnepu ba, genafpevor naq cebbsernq

Thgraoret™ pbyyrpgvba. Qrfcvgr gurfr rssbegf, Cebwrpg Thgraoret™
ryrpgebavp jbexf, naq gur zrqvhz ba juvpu gurl znl or fgberq, znl
pbagnva “Qrsrpgf,” fhpu nf, ohg abg yvzvgrq gb, vapbzcyrgr, vanpphengr
be pbeehcg qngn, genafpevcgvba reebef, n pbclevtug be bgure
vagryyrpghny cebcregl vasevatrzrag, n qrsrpgvir be qnzntrq qvfx be
bgure zrqvhz, n pbzchgre ivehf, be pbzchgre pbqrf gung qnzntr be
pnaabg or ernq ol lbhe rdhvczrag.

1.S.2. YVZVGRQ JNEENAGL, QVFPYNVZRE BS QNZNTRF - Rkprcg sbe gur “Evtug
bs Ercynprzrag be Ershaq” qrfpevorq va cnentencu 1.S.3, gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba, gur bjare bs gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret™ genqrznex, naq nal bgure cnegl qvfgevohgvat n Cebwrpg
Thgraoret™ ryrpgebavp jbex haqre guvf nterrzrag, qvfpynvz nyy
yvnovyvgl gb lbh sbe qnzntrf, pbfgf naq rkcrafrf, vapyhqvat yrtny
srrf. LBH NTERR GUNG LBH UNIR AB ERZRQVRF SBE ARTYVTRAPR, FGEVPG
YVNOVYVGL, OERNPU BS JNEENAGL BE OERNPU BS PBAGENPG RKPRCG GUBFR
CEBIVQRQ VA CNENTENCU 1.S.3. LBH NTERR GUNG GUR SBHAQNGVBA, GUR
GENQRZNEX BJARE, NAQ NAL QVFGEVOHGBE HAQRE GUVF NTERRZRAG JVYY ABG OR

1.S.3. YVZVGRQ EVTUG BS ERCYNPRZRAG BE ERSHAQ - Vs lbh qvfpbire n

jvgu lbhe jevggra rkcynangvba. Gur crefba be ragvgl gung cebivqrq lbh
jvgu gur qrsrpgvir jbex znl ryrpg gb cebivqr n ercynprzrag pbcl va
